1b1: rgya gar skad du A r+ya ma hA badz+ra ma ru sha kha ra kU TA gA ra d+hA ra NA/ bod skad du//
1b2: 'phags pa rdo rje ri rab chen po'i rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzungs/ sangs rgyas dang / byang
1b3: chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ / 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus cig na/
1b4: bcom ldan 'das rdo rje'i lhun po chen po'i rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa rdo rje chen po'i ting nge 'dzin gyi sa'i
1b5: gnas/ rdo rje chen po'i dpag bsam gyi shing ljon pas legs pas brgyan pa/ rdo rje chen po'i rdzing gi
1b6: rin po che'i pad mo'i 'od kyis snang bar byas pa/ sa phyogs rdo rje chen po'i bye ma bdal ba/ rdo rje chen
1b7: bor byin gyis brlabs pa/ 'khor gyi khyams rdo rje chen po las byas pa/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyi
1b8: rdo rje chen po'i seng ge'i khri bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag stong gis rnam par mdzes pa/ chos bstan pa

2a1: dang cho 'phrul can/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis byin gyis brlabs pa/ chos thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyis nges par 'byung ba na/
2a2: byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag brgyad bcu rtsa bzhi thams cad kyang skye ba gcig gis thogs pa/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog pa/ mthu chen po thob pa/
2a3: rdo rje chen po'i rnam par thar pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis sangs rgyas kyi zhing du rnam par 'phrul pa dang cho 'phrul chen po kun tu ston pa/ sems kyi skad cig thang cig yud tsam gcig la sems can thams
2a4: cad kyi sems dang / spyod pa'i rjes su 'jug pa'i chos bstan pa sna tshogs mnyam pa nyid snyan cing rgya che la zab pa dang / spobs pa dang / cho 'phrul dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing du mar de bzhin gshegs
2a5: pa la mchod pa chen po'i sprin gyis mchod pa dang / rnam par thar pa'i sgo dang gzungs dang / ting 'dzin dang dbang dang / mngon par shes pa dang ma 'dres pa dang / byang chub kyi yan lag dang / lam dngas bcu
2a6: dang / pha rol du phyin pa dang / thabs la mkhas pa dang / bsdu ba'i dngos po dang / byams pa dang snying rje dang / dga' ba dang btang snyoms dang / byams pa'i stobs dang dben pa dang / yongs su byang ba'i sems
2a7: kyi rgyun dang ldan pa sha stag la 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje snying po zhes bya ba dang / rdo rje mig dang rdo rje'i lus dang / rdo rje'i blo gros dang lag na rdo rje dang / rdo rje 'dus pa dang
2a8: rdo rje mthu bo che dang / rdo rje rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rdo rje brtsegs pa dang rdo rje'i phung po dang / rdo rje'i nga ro dang rdo rje bzang po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i tog ces bya ba dang /

2b1: ngag la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag brgyad bcu rtsa bzhi dang / nyan thos chen po rab tu mang po thams cad kyang dgra bcom pa/ zag pa zad pa/ srid par kun du spyod
2b2: bachad pa/ yang dag pa'i shes pas sems shin du rnam par grol ba/ rdzu 'phrul gyi stobs dang / cho 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pas rnam par 'phrul ba'i mthu chen po thob pa/ lta ba chags pa med pa/ thams
2b3: cad kyang dri ma dang bral ba/ kun nas nyon mongs pa'i bag chags kyi sa bon nges par sregs pa sha stag la 'di lta ste/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu dang / tshe dang ldan pa byams ma'i bu gang po dang / tshe dang ldan pa
2b4: ka bi na dang / tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor dang / tshe dang ldan pa maud gal gyi bu chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa skul byed dang / tshe dang ldan pa dga' byed dang / tshe dang ldan pa ga ya 'od srung dang / tshe dang ldan pa 'od srung
2b5: chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa lteng rgyas 'od srung dang / de dag la sogs pa nyan thos chen po rab tu mang po dang / lha'i bu dbang phyug chen po la sogs pa gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu grangs med dpag tu
2b6: med gzhal du med pa dag dang / mi 'jed kyi bdag po tshangs pa dang / lha'i bu tshangs pa bzang po la sogs pa tshadangs ris kyi lha'i bu rnams dang / lha'i bu rab 'thab bral g.yog 'thab bral gyi lha'i ris kyi
2b7: lha'i bu dang bcas pa dang / yongs su dga' ldan dang / 'phrul dga' dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed dang / lha'i dbang po brgya byin lha'i bu thams cad kyi 'khor can dang / lha ma yin gyi dbang po thag bzangs
2b8: ris dang / stobs can dang rab sim dang / sgra gcan dang rnam par snang byed dang / de la sogs pa lha ma yin gyi dbang po tshad med/ grangs med dpag tu med pa rnams dang / klu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho dang / ma dros pa

3a1: dang 'jog po dang / nor rgyas kyi bu dang / dung skyong dang / stobs kyi rgyu dang / pad ma dang pad ma chen po dang / mtha' yas dang / de dag la sogs pa klu'i rgyal po tshad med/ grangs med dpag du med pa
3a2: bdag dang / mi'am ci'i rgyal po ljon pa mi 'am ci'i rgyal po'i g.yog du ma can dang / dri za'i rgyal po gtsug phud lnga pa dri za'i rgyal po'i g.yog du ma can dang / rig sngags 'chang gi rgyal po don thams cad
3a3: grub pa rig sngags 'chang gi rgyal po'i g.yog du ma can dang / nam mkha' lding gi rgyal po gser mig nam mkha' lding gi rgyal po'i g.yog du ma can dang / gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po chen po rnam thos kyi bu dang /
3a4: nor bu bzang dang / gang ba bzang dang / gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po lnga rtsen gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po g.yog du ma can dang / 'phrog ma bu lnga rgya'i g.yog can dang / 'jig rten gyi ma bdun dang / sring mo bdun dang /
3a5: drang srong chen po bdun dang / bar snang la rgyu ba'i rgyu skar dang / gza'i lha thams cad dang / phyogs kyi lha rnams dang / phyogs mtshams kyi lha rnams dang / sa'i lha dang dbyangs can dang / 'byung po rnams
3a6: dang / bgegs rnams dang log 'dren rnams dang / yi dgas rnams dang / 'byung po rdzu 'phrul chen po rnams dang / ri'i rgyal po thams cad dang / 'jig rten skyong ba chu lha g.yog rgya mtsho'i lha thams cad/
3a7: dang bcas pa dang / 'phags skyes po dang / mig mi bzang dang / lag na be con dang / bden bral dang / me'i lha dang / rlung gi lha chen po bdun dang / dbang bdag chung ma dang bcas pa'i tshogs bye ba khrag
3a8: khrig 'bum phrag du ma'i 'khor can dang / sred med kyi bu g.yog dang bcas pa dang / byin pa po dang / phreng ba can dang / lcags can dang / tshogs kyi bdag po chen po dang / sprin ta la la dang log 'dren gyi

3b1: gyi dbang po bgegs log 'dren gyi g.yog du ma can dang / shing gseb gyi lha drug bcu dang / sring mo bzhi ming po dang bcas pa dang / ma bdun dang rdo rje lcags kyu can dang / rdo rje lu gu rgyud dang / rdo rje pho nya mo
3b2: drug bcu rtsa bzhi dang / rdo rje'i sde dang / lag bzangs dang gtsug gis 'gro ba rdo rje'i rigs kyi 'khor du ma dang bcas pa dang / de ma yin pa bzhin yang sangs rgyas dang / chos dang / dge 'dun la mngon par
3b3: dad pa'i lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang lto 'phye chen po dang // 'byung po dang yi dgas dang / sha za dang smyo byed dang / brjed byed dang sgrub pa
3b4: dang / sbrul 'dzin bcas dang / gnon po tshad med dpag tu med grangs med pa rnams dang / lha'i bu nyi ma dang / lha'i bu zla ba dang / dus tshigs kyi lha dang / nub ka'i lha dang / dus kyi lha thams cad dang
3b5: gnam sa'i lha rnams dang yang thabs gcig go/ de ltar yang bcom ldan 'das de chos kyi 'khor lo ni shin du bskor sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa ni shin du yongs su mthar phyin/ bsod nams dang ye shes
3b6: kyi tshogs ni shin tu yongs su rdzogs thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang / byang chub chen po dang / pha rol tu phyin pa dang / sa bsnyes pas ni shin du yongs su gzung skyes bu chen po'i mtshan 'bar ba
3b7: sum bcu rtsa gnyis kyis ni sku brgyan/ dpe byed bzang po brgyad bcus ni yan lag dang / nying lag thams cad rnam par spras/ spyi gtsug ni sems can thams cad kyis bltar mi mthong / bdud
3b8: kyi cher ma thams cad ni dkrugs/ de kho na nyid mkhyen pa nyid ni rim par thugs su chud/ spyan rnam lnga ni mnga'/ rnam pa thams cad kyi mchog dang ni ldan thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang ni

4a1: sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang ni ldan/ bdud dngabs kyis rgol ba dang / ngan pa'i tshogs can gyi tshogs thams cad ni bcom/ brjod pa'i sgra dang tshigs su bcad pa ni 'phagras
4a2: khyu mchog dang seng ge'i sgra ni spogs/ ma rig pa'i mun pa ni kun tu gsal/ bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med dpag tu med par sbyin pa dang / tshul khrims dang / bzod pa dang / brtson
4a3: 'grus dang / bsam gtan dang / shes rab dang / thabs dang stobs dang / smon lam dang ye shes kyi pha rol du phyin pa dang / bka' ba spyad pas mngon par grub pa'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang /
4a4: byad bzang po brgyad bcus sku brgyan pas ni mdzes shing rin po che chen po'i pad ma'i snying po'i seng ge'i khri la ni bzhugs te/ gdan rin po che dang / rdo rje'i pad ma'i seng ge'i khri ri rab tsam rdo rje dang / rin po che dang / mu
4a5: tig dang ldan pa'i dril bu g.yer ka'i dra ba du ma sil sil sgra 'byung ba/ rdo rje dang / rin po che du ma'i sngags bu la rtsa ba legs par brten pa/ rdo rje dang / rin po che du ma'i chu srin gyi kha nas byung ba'i mu tig dmar po'i
4a6: phreng ba dang ldan pa'i snam rten dang bcas pa/ rin po che du ma'i pad ma'i snying po la chags pa'i rin po che ke ke ru dang / ke ke ru chen po dang / an da rnyil dang / mthon ka chen po dang / dun las du ma'i 'od zer 'bar bas
4a7: snang bar gyur pas kun tu mdzes pa/ rin po che dang / rdo rje'i thur mas brgyan pa'i gdugs yu bas bstod pa bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du mas grib mar bsgribs shing bskyabs pa/ dpag bsam gyi shing du mas mdzes
4a8: bar byas pa rgya che ba la bzhugs te/ gser gyi ri bo ltar dpal gyis 'bar ba/ nyi ma stong pas lhag pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor 'byor bsas phyogs mdzes par gyur pa/ zla ba nya ba ltar 'jig rten kun gyis mthong na dga'

4b1: dpag bsam gyi shing ljon pa chen po ltar sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams kyis yang dag par byas par chos ston te/ ma par spyod pa/ thog mar dge ba bar du dge ba/ tha mar dge ba don bzang po/ tshig 'bru bzang po ma 'dres pa
4b2: yongs su rdzogs pa/ yongs su dag pa yongs su dkar ba yang dag par ston to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi spyi gtsug gi mtshams kyi mdzod spu nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kun tu ston pa zhes bya ba'i 'od
4b3: zer gyi dra ba chen po byung ste/ 'od zer gyi dra ba des stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di snang bas gsal bar byas par gyur to// gang gA'i klung gi bye ma ji snyed pa dang mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing de
4b4: dag thams cad kyang snang ba des gsal bar snang bar gyur to/ / sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang dag bzhugs pa de dag kyang seng ge'i khri du ma bkod pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzhal med
4b5: khang rnams na chos ston to/ / nyan thos chen po de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dag dang thabs gcig go/ dge slong dang / dge slong ma dang / dge snyen dang / dge bsnyen ma dang / lha dang / klu dang /
4b6: gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po rnams dang yang thabs gcig go/ de dag thams cad kyang rdo rje lhun po chen po'i rtse mo khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzungs yang
4b7: dag par rab tu ston to/ / de dag thams cad kyang kun du snang ngo // skad cig de la sems can de dag thams cad bde ba thams cad kyis tshim par gyur to// 'on pa rnams ni sgra thos so// long ba rnams ni mig thob bo// /
4b8: smyon pa rnams ni dran pa rnyed do// nad pa rnams ni sos par gyur to// sbrum ma rnams ni bde bar btsas so// sems can dmyal ba thams cad kyi sdug bsngal rnams ni med par gyur to// yud tsam de la dud 'gro'i skye

5a1: gnas dang / yi dgas kyi skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten rnams kyi ming yang mi drag par gyur to// 'jig rten gyi bar gang dag mun pa mun nag dang / mun pa mun nag chen por 'dug pa de dag thams
5a2: cad kyang gsal bar snang bar gyur to/ / der sems can gang dag skyes pa de dag thams cad dang / sems can gzhan 'dir skyes pa rnams kyang gcig gis gcig shes so// de nas sems can de dag thams cad kyi
5a3: ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos kyi dga' ba thob ste/ bde ba mchog gis tshim par gyur nas kun tu bltas pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mthong te/ de dag gis gser
5a4: gyi mchod sdong ltar dpal gyis 'bar zhing rang gi gzi brjid kyis mngon par 'phags pa de mthong nas de nyid la skyabs su dong ngo / / skyabs su dod ma thag du de dag thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil
5a5: 'khor de nyid du bdag son pa snyam du shes so/ / snang ba des bdud kyi khyim thams cad kun tu 'bar rab tu 'bar kun du rab tu mched cing 'bar te/ me lce gcig tu gyur par kun du snang ngo // bdud kyi ris kyi lha
5a6: de dag kyang skad cig de la nyam thag pa'i sgrar ngu zhing skrag nas byer ro/ / bdud sdig can yang bzhin bzang po d+hi rI por gyur cing lus rdul nas bdud kyi ris kyi lha'i bu thams cad la smras pa/ grogs po dag bdud kyi khyim
5a7: thams cad kun du 'bar/ rab tu 'bar kun du rab tu mched cing 'bar te me lce cig tu gyur pa dang / dge sbyong gau ta ma ri rab kyi rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa na chos ston pa 'di la ltos/ des bdag cag phung po thobartsams
5a8: so/ / phyogs gang du gnas gtol med do// longs la dge sbyong gau ta ma de'i gan du song te bdud kyi yul 'di thal bar ma gyur gyi bar du gzhom mo// de skad ces smras pa dang / bdud kyi ris kyi lha'i bu de dag thams cad

5b1: kyis rje bka' bzhin 'tshal zhes smras nas/ rang rang gi gnas su dong ste/ lag na mtshon cha sna tshogs can/ gos sna tshogs bgos pa/ cha byed dang rgyan sna tshogs can/ mche ba mi bzad par 'jigs su rung ba bzhin
5b2: mi thug par bsgyur ba/ mig dang bzhin dang / s+tha kun du 'bang shing rab tu 'bar ba dag skad cig de nyid la gcig tu 'dus nas bdud sdig can gal bder dong ste phyin nas bdud sdig can la 'di skad ces smras so//
5b3: bzhengs bzhengs thog mar bzhud la ji tsam du dge sbyong gau ta ma nyan thos dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun dang bcas pa/ de ci nas kyang phyis bdag cag gi yul du gnod pa cung zad kyang mi bskyed pa dang / bdag
5b4: cag gi yul gnod par mi 'gyur ba de nyid du phye mar brlag go/ / rnam par gzhom mo// de nas bdud sdig can dga' zhing mgu ste/ shin du dga' bas spu'i khung bu khyab nas skad cig de nyid la bdud kyi ris kyi lha'i bu
5b5: thams cad dang lhan cig tu bdud kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen po dang bdud kyi sde chen pos par sdang dpag tshad stong phrag brgyad bcu rtsa bzhir khyab par byas te/ dung dang rnga dang rdza rnga dang / kha ra rnga dang rgyud gcig pa dang /
5b6: lcags kyi sil dkrol dang / rnga bo che brdung zhing hu du zhes bya ba dang / bi tsi zhes bya ba dang / zung shig zung shig/ sod cig sod cig ces bya ba'i sgra 'byin cing gzhol ba dang / gtun shing dang gtun rked nyag dang / phur
5b7: bu dang / rdo rje rtse gcig pa dang / mda' bo che dang / mdung thud dang / rtse gsum pa dang / ral gri dang 'khor lo dang / gzhu dang mnga' la sogs pa'i mtshon cha lag na thogs shing bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste skad
5b8: cig de nyid la a la la zhes bya ba'i sgra phyung nas bcom ldan 'das la mtshon cha thams cad kyi char phab pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi mthus mtshon cha de dag thams cad me tog gi gdugs kyi sprin chen por gyur par

6a1: snang ngo / / bdud kyi sgra de dag thams cad kyang sangs rgyas kyi sgra dang / chos kyi sgra dang dge 'dun gyi sgra dang / yang dag par 'gro ba'i sgra rnams su grag go/ bdud sdig can ni zhags pa lnga'i bcings bas
6a2: bdag nyid bcings par mthong ngo / / de nas bdud kyi ris kyi lha'i bu de dag thams cad kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul ngo mtshar du gyur cing dga' ba thob ste/ bcom ldanas de nyid la skyabs su dong ngo // bdud/
6a3: sdig can ni bdag nyid dgral bar 'dod na 'grol ma nus te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi khyams su bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar shing rtsa ba nas bcad pa bzhin du rdo rje'i khams kyi khyams chen por 'gyel te/
6a4: de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe byams pa chen po'i thugs dang / thugs rje chen pos brlan pa'i spyan gyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi khyams thams cad du gzigs nas/ gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag
6a5: na rdo rje la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / gsang ba ba'i bdag po lag na rdo rje bdud sdig can 'khor gyi khyams 'di nas slong la stan la zhog ste/ rdo rje rnam par thar pa'i sgo chen po'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i
6a6: byin gyi rlabs bsam gyis mi khyab pa bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad 'joms par byed pa zhes bya ba gang gis/ bdud kyi ris kyi lha'i bu 'di dag dang / bdud sdig can 'di sangs rgyas la skyabs su 'dod pa dang /
6a7: gzhan yang gang dag sdang ba bgegs dang / log 'dren dang yi dgas dang / brjed byed dang 'byung po dang / gdon dang mkha' 'gro ma dang sgrub pa dang sbrul 'dzin bcas dang / gnon po dang zas su btsas pa za
6a8: ga la sogs pa sdang ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ rab tu sdang ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i snyan pa la ma gus pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos nyid khong du ma chud pa/ de dag thams cad

6b1: gang gis 'dzud pa dang / dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su 'gro bar byed pa yang ston cig/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ des ngan 'gro log par ltung bar 'gro ba'i phyir ro// de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / gsang ba ba'i
6b2: bdag po lag na rdo rjes/ bcom ldan 'das kyi bka' mnyan nas rin po che'i pad ma'i rdo rje'i stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga rin po che'i pad ma'i snying
6b3: la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su bral mo sbyar ba bdud nas/ bcom ldan 'das la tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshigs su gcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// sems can kun gyi nyon mongs
6b4: pa/ / gzhig pa'i slad du 'dren pa zung // khyod ni bdud rnams kun las rgyal// 'jig rten rtsa lag gcig pu khyod// thar pa'i grong khyer 'jug pa'i lam// ye shes ma lus khyod gcig pus// yang dag
6b5: brnyas nas thugs rdza yis/ / brlan pa'i thugs kyis bstan pa mdzad// khyod sngon sbyin dang tshul khrims dang // bzod dang brtson 'grus bsam gtan dang // shes rab la sogs yon tan gyis// bdag
6b6: mdzad slad kyis sems can bcud/ / khyod kyis chos rnams skye med par// bshad cing de bzhin rnam rtse yang // 'bras bur dogs pa ma mchis pa// kye ma mgon po khyod kyis bshad// 'khor lo yan lag
6b7: bcu gnyis pa/ / khyod nyid mkhyen nas rab tu bskor// mu stegs can dang bdud btul te// chos kyi snang ba gsal bar mdzad// nyon mongs brag chen rnam kun tu// ye shes rdo rjes rab bcom nas// sus
6b8: kyang thob par ma gyur pa'i/ / byang chub bla na med pa brnyes// gang gi mtshan yang rdzogs pa yi// byang chub sa bon nyid 'gyur ba// khyod ni 'jig rten mchog gcig za// dam pa rab sbyin bdag po lags//

7a1: khyod ni mgon po khyod ni pa// khyod skyabs khyod ni dpung gnyen lags// thugs rje chen po ye shes nyid// mya ngan 'das gnas gcig pu khyod// khyod nyid gshegs nas sems can rnams// sem
7a2: can dmyal las rnam par grol/ / rang gi sku yang yongs btang nas// khyod kyis srog chags rnams kyang bsrungs// lus can kun gyis ma thob pa'i// ye shes khyod kyis brnyes gyur nas// grol te 'jig
7a3: rten rnams kyang 'grol/ / kye ma khyod ni rtsa lag bzang // mgon po khyod kyi 'od zer gyi// dra bas 'jig rten khams rnams khyab// mya ngan 'das las lhag pa bde// lus can kun gyis thob par mdzad// khyod
7a4: kyi 'od kyi gzis bcom pas/ / gza' rnams kun dang dgung zla dang // gdugs rnams dang ni zhugs rnams dang // nor bu lha mer ma gyur to// de nas gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rjes tshul dang 'dra ba'i
7a5: tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis/ bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod nas// yang rin po che pad ma'i snying po la 'dug ste/ bcom ldan 'das legs so zhes gsol nas// rdo rje'i rnam par thar pa
7a6: sgo chen po'i ting nge 'dzin bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad 'joms par byed pa zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs so/ / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rjes rdo rje'i rnam par thar pa'i sgo chen po'i ting nge 'dzin
7a7: bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad 'joms par byed pa zhes bya ba 'di la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ de nas de'i tshe stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di rnam pa drug du g.yos/ kun du
7a8: rab tu g.yos te/ shar phyogs mtho na nub phyogs dma'// nub phyogs mtho na shar phyogs dma'/ lho phyogs mthon byang phyogs dma'// byang phyogs mthon lho phyogs dma'/ mtha' mtho na dbus dam

7b1: dbus mthon ni mtha' dma' bar gyur to/ / phyogs thams cad dang phyogs mtshams thams cad kyang dgas dang / yid bde ba skyes par gyur nas/ lA ma me/ ldan no// lhang nge'o// gas ba pa'i bdag po
7b2: lag na rdo rje'i yan lag dang nying lag gi mtshams thams cad nas rdo rje kun du 'bar ba/ rab tu 'bar ba kun du rab tu mched cing 'bar ba/ me lce gcig du gyur pa dag byung bar kun du snang ngo //
7b3: rdo rje 'bar ba'i snang ba des phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med grangs med dpag tu med pa ji snyed pa dag na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang dag da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes la chos kyang ston te/
7b4: tshangs par spyod pa thog mar dge ba/ bar du dge ba tha mar dge ba/ don bzang po tshig 'bru bzang po/ ma 'dres pa yongs su rdzogs pa/ yongs su dag pa yongs su byang ba/ yang dag par ston pa/ nyan thos kyi dge
7b5: 'dun dang bcas pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i dge bdun dang bcas pa de dag 'khor gyi khyams rgya che zhing rgya che ba dag kun tu snang ngo // byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi spyan
7b6: sngar/ rdo rje 'bar ba'i snang ba rgya chen po des snang bar gyur nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag la so sor zhus pa/ bcom ldan 'das snang ba rgya chen po kun du gda' ba 'di su'i lags/ de nas sangs rgyas bcom
7b7: ldan 'das de dag gis so so'i byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / rigs kyi bu dag de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa zhes bya ba mi 'dzed kyi
7b8: 'jig rten gyi khams na ri rab kyi steng na chos ston to/ / bcom ldan 'das des bdud sdig can zhags pa'i bcing ba lngas bcings te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar 'gyel ba gzigs nas byang chub sems dpa' sems

8a1: dpa' chen po gas ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje zhes bya ba la 'di skad du/ gas ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje khyod kyis rang gi rdzu 'phrul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa'i cho 'phrul ston cig ces bka' stsal to//
8a2: rigs kyi bu dag 'di ni rdo rjes rnam par thar pa'i sgo chen po'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ de'i rdo rje'i rnam par 'phrul pa chen po'i byin gyi rlabs so// de skad ces bka' stsal te/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra
8a3: bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag gis gnang nas/ rigs kyi bu de dag thams cad kyis de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag la phyag 'tshal te/ byang chub
8a4: sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i rnam par 'phrul pa'i cho 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams mi 'byed 'dir lhags nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par
8a5: rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa dang gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la mchod pa'i sprin dang / gdugs kyi sbyin dang / rgyan phreng gyi sprin dang / dpung rgyan gyi sprin dang / me tog gi sprin dang / na bza'i sprin chen pos
8a6: mchod pa chen po byas nas/ nam mkha'i dkyil na 'khor bzhin du bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la lan bdun bskor ba byas te/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lhar rin po che'i pad ma'i rdo rje'i bstan la btsugs nas/ bcom
8a7: ldan 'das la logs su lta zhing / bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa sa gnang nas/ rang rang gi rin po che'i pad ma'i rdo rje'i bstan de dag la 'khod par gyur to// de'i tshe shar phyogs logs
8a8: na 'jig rten gyi khams rdo rje'i rtog ces bya ba de na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje'i snying pos rab tu 'joms pa zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhos te/ 'di ltar

8b1: rdo rje'i ri rab chen po'i rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzungs 'di nyid la brtsams te chos kyang ston to/ / rdo rje 'bar ba'i snang ba des kyang 'jig rten gyi khams ji snyed pa de dag thams cad kun nas snang bar gyur to//
8b2: nas 'jig rten gyi khams de na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa de'i 'khor gyi khyams su 'dus te 'dug par gyur pa des ngo mtshar de mthong nas/ de bzhin gshe
8b3: pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje'i snying pos rab tu 'joms pa zhes bya ba de la zhus pa/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'bar ba'i snang ba 'di lta bu gang gis 'jig rten gyi khams 'di thams cad skar
8b4: bar gyur te/ sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun chad cing sems can dmyal ba dang / dud 'gro'i skye gnas dang yi dgas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sdug bsngal thams cad mi gda' bar gyur/ lha
8b5: dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang dri za dang / lha ma yin dang nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po la sogs pa 'jig rten na rdzu 'phrul che zhing dbang che bar grags pa thams cad kyang kun nas mchod pa'i/ sprin
8b6: chen pos dga' ba dang yid bde ba skyes te/ nub phyogs su mchi bar gda' ba 'di su'i legs/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje'i snying pos rab tu 'joms pas/
8b7: byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu nub phyogs kyi logs na mi 'dzod kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag
8b8: par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa zhes bya ba rdo rje chen po'i ri rab kyi rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa na rdo rje chen po'i ri rab kyi rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzungs/ shes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs ston to//

9a1: bcom ldan 'das ngas lha gtsug gi samams kyi mdzadang sun pa 'dabar bye pa can pazung// 'ang ba kyang bcan 'das 'jig rten gyi khams dang drad sdig pan yul ma thag dra kun du khras da/
9a2: lnga'i bu thams cad dang / gzhan yang bdud kyi ris kyi lha'i bu rnams dang / dpung gi tshigs chen po dang lhan cig tu bcom ldan 'das la gtse ba'i phyir lhags pa dang / de la sangs rgyas kyi mthus de bzhin gshegs
9a3: pa'i rdo rje'i 'khor gyi khyams de nyid du zhags pa lnga'i bcing bas bcings pas bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar 'gyel te/ de la thugs che ba'i phyir bcom ldan 'das des byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gas
9a4: ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la ston cig par bka' lung byin nas/ gsarab pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje des rdo rje'i rnam par thar pa'i sgo chen po zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ yan lag dang nyid lag
9a5: gi mtshams thams cad nas rdo rje rnams bstan to/ / 'di ni rdo rje de dag nyid kyi rdo rje 'bar ba'i snang ba'o// rigs kyi bu rdo rje 'bar ba'i blang ba des kyang phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams cad med grangs med dpag tu
9a6: med pa rnams su 'jig rten gyi khams gang ga'i klung gi bye ma dang mnyam pa ji snyed pa snang bar byas te/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang dag bzhugs pa de dag thams cad kyang bskum/
9a7: byang chub sems dpa' de dag gi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de dag kyang bskul bas ngo mtshar thob par gyur pa dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dga' yang so sor
9a8: nus so/ / rigs kyi bu de nyid kyi mthus/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa de'i spyan sngar 'dugacing bsnyen bkur byed/

9b1: pa yang mtha nga // de skad ces bka' bral pa dang / de bzhin gshegs par gra btsam pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo lngam stong pas rab tu 'joms pad ma byang chub sems dpa' sam sa dpa
9b2: chen po rdo rje'i snying pos 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das bdag 'jig rten gyi khams mi 'jed der de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa de la
9b3: blta ba dang / phyag bgyi ba dang bsnyen bkur bgyi ba dang / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje de yang blta bar bgyi ba'i skad du mchi'o// de skad ces gsol pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
9b4: dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje'i snying pos rab tu 'joms pas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / rigs kyi bu de'i bus la bab par shes
9b5: na song shig/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po bcom ldan 'das des gnang nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
9b6: rgyas rdo rje'i snying pos rab tu 'joms pa de la lan bdun bskor ba byas te 'jig rten gyi khams de nas mi snang bar gyur nas/ nam mkha'i dkyil gyi lam nas byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag
9b7: dgu bcu rtsa dgu dang lhan cig tu byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rdzu 'phrul chen pos 'jig rten gyi khams mi 'jed 'di ga la ba der song ste phyin nas byang chub
9b8: sems dpa' de dag thams cad dang lhan cig smra ba na/ bsod nams kyi tshogs bsags pa las grub pas byin pa'i rin po che de dag las 'od zer 'di lta ste/ sngon po dang ser po dang / dmar po dang ldang sngon

10a1: dang / ljang zer dang btsod ka dang shel dang dngul dang / nor bu dang mu tig dang / gser dang pad ma rA ga dang / rdo'i snying po dang / ke ke ru dang / ke ke ru chen po dang / and rnyil dang / mthon ka chen po dang / dun las dang /
10a2: go mu ta ra ka dang mu tig dmar po'i kha dog lta bu rnams byung ste/ de dag gis thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams la lan 'bum phrag du mar bskor ba byas te steng gi bar snang khyab par byas nas lha'i snang bas snang bar byas te 'dus
10a3: nas 'ji'i lta bur gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa'i zhabs mtshan thams cad phun sum tshogs pa/ 'jam pa mnyen pa/ rab tu gzhon pa sha rgyas
10a4: snum pa/ long bu gnyis kyi rtsa mi mngon pa/ pad ma gsar dra kha bye ba lta bu dang / dung dang nya dang / rdo rje dang / rgyal mtshan dang / lcags kyu dang / pad ma dang / chu srin ma ka ra'i mtshan dang ldan pa gnyis la lan 'bum phrag du ma
10a5: bskor ba byas nas nub par gyur to/ / nam mkha'i dkyil na 'od zer re re'i rtse mo las pad ma bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag brgyad bcu tshad shing rta'i phang lo tsam pa rin po che sna bdun gyi rgyu las byung ba 'di lta ste/ gser gyi rgyu las
10a6: byung ba dag/ and d+hil dang / dngul dang / byi ru dang shel dang / ke ke ru dang / dung dang / dun las kyi rgyu las byung ba dag 'thon to// de la gsar gyi rgyu las byung ba'i pad ma rnams kyi 'dab ma ni and rnyil gyi rgyu las byung bdag
10a7: go/ snying po ni dngul gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// ze ba ni byi ru'i rgyu las byung ba'o// chu ba ni shel gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// ze 'bru ni ke ke ru'i rgyu las byung ba'o// a nad rnyil gyi rgyu las byung ba'i bad ma rnams kyi mdab ma nang ngul gyi
10a8: rgyu las byung ba dag go/ snying po ni byi ru'i rgyu las byung ba'o// ze ba ni shel gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// chub ni ke ke ru'i rgyu las byung ba'o// ze 'bru ni dun las kyi rgyu las byung ba'o// dngul gyi rgyu las byung ba'i pad ma rnams kyi mda' ma ni

10b1: b+hi dri'i rgyu las byung ba dag go/ / snying po ni shel gyi rgyu las blang ba'o// ze ba ni ke ke ru'i rgyu las byung ba'o// chu ba ni dran las kyi rgyu las byung ba'o// ze 'bru ni gser gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// byi dri'i rgyu las byung ba'i pad ma rnams
10b2: gyi mdab ma ni shal gyi rgyu las byung ba dag go/ / snying po ni ke ke ru'i rgyu las byung ba'o// ze ba ni dran las kyi rgyu las byung ba'o// chu ba ni gser gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// ze 'bru ni and rnyil gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// shel gyi rgyu
10b3: las byung ba'i pad ma rnams kyi mdab ma ni ke ke ru'i rgyu las byung ba dag go/ snying po ni dun las kyi rgyu las byung ba'o// za ba ni gser gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// chu ba ni a nang rnyil gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// ze 'bru ni dngul gyi rgyu/
10b4: las byung ba'o// ke ke ru'i rgyu las byung ba'i pad ma rnams kyi mdab ma ni dun las kyi rgyu las byung ba dag go/ snying po ni gser gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// ze ba ni a nad rnyil gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// chu ba ni dngul gyi rgyu las
10b5: byung ba'o/ / ze 'bru ni byi ru'i rgyu las byung ba'o// dun las kyi rgyu las byung ba'i pad ma rnams kyi mdab ma ni gser gyi rgyu las byung ba dag go/ snying po ni and rnyil gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// ze ba ni dngul gyi rgyu las
10b6: byung ba'o/ / chu ba ni byi ru'i rgyu las byung ba'o// ze 'bru ni shel gyi rgyu las byung ba'o// de bzhin du sbyar ste/ de ltar rin po che du ma'i rgyu las byung ba'i pad ma dag go/ rin po che'i pad ma re re la yang sa bcu la rab tu gnas/
10b7: pa'i ba'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun du mdzes pa'i spyod lam phun sum tshogs pa dag ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// byang chub sems dpa' re re'i lte ba nas kyang 'od zer 'bum 'bum
10b8: 'byung ngo / / 'od zer gyi rtse mo re re las kyang rin po che thams cad kyi rgyu las byung ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa nor bu dang / rin po chernas pa sna tshogs kyi stegs pas bskor ba/ shel gyi rgyu las byung ba'i zla bas spras

11a1: ba'i khang bran gyi rtse mo la seng ge'i rna ba'i steng na rin po che'i rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang rnam par rgyal ba'i ba dan sbyangs pas nam mkha' kun tu khebs pas pad ma rAg dang and rnyil dang / ma
11a2: gad dang / bai dUr+ya dang rje'i snying po dang / spug dang / ki ke ru las byas pa'i ka ba chen po'i slad la 'dzam bu'i chu bo'i gser gyi shing sa la gcod pa lta bu'i tshogs bkod pas rnam par sbas te/ mdzes par byas
11a3: pa dngul las byas pa'i phug ron gyi phreng gi mtha' mthar mu tig dmar po dang ldan pa dril bu g.yar ka'i dra ba sbyangs pa'i sgras sad par gyur nas rab tu dga' zhing dregs pa'i phu ga ron dang / bya bang dang / ne tso dang ri
11a4: skegs dang / rma bya'i nga ro dag gis nyams dga' ba/ khyams dang 'dun khang chen po'i nyen 'khor stegs bur bskor bas mdzes par byas pa/ rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs pa las byas pa'i sgo khang can/ shel gyi
11a5: rgyu las byas pa'i stegs bu dang ldan pa/ bkra shis kyi gser gyi bum pa du ma nas spos chu dri zhim pos chag chag btab pa/ rdzing chen po'i 'gram gyi ne'u gsing mar gad kyi rgyu las byung ba/ ka tsa li na da'i gos ltar
11a6: reg na bde bas mdzes pa'i phyogs na bde bar nyal ba'i ngang pa dang / khrung khrung dang / ngur ba dang / ka lan da ka'i khyu gnas pa/ gser gyi bye ma brdal ba'i gtos chen po rin po che sna bdun gyi them skas kyi phreng bas
11a7: brgyan pa/ yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i chus yongs su gang ba/ grangs 'bum phrag du mas kun nas yongs su bskor ba dag byung ngo // rdzing bu re re nas kyang rin po che'i pad ma bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag dgu bcu
11a8: rtsa dgu rtsa dgu byung ngo / / rin po che'i pad ma re re'i snying po la yang sil snyan dang / pheg rdob pa dang / glu dbyangs rnams kyi sgra phyung bas/ lha'i bu mo dag glu len gar byed cing yongs su spyod do// sil snyan dang theg/

11b1: rdob pa dang / klu dbyangs kyi sgra byung ba de dag las kyang tshigs su bcad pa 'di lta bu 'di dag byung ngo // sbyin dang tshul khrims kyis ni gang zhig dpag med cing // de bzhin bzod dang brtson 'grus dag gi stobs ldan pa/ bsam/
11b2: tan gyis ni nI zhing dbang gis kun 'byor pa/ ye shes sgron mede la sgrubasu 'dod bar gyis// bsam gyis mi khyab stobs dang smon lam rnams dang ldan/ thabs dang byang chub yan lagating 'dzin rnams kyis dag/
11b3: rnam par grol ba'i lam dang stobs bcur ldan pa yi/ thub pa gang yin de la mchod phyir 'dod par gyis// 'dam rdzab nas ni pad ma rgyas pa ji bzhin du/ gang zhig nyon mongs 'dam gyis rtag par mi gos pa/
11b4: dang skye ba'i sdug bsngal rnam par gsal ba yi/ rgyal ba 'jig rten mgon po de la lta phyir dang // gcig kyang mi ldan min par gyur pa gang zhig gis// skye dgu rnams kyi gti mug sgo glegs rnams bshig/
11b5: cing / sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi sbyor bar bzhig// shAkya tog ldan de la skyabs su 'dor bar gyis// de ltar khang pa brtsegs pa dpag bsam gyi shing ljon pas legs par brgyan pa rnam pas tshogs bye ba khrag
11b6: khrig 'bum phrag du ma nam mkha'i dkyil na kun du snang ste/ kha cig tu ni rin po che'i sprin gyi char 'bab par kun tu snang ngo // kha cig tu ni me tog gi gdugs kyi sprin gyi char/ kha cig tu ni go shir sha'i tsan dan
11b7: dang / spos dang byug pa dang / phye ma'i sprin gyi char/ kha cig tu ni gos kyi phreng ba'i sprin gyi char/ kha cig tu ni ka shaM ka ris dang du gula'i ras dang / za zug gi sprin gyi char kha cig tu ni dpag bsam gyi shing ljon gyi
11b8: sprin gyi char/ kha cig tu ni me tog pad ma dang / ut+pa la dang / ku mu da dang / pad ma dkar po dang / dri mchog dang / a ti mug ta ka dang / ka tsa lin da dang / ma hA ga tsa lin da dang btang gzung dang / btang bzung chen

12a1: bo dang / many+dzuka ka dang / many+dzu sha ka chan po dang / man dA ra ba dang / man dA rab can pa sprin bya char mngon par bab bo// ma togag char de dag las degang byung ba das sangs rgyas kyi na
12a2: med grangs med pa dag gang ga'i klung gi bye ma'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul dang mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams rgyas par khyab bo/ / 'jig rten gyi khams de dag na sems can gang dag 'gro ba drug tu skyes pa de
12a3: dag thams cad dri des mchog tu bde bas tshim zhing sems dga' bar gyur te/ sdug bsngal thams cad dang bral nas phan tshun 'dri ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams mi 'jed de na byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i
12a4: snying po byang chub sems dpa'i cho 'phrul sna tshogs ston pargyang ring po nas mthong ngo / / de dag gis mthong nas kyang phyag 'tshal lo// skyes bu dam pa de la phyag btsal ma thag tu sems can gang dag ngan 'gro
12a5: log par ltung bar dong ba de dag kyang mchog tu bde ba dang / dga' ba dang rangs pa dang / dad pa thob nas skad cig de nyid la ngan 'gro log par ltung ba las grol te sum bcu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams kyi nang du skyes
12a6: nas bar snang la 'khod de/ / de dag gis bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa dang / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje dang / byang chub sems
12a7: dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po la mchod pa'i sprin chen pos mchod nas lan 'bum phrag du ma mtha' yas mu med par bskor ba byas te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdo rje'i 'khor gyi khams chen po thams
12a8: cad dang ldan pa la lan bdun bskor ba byas nas lha rnams par snang las babs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar rang rang gi rin po che'i gzhal med khang gi khang pa brtsegs pa dgan lha'i bu mo bye ba khrag

12b1: khrig 'jam phyag du ma dang lan cigatus sa stan dang / bgardob pa dang zhwa byangs kyi sgra 'byin nang tshul dang 'dab phyogs su bcad pa 'di dag gis bcom ldan 'das la mngon par brjod do// gang da
12b2: ngan 'gro mchog tu sdug bsngal 'khrugs pa yi/ / ming yang bde bshegs stobs kyis dang du med mdzad dang // bsod nams mi ldan sems can rnams la'ang rgyal ba mchog/ byams par mdzad bkyem
12b3: ngo mtshar rmad du byung / / bdag cag rnams kyi rmongs pa'i snying gis bsgrubs pa yi// sdig pa'i las gang shin tu bgyid dka' sna tshogs pa// de dag thub pa'i bya dgas de ring blo bur du// skad cig tu ni ji ltar
12b4: rnam par zhig par gyur/ / ji ltar gdugs kyis mun pa mun nag kun bcom dang // ji ltar zhugs 'bar bas ni ras rnams sreg pa dang // bser mas shing bal ltar yang sprin mthor ji bzhin du// de ltar 'gro
12b5: ba'i sdig pa bde bar gshegs kyis bcom/ / bde gshegs sras po mthong ngam thos sam dran gyur na// lhan cig skyes dbang 'od zer dra bas sdig 'phrogs pa// 'gro ba yongs kyi srid pa'i spros pa
12b6: gzhig pa yi/ / thugs dang rtag tu ldan zhing skyo bar 'gyur mi mnga'// mig dang mgo dang snying dang sha khrag tshil rnams dang // srog dang sdug dang bu rnams rtsa ltar bor nas ni// mi mtshungs sems can don
12b7: phyir thugs rjes thugs brlan pa/ / 'jig rten mgon sras de dag rnams la phyag 'tshal lo// yi dgas ltogs la chu dang ro rgya'i zas rnams dang / de bzhin skye bo'i nor 'dod snying dang ldan pa la// thugs
12b8: rje spyod cing rnam pa sna tshogs tshim mdzad pa/ / byang chub sems dpa' khyu mchog de la skyabs su mchi// gang dag mnar med pa yang rab tu bsil mdzad pas// mchog tu che ba'i sems can dmyal 'ang

13a1: bsil bar 'gyur/ / rang bde mi gzigs sems can don brtson thugs ldan pa// 'jig rten 'gon sras mnyam pa med na de la phyag 'tshal lo// gang dag srid par 'khor ba'i srid
13a2: pa'i skyon las grol/ / rkang pa gsung yang las kyi 'bras bu mi 'dor zhing // ye shes me yis rnyog pa sregs kyang thugs rjes brtan// spyod pa bcug med dbang ldan de la phrag 'tshal lo// rtsem dpal ldan rdo rje hU~M
13a3: po bde gshegs sras/ / mtshan gyis mtshan btab sku las 'od stong mang byung ba'i// dri pa rnams dang sna tshogs grwa yis bdag cag sim// skad cig gis ni dmyal bas sum bcu'i lha dbang gyur// bdag cag rnams kyis
13a4: rgyal dang de bzhin rgyal sras dang / de dag rnams kyis gsungs pa mchog tu zhi chos la// gus bstod dge ba rgya chen de ring gang thob pa// de myur 'jig rten thams cad bde gshegs thob par shog/ de ltar tshul dang
13a5: 'dra ba'i tshigs su bcad pa rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la bstod nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang ste/ de dag rang rang gi rin po che'i gzhal med khang gi khang pa brtsegs pa rnams su 'khod de chos nyan pa'i phyir/
13a6: phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying pos byang chub sems dpa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul chen po 'di lta bu 'di bstan nas// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
13a7: padagra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa dang gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdo rje'i 'khor gyi khyams chen po thams cad dang ldan pa la mchod pa'i sprin chen po
13a8: rnams kyis mchod nas ting nge 'dzin de las langs te/ bar sdang las babs nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag dang lhan cig tu la na 'bum phrag du ma mtha' yas su med par bskor ba byas nas

13b1: pus mo g.yas pa'i lhang rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po la btsugs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas bcom ldan 'das la lta'o// rigs kyi bu de dag thams cad kyang dga' ba dang mgu ba skyes nas de bzhin
13b2: du bcom ldan 'das la lta'o/ / bltas nas kyang sgra skad kyi ro gcig tu bcom ldan 'das la tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// dran pa'i gzhus 'phangs pa ye shes rab
13b3: mda' mang gis/ / ma 'phangs mthur ldan bdud bzhi pa ma mdzad cing 'jig rten nyon mongs nyen pa'i mun pa gsal mdzad nas// bla ma sprin med zla ba bzhin du lta de'o// dam chos 'od mang gti mug bcom pa
13b4: dra ba yis/ / 'dul ba'i pad ma'i gnas rnams kha phye nas// ye shes nam mkha' che la dri med 'bar ba'i gzugs// nyi ma ji bzhin gdung bar bgyi ba'i bdud sde gdungs// mu stegs can gyi nga rgyal mtha'
13b5: dag pha ma mdzad cing / / 'gro ba'i 'dod chags rab gdung ma lus rab zhi mdzad/ dge ba'i lo tog rtsi chen yang dag 'phel mdzad pa/ dge ba'i char pa phab cing 'brug ltar skrag tu gsol// mgon po mu stegs
13b6: can gyi wa brgya pa ma mdzad cing / / bdud rnams bcom ste byang chub dam pa rab brnyes nas// ma 'dres bsags pa'i bden pa'i stobs kyis mthu mnga' ba// skye ba'i 'jigs las rab grol seng ge ji bzhin
13b7: sgrogs/ / spyod pa zab cing brtan la rtag tu mi dpogs pa// sems can gnas gyur stobs dang ting 'dzin nor bu bkram// dri med chos lhun 'dul ba'i ri bos rnam 'dzin pa// ye shes rgya mtsho mchog khyod skye
13b8: dgu mchog gtso ba/ / tshul khrims bzang po'i rtsa ba sbyin pa'i chus btab 'phel// byams dang bzod pa'i me tog yal ga 'khrungs pas mdzes// byang chub yan lag lam gyi 'bru chags 'dod byas bsten

14a1: bsod nams dpag pasam shing kyad na ga las byung / / sam bcurgya gnyis 'ab ba mtshan byas yan lag brtan// depe byu bdang bag na can ma gal gyis ban par// sa dang dbad
14a2: dam chos phu rab brtan btab pa/ lhun po bzhin du mi g.yo khyod ni 'gro bar mdzes// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snyi pos byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag dang
14a3: lhan cig tu bcom ldan 'das la tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang ste/ rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po la phyogs gcig du 'dug go/ rigs
14a4: kyi bu de dag thams cad kyang chos nyan pa'i phyir de bzhin du rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po dag la 'khod do/ / de bzhin du sbyar ste/ de ltar lho phyogs na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
14a5: sangs rgyas dpal gyi snying po brtsegs pa rnam par bsgrags pa'i rgyal po'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams dpal 'byung ba nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i me tog ces bya ba byang
14a6: chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du mas yongs su bskor te mdun du bdar ba nas 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed 'dir 'ongs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang nas rigs kyi bu de dag dang lhan
14a7: cig tu rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po la phyogs gcig tu 'dug pa'i bar du'o/ / de bzhin du nub phyogs na bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas tshe dpag med/
14a8: sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba can zhes bya ba de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug ces bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/

14b1: mthu chen thob pa byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du mas yangs su bska te mdun du bdar ba nas 'jig tan gyi khams mi 'byad 'dir 'das te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gnad nas ngan pa cha bad/
14b2: ma'i snying po la 'dug cing rigs kyi brede dag thams cad kyang chos nyan pa'i phyir de bzhin du rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po dgal 'khod pa'i bar du'o// de bzhin du byang phyogs na bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gzha /
14b3: pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas chos mchog rang bzhin gyis rnam par nges pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba thams cad 'byung ba nas// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
14b4: chen po rin po che'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du mas yongs su bskor te mdun du bad ba nas 'jig rten gyi khams mi 'jed 'dir 'ongs te/ bcom ldan 'das
14b5: kyis gnang nas rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po la 'dug cing rigs kyi bu de dag thams cad kyang chos nyan pa'i phyir de bzhin du rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po dag la 'khod pa'i bar du'o/ / de bzhin du byang shar gyi phyogs
14b6: n a bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas rab gsal dbang phyug gi rgyal po'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams dpal
14b7: brtsegs nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po blo gros brtan pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du mas yongs su bskor te mdun du bdar ba nas
14b8: 'jig rten gyi khams mi 'jed 'dir 'ongs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang nas rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po la 'dug cing rigs kyi bu de dag thams cad kyang chos nyan pa'i phyir de bzhin du rin po che'i

15a1: pad ma'i snying po dag la 'khod pa'i bar du'o/ / de bzhin du shar lho'i phyogs na bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dbang po'i tog gi rgyal
15a2: mtshan gyi rgyal po'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams the tshom dang bral ba nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po blo gros bzang po zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du
15a3: mas yongs su bskor te 'dun du bdar ba nas 'jig rten gyi khams mi 'jed 'dir 'ongs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang nas rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po la 'dug cing rigs kyi bu de dag thams cad kyang chos
15a4: nyan pa'i phyir de bzhin du rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po dag la 'khod pa'i bar du'o/ / de bzhin du lho nub kyi phyogs na bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rin chen
15a5: rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che brtsegs pa nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rin po che blo gros zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' sems
15a6: dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du mas yongs su bskor te mdun du bdar ba nas 'jig rten gyi khams mi 'byed 'dir 'ongs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang nas chos nyan pa'i phyir byang chub
15a7: sems dpa' chen po de dag dang lhan cig tu rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po la 'dug cing rigs kyi bu de dag thams cad kyang chos nyan pa'i phyir de bzhin du rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po dag la 'khod pa'i bar du'o/ / de
15a8: d e bzhin du 'og gi phyogs na bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rin po che'i pad ma la rab tu gnas pa'i ri dbang gi rgyal po'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi

15b1: khams padam kan pa nas/ byang chub sams dpa' sems dpa' chen po nam ma 'a' thos zhes kyang byang chub ses dpa' bya ba khrag khrig 'bram phrag dums yongs su gagang ta mdun du ba dang /
15b2: nas 'jig rten gyi 'ams ni 'byed 'dir 'ongs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang nas rin po che'i bad pa'i tid bol 'dag cing rigs kyi pade dag thams cad kyang chos nyan pa'i gyu de bzhin
15b3: du rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po dgal 'khod pa'i bar du'o/ / de bzhin du seng gi phyogs na bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra btsam pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas g.yul las
15b4: r nam par rgyal ba'i dpal gyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams bdud kyi tsher ma dkrugs pa nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bdud kyi sgrib pa las rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba
15b5: b yang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du mas yongs su bskor te mdun du bdar ba nas 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed 'dir 'ongs te bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang nas rin po tshe'i pad+ma
15b6: ma'i snying po la 'dug cing rigs kyi bu de dag thams cad kyang chos nyan pa'i phyir de bzhin du rin po che'i pad ma'i snying po dag la 'khod pa'i bar du'o/ / de nas de'i tshe stong gsum gyi stod chen po'i 'jig
15b7: rten gyi khams mi 'jed 'dir byang chub sems dpa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rnam par 'phrul pa du ma bstan pas gzhal med khang dang / me tog gi sprin dang rin po che'i sprin dang / phye ma'i sprin dang / spos
15b8: dang byug pa dang / gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / rnam par rgyal ba'i ba dan gyi sprin dang / rin po che spug dang / rdo'i snying po dang / bai dUr+ya dang an da rnyil dang / byi ru dang mar gang

16a1: dang / ma ste dam po nga 'dum ca chuba'i gas stan dang / dag pas ma rgyags nga/ rje'i bdas rnams thabs pa 'arjo dgas lags par brtan r+dz+dza /
16a2: 'jigarten gyi khams pa dang ska ba bzhin du thogs pabu'i 'jig can gyi khams cad med byangs med pasam kyis ma khya nga dpagatsus pa kun la du me cing rjod dum par gartogs pag
16a3: b yem snyed las shin tu 'das pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams dag nags dab pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje'i rnam par thar ba'i nichen po'i ting 'din rnam par 'phrul pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis de bzhin du rmi
16a4: par rgyan par kun tu snang ngo / / 'jig rten gyi khams de dag na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gang dag bzhugs te 'tshe zhing bzhes pa de dag thams cad
16a5: de na bzhugs bzhin du phyag g.yas pa gser gyi kha dog lta bu brkyang ste/ 'jam zhing mnyen la rab tu gzhon zhing pad ma dang yal ga gzhon sha chags shing 'jam pa'i sor mo'i ngos can gdugs
16a6: dang / rgyal mtshan dang / lcags kyu dang bum pa dang / nya dang / sgo khang dang / gzhal med khang dang dung dang // rdo rje dang pad ma dang / dpal be'u dang 'khor lo'i mtshan gyis brgyan pa
16a7: rabs bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du ma nas sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par mdzad pa'i rgyu 'thun pas mngon par grub pa'i dpe byad bzang pos rnam par sbas pa/ sen
16a8: ma zangs 'dra zhing rgyas la snum zhing srab pa'i nor bu'i mdongs kyi me tog gi 'od zer gyis khrig ma mdzes par gyur pa sems can thams cad la mi 'jigs pa sbyin pa dang / yang dag

16b1: par 'thun pa'i phyag rnams kyis gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la yang dag par gzeng bstod pa dang / yang dag par dga' bar bya ba'i phyir spyi bo la blugs nas dus cig tu sgra skad kyi nga ro/
16b2: gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad go bar mdzad cing 'di skad ces/ kye rigs kyi bu gang gi phyir bdud sdig can dang / gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la ma dang cing sdang
16b3: ba'i bgegs dang log 'dren drag shul can drag shul gyi sems dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba gcod pa'i phyir zhugs pa thams cad tshar gcad pa dang / rnam par gzhig pa dang / de bzhin du
16b4: byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sems dang po bskyed pa sems zhum pa brtson 'grus brtan po ma yin pa'i go cha bgos pa rnams kyang yang dag par gzeng bstod pa dang / rab tu dga' bar bya ba nas khams
16b5: gsum par gtogs pa'i sems can thams cad kyi bar dag kyang mya ngan las 'das pa theb par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas dang / chos dang / dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcad pa'i phyir khyod rdo rje'i rnam par thar pa'i sgo chen po'i
16b6: ting nge 'dzin bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab par bsags pa yongs su rdzogs pas grub pa'i mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos smras pa/ ting nge 'dzin dang / dbang dang / gzungs dang stobs dang /
16b7: byang chub kyi yan lag dang / 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'i mthus grub pa/ sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal dang / nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa nye bar zhi ba/ sems can dmyal ba dang dud 'gro'i skye gnas
16b8: dang / yi dgas dang gshin rje'i 'jig rten du ltung ba'i 'jigs pa'i bdud kyi tsher ma ma lus par 'don par lha dang / klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po

17a1: rgyu dang/ ga nga smra ga sa nga 'ag nga
17a2: zhugs pan legs po legs sa nas ga dbul te/ / dka sangs rgyas som ldan 'das dag gis gsung ba ba'i bdag pa lagan rtagazeng bstod do// rangab tu dga' bar ma dang nas rang rang gi phyag
17a3: ste/ rang rang gi byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams chos nyan du gzung ba'i phyir 'jig rten gyi khams mi 'jed 'dir bkye'o// de dag gis gnang bas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' can
17a4: po de dag thams cad kyis kyang de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag la phyag 'tshal nas byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa'i byin gyis rlabs chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rdzu 'phrul chen pos ji tsam du skyes bu stobs dang ldan pas lag pa bskum pa las brkyang ba dang /
