17a7: rgyas shAkya thub pas de'i tshe gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje bdud sdig can 'di rdo rje'i lags pas bcings pa 'di las khrol la ji nas kyang
17a8: sangs rgyas la skyabs su 'gro bar 'gyur ba dang / tshes la skyabs su 'gro bar 'gyur ba dang / dge 'dun la skyabs su 'gro bar 'gyur ba dang / zhan yang gang dag lha dang / klu dang gnod sbyin dang dri za dang / lha ma yin dang /

17b1: nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa gang dag ji tsam du de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la gnas par 'gyur ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la zhugs nas
17b2: kyang ji nas khong du chud par 'gyur ba de ltar gyis shig/ de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rjes bcom ldan 'das kyi ltar mnyan nas bcom ldan 'das la legs so leg so zhes
17b3: gsol te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal nas yang rdo rje'i rnam par thar pa'i sgo chen po'i ting nge 'dzin bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad 'joms par byed pa zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs
17b4: so/ / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rjes rdo rje'i rnam par thar pa'i sgo chen po'i ting nge 'dzin bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad 'joms par byed pa zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ de nas de'i tshe stong
17b5: gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di rnam pa drug tu rab tu g.yos te/ 'gul rab tu 'gul/ kun du rab tu 'gul to// chem che ma rab tu chem che ma kun du rab tu chem chem mo// gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag
17b6: na rdo rje yang me lce 'bar ba gcig tu gyur te/ 'bar rab tu 'bar/ kun du rab tu mched cing 'bar te/ 'jig su rung ba'i mche ba rnon po drag po gzangs can 'jigs pa chen po skyed pa gtsigs te/ mche ba mnan
17b7: nas me lce chen po ltar sma ra ser zhing 'jigs 'jigs ltar 'dug ste/ mi bzad pa rna ba las 'phyad pa'i sbrul dug 'thor dang / ba lang rna lta bu dang / gzar bu lta bu dang / sbrul chen po kha gdangs pa'i kha nas
17b8: byung ba'i mche ba'i rtse mo nas dug drag po 'bar ba 'byung ba'i tshogs kyi phreng bas bzhin du ma 'bar ba/ lag pa stong phrag du ma la rdo rje dang zhags pa dang / gtun shing dang gtun shing rked nyag dang ral gridang 'khor lo dang

18a1: lcags sgrog la sogs pa thogs pa'i mtshon cha'i rtse mo la me stag rab tu 'phro ba'i snang bas stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi khongs su gtogs pa'i gnod sbyin dang / srin po
18a2: dang yi dgas dang / sha za dang ma mo dang / 'byung po'i gdon dang bgegs dang log 'dren la sogs pa sdang ba rab tu sdang ba'i sems can skrag par byed pa ri dgas kyi dbang po'i lpags pa khrag dang bcas pa sham
18a3: thabs su bgos gasngal chen po'i lus kyis rgya gram du dam du bcings pa/ 'jigs pa pas kyang 'jigs par byed pa/ 'chi bdag kyang skrag par byed pa/ khams gsum pa thams cad kyis bsdus pa la bu
18a4: lus dang ldan pa'i khro bor gyur nas lus kyi tshigs thams cad las kyang khro bo kha dog du ma 'di lta ste/ kha dog sngon po dang / ser po dang dmar po dang / dkar po dang nag po ste/ thams cad kyang rdo rje'i rang bzhin
18a5: c an khro gnyer mi mnyam pas rnam par spras pa'i gnyer ma'i khrim gnyer can gyi dpral ba'i dbyes nas me thag lta bu'i rdul gyi thigs pa rtsub po 'dzag pa las drug 'chang rnam pa sna tshags kun du byung bas yan
18a6: lag dang nying lag kun du dkris pa'i mngon rtags can du gyur cing rdo rje drag shul can du snang ste/ mche bas mi bzad par 'dug pa'i kha gdangs pa las ha ha zhes gad mo rtagad 'byung zhing / 'jig pa'i dus kyi
18a7: klung gis char pa dang bcas pa'i sprin dkrugs pa las char gyi rgyun rags pa 'bab pas yongs su gang bas rgya mtsho dkrugs nas rlabs chen po g.yo ba dang / rta rgod ma'i kha nas me 'byung ba lta bu'i hUM zhes bya
18a8: bzab cing brtan pas rgyu ba'i 'byung po'i tshigs 'jigs skrag ste 'byer zhing 'thor nas sngangs te skyabs su dong zhing 'dud pas nyi ma stong pas 'bar ba'i lus rnams mthong ba na/ sna sbar sgur can zhom pa

18b1: wA bu'i bu ga zab mo'i sbubs kyi nang nas sbrul sna tshogs 'khyil ba'i gtsug gnang bu'i 'od kyis 'gras pa rnam par mdzes pa/ glog stong 'dus pa ltar ser zhing dmar ba'i mig gis 'bras bu'i 'od zer gyis sgra
18b2: tshogs rtsub cing bshoral gyen du 'greng ba'i rtse mo brgyan cing 'dres te gsal bar gyur pa/ sbrul gyi gde dag stong gis gdugs byas shing sbrul rnam pa sna tshogs kyi do shal dang / ska rags dang dpung brgyan dang /
18b3: gdu bu dang // rnachas lus brgyan pa/ rdo rje 'bar ba dri ma med cing drag shul can mo bzang ba lag na thogs pa/ 'dzub mo rnams las hUM zhes bya ba'i seng ge'i sgra chen po dag gis bgegs dang log 'dren
18b4: thams cad kun du sdigs pa dag 'thon te/ gang de dag gi mig dang kha rnams nas rnam grum pa lta bu'i sgra chen po'i tshogs las me lce chen po 'bar ba'i tshogs kyi sdang ba byung ste/ des sdang ba'i bgegs dang log
18b5: 'dren la sogs pa drag shul can drag shul gyi sems dang ldan pa/ sdig pa can sdig pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ sdang ba can sdang ba'i sems dang ldan pa rnams tshig par byed/ rmongs par byed 'tshog par byed de
18b6: mi bzad pa drag pa/ rtsub pa sdug bsngal ba/ yid du mi 'ong ba'i tshor ba myong bar byed do// de dag tsho rabs nyen pas dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su dong ngo // de'i tshe bdud sdig can gyis bgegs dang / log
18b7: 'dren de dag tshor ba chen pos nyan te dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su dong ba mthong nas 'jigs dang grag ste skyabs pa rnyed nas rlung drag pos bskyod pa'i shing bzhin du 'dar rab tu 'dar te/ ngu bar 'dod na yang
18b8: ma nus nas ri mo bzhin du lus thams cad g.yo ba med par gyur to/ / de nas gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje sangs rgyas kyi mthus bdud sdig can 'dul bar byed de// sdang ba dang gdon dang / bgegs dang /

19a1: log 'dren thams cad dang / bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad 'joms par byed pa/ rdo rje'i rnam par thar pa'i sku chen po'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ de lta bu'i gzugs su 'dug pa'i rkang
19a2: pa gnyis las khro bo 'bar zhing 'jigs 'jigs ltar 'dug pa/ drag shul gyi gzugs can/ seng ge'i sgra chen po hUM zhes bya ba 'di gnyis phyung ste/ de gnyis skar mda' bzhin du nam mkha'i dkyil du rgyang ring du 'bur/
19a3: te/ nam mkha' la gnas pa'i shugs kyis bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa la lan 'bum phrag dum mtha' yas mu med par bskor ba byas te/
19a4: gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu ci bgyi bka' stsol cig/ de nas gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje lhung mi smra bar 'dug ste/ yang dpral ba'i dkyil nas rdo rje khre bo 'jigs
19a5: pa chen po'i gzugs can mche ba mi bzad pa drag pas 'jigs su rung ba'i kha gdangs te/ mchu ma rungs par bsgyur ba'i kha nas dus kyi tha ma 'jig pa'i tshe rnam par 'thor pa'i rlung drag po'i shugs kyis rab tu bskyod
19a6: pa'i sprin nag po'i tshogs rab tu sgrog pas rnam par dkrugs pa'i rgya mtsho chen po'i sgra drag po lta bu'i hUM zhes bya ba'i seng ge'i sgras gang ba/ bgegs dang log 'dren thams cad 'jigs nas 'bros shing sgyid lug
19a7: nas phyogs smad par byed pa/ lag pa dang rkang pa dang / sen mo dang mig dang / ag tshe ma dang sgra thams cad rdo rje 'bar bar snang bas stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par 'gengs
19a8: pa/ gzi brjid thams cad kyi gzi brjid rnams rang gi gzi brjid kyis zil du rlag par byed cing rgyang ring du byed pa'i rdo rje 'bar ba'i snang ba des rgyu skar dang / gza' dang skar ma dang / nor bu rnams kyis 'od ltar

19b1: mer ma yin/ lhan ner ma yin/ lhang nger ma yin par byed pa/ gang nyi ma dang zla ba rdzu 'phrul che ba/ dbang che bar grags pa/ mthu che ba yang lham mer ma yin/ lhan ner ma yin lhang nger ma yin par byed pa/ de bzhin
19b2: gshegs pa'i 'od dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sa bcu la rab tu gnas pa rnams kyi 'od ma gtogs par 'od gzhan thams cad mog mog por byed pa gzhan phyung ngo // de nas rdo rje khro bo des
19b3: bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa la lan 'bum phrag du ma mtha' yas mu med par bskor ba byas te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang nas
19b4: gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la 'di skad ces smras so/ / rigs kyi bu ci bgyi bka' stsol cig/ de nas gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rjes khro bo chen po rdo rje khro bo de dag la 'di skad ces smras so// kye skyes bu
19b5: dam pa dag deng la bdud sdig can dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su 'dzin du chug shig/ 'di dam tshig la gnas par gyis shig/ gzhan yang gang dag sdang ba gdon dang bgegs dang log 'dren la sogs pa drag
19b6: shul can drag shul gyi sems dang ldan pa/ sdig pa can sdig pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ sdang ba can sdang ba'i sems dang ldan pa dag dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la mi 'jug pa dang / mi rtogs pa dang /
19b7: yid mi ches pa thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la gnas par gyis shig dang / des sems can thams cad kyi yun ring po'i don dang / phan pa dang bde bar 'gyur ro// de skad ces smras pa dang / bre ches
19b8: rdorje lde ba de dgas gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje'i chog mnyan nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa yang bzung ste/ dus gcig du sgra skad kyi nga ro gcig tu seng ge'i sgra chen po hUM zhes byas stong gsum gyi stong na/

20a1: 'di rten gyi khams rgyas par 'gengs shing gsang sngags kyi gzhi dag smras so// sangs rgyas la phyag 'tshal lo// chos la phyag 'tshal lo// dege 'dun la phyag 'tshal lo// yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgya
20a2: na thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun dang bcas pa bdun po dag la phyag 'tshal lo// gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje drug po la phyag 'tshal lo// rig sngags kyi rgyal po chen po
20a3: rdo rje'i lcags kyu la phyag 'tshal lo/ / rdo rje'i lu gu rgyud la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje'i gnam lpags la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje'i shugs la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje bcon la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje yan lag
20a4: dmar la phyag 'tshal lo/ / stobs po che la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rjes rnam par 'joms pa la phyag 'tshal lo// 'gro lding ba la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje po nya mo drug bcu rtsa bzhi la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje'i khri
20a5: po rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ / tad+ya thA/ oM tran tra Ta/ tron ya tro TiT ya/ sUT+Ta s+phu Ta/ s+phu Ta ya sman ya/ s+phoT ya s+phoT ya/ moT moT/ moT ya mo Ta ya/ b+hAn+d+ha b+hUR+ShA/ g+hA d+hA pa ya krAr+'u pa ya/ sarba sat+ka ni/ tras
20a6: sa/ tras ya trA sa ya/ b+h+ra ma b+ha ma/ sam b+h+ra ma ya/ saM b+hU ma ya/ sarba b+hU ta ni/ ku Ta ya ku Ta ya/ saM ku Ta ya saM ku nA ya/ sarba shat+taM naM/ g+ha Ta g+ha Ta/ saM g+ha~M Ti ya~M sa~M g+hA ta ya~M/ sarba bi d+hi badz+ra badz+ra/ s+pho Ta ya badz+ra
20a7: badz+ra/ ka Ta badz+ra badz+ra/ maT+Ta badz+ra badz+ra/ ud tse thA ya badz+ra badz+re/ ha na badz+ra badz+ra/ da ha badz+ra badz+ra/ pa tsa badz+ra badz+ri/ mA thA badz+ra badz+ra/ ud sA d+ha ye ma hA badz+ra badz+ra/ d+hA ra badz+ra pA ti pri ya/ ka ha ka ha/ ha sa ha sa/ ma hA TadaH
20a8: sa/ kha cig tu rgya mtsho'i rlabs 'khrugs pa lte bur zab cing 'jigs su rang ba'i hUM zhes bya ba'i seng ge'i sgras sdang ba rab tu sdang ba bgegs dang log 'dren kun tu grag par byed pa dang / sdang ba thams cad gzhas

20b1: du gsol/ 'joms su stsal du gsol// hUM hUM phaT/ badz+ra b+ha ra brad s+pho Ta/ bsgrub par bya ba lha dang lha ma yin dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / gnod sbyin dang srin po dang / yi dgas dang / sha za dang ma mo dang / 'byung ba
20b2: dang / gdon gyi tshogs mthar 'byin pa/ 'byor bar mdzad pa/ hUM hUM phaT he he phaT// a mo g+ha phaT/ rgyal chen bzhi'i ngos kyi / nga khyi ma dang bcas pa dang / bangang chung ma dang / lcags dang rtsal ga dang @
20b3: pa/ g.yo bar bgyid du su la du gsol// hUM hUM phaT/ 'byer bar bgyid du sbrul du gsol/ hUM hUM phaT/ sum bcu rtsa gsum gyi lha khang khyim dang bcas pa/ bu dang chung ma dang / phyugs dang rtsa lag dang bcas pa g.yo
20b4: bar bgyid du stsal du gsol/ / hUM hUM phaT/ 'byer bar bgyid du rtsal du gsol// hUM hUM phaT/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin khang khyim dang bcas pa/ bu dang chung ma dang / phyugs dang rtsa lag dang bcas pa g.yo bar bgyid du rtsal
20b5: du gsol/ / hUM hUM phaT/ 'thab bral gyi lha khang khyim dang bcas pa/ bu dang chung ma dang phyugs dang rtsa lag dang bcas pa g.yo bar bgyid du stsal du gsol// hUM hUM phaT/ dga' ldan gyi lha khang khyim dang bcas pa/ bu dang /
20b6: chung ma dang phyugs dang rtsa lag dang bcas pa g.yo bar bgyid du srul du gsol// hUM hU~M phaT/ 'phrul dga'i lha khang khyim dang bcas pa// bu dang chung ma dang phyugs dang / rtsa lag dang bcas pa g.yo bar bgyid
20b7: dusu la du gsol/ / hUM hUM phaT/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha khang khyim dang bcas pa/ bu dang chung ma dang / phyugs dang rtsa lag dang bcas pa g.yo bar bgyid du stsal du gsol// hUM hUM phaT/ de bzhin du 'od
20b8: gsal dang / tshangs ris nas gnas gtsad ma'i ris 'og min gyi bar gyi lha khang khyim dang bcas pa/ tha dang chung ma dang / phyugs dang rtsa lag dang bcas pa g.yo bar rabagyid du stsal dri gsol/ hU~M hUM phaT/

21a1: 'byer bar bgyid du stsal du gsol/ rig sngags 'chang grub pa rnams rengs par mdzad du gsol/ rmugs par mdzad du gsol/ rmongs par mdzad du gsol// gcu par gsol gcad du
21a2: gsol/ / gzhig du gsol/ rnam par gzhig du gsol/ mnan du gsol/ hUM hUM phaT/ oM khro bo khro bo chen po rnam par bkra ba/ ser skya bo nag po/ dmar po ser po/ mi pham pa/ rtag tu 'bar ba'i khro bo/
21a3: su ru su ru/ mu ru mu ru mu ru/ tu ru tu ru tru ra/ g+hu ru d+hu ru g+hu ru/ d+hu ru d+hu ru d+hu ru/ tha ra tha ra tha ra/ b+ha ra d+ha ra/ ha ra ha ra/ ya ra ya ra/ ma rA ma ra/ kra hu ku hu/ tsi li tsi li/ mi li mi li/ lu D+ha lu Tu/ sarba
21a4: nA lA ma ma hAM/ pu lu pu lu len tam/ lo ha si lin tA ma/ mu lu lad khA se/ tsu lu tsu len tam/ ma lu bu len tam/ ma lu ru bi/ kurbi burba/ led+b+ha s+phu ra g+ha N+ya s+phu bi ri tsu/ su ru su ru/ mu ru mu ru/ su
21a5: mu su mu ru/ Ta ka Te/ bi ga Te naM ga Te/ ka Ta bi ka Te bi ka Te/ ni ka Te/ ka Ta da ka Te/ dza ye bi dza ye/ dza yan ti/ bi dza ya na ti/ ti ming gi si/ ma hA ti ming gi si/ b+hU tad ga me/
21a6: g+hA ta b+ha rA ya ne/ sdang ba rnams la rjes su 'doms pa/ ma dul ba rnams 'dul ba/ drag shul can rnams 'byer bar mdzad pa/ dpa' bo rnams kyi nang na dpa' ba/ des pa rnams kyi nang na nges pa/ ma grub
21a7: pa rnams grub par mdzad pa/ grub pa rnams chud mi za bar mdzad pa/ sems can thams cad la phan pa mdzad pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis mnas bsgrags pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad la bsnyen
21a8: bkur mdzad pa/ rdo rje'i rigs kyi rig sngags thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa/ tshur gshegs tshur gshegs/ rdo rje ri rab kyi rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa na bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar lha dang / klu dang /

21b1: gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po la sogs pa thams cad kyi mdun du dam tshig gang bcas pa de rjes su bstang du gsol/ rjes su sbyang du gsol// gshegs su
21b2: gsol/ myur du gshegs su gsol/ bdag gi las rnams myur ba myur bar bsgrub du gsol/ skrag par byed pa/ rdo rje 'dzin pa lag na rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo// hu ru hA ru/ grub pa drag po lag na rdo rje bka' stsol
21b3: cig swA hA/ shin tu grub par byed pa la swA hA/ rdo rje chen po la swA hU~M/ rdo rje phur pa la swAhA/ rdo rje 'joms pa la swA tA/ rdo rjes byin gyis rlabs pa la swA hA/ rdo rje ka li ki l-i las / drag po kai la~M ki l-i la swA hA/ pa pog g-i ts+tshaH/
21b4: ki li ki li la swA hA/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa la swA hA/ bdag gi gnod pa dang / nad mgo ba thams cad dang / rims thams cad med par mdzod cig swA hA/ de nas rdo rje khro bo chen pos 'di skad
21b5: spras pa dang / stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di rnam pa drug tu g.yos te/ phyogs dang phyogs mtshams thams cad dang de bzhin du bar snang la rdo rje'i skar mda' chen po'i be tson 'bab par snang
21b6: ngo/ / gan ma grum pa'i sgra chen po yang grag go/ kun nas sa chen po 'di grum par kun du snang ngo // sa chen po'i se ra ka de dag nas yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i chu'i rgyun gyen du byung ngo // chu'i rgyun de dag gis rnam par
21b7: 'jig pa'i dus kyi chu bzhin dras chen po thams cad kun du gang bar snang ngo / / gang dag sa'i 'og na gnas pa'i klu chen po dang / lha chen po dang lha ma yin chen po de dag thams cad kyang sa'i 'og nas 'thon cing dri
21b8: rab kyi drang du 'bon te gyen du byung nas bcom ldan 'das la skyabs su dang ngo / / de nas drag shul can drag shul gyi sems dang ldan pa/ sdang ba can sdang ba'i sems dang ldan pa'i 'byung po dang / bgegs dang log

22a1: 'drer gang dag 'khod pa de dag kyang kun du 'bar/ rab tu 'bar zhing / kun du rab tu 'bar te/ me lce gcig tu gyur pa dag gis rang rang gi lus kun du rnam par 'joms par shes te/ de dag sdug
22a2: bsngal ma bzadang cing drag la rtsub pas nyen nas ha ta zhes bya'i du skad 'thon te tshig 'di skad ces kyang smras so/ / gsang ba pa'i bdag po bdag cag skad cig gis srog kyang ma mchis par 'gyur du bgyid na 'jim
22a3: pa chen por ltung ba 'di las yongs su sgrub tu gsol/ / bgegs dang log 'dren rnams ji lta ba de bzhin du gzhan 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan thams cad na gnas pa dang / ri dang chu bo dang / lteng ka dang rdzing dang
22a4: dur khrod dang shing dang / thibs po dang khron pa rnyed pa dang / btung chu dang lam gyi gzhi mdo dang / sum mdo dang / gtsug lag khang zhigs pa dang / gnas dang lha khang na gnas pa dag thams cad kyis kyang gsang ba
22a5: ba'i bdag po lag na rdo rje 'jigs pa chen por ltung ba 'di las yongasu bskyab tu gsol/ yongasu su du gsol zhes ched du brjod pa ched du brjod do// de bzhin du lha'i khang pa thams cad g.yos/ rab tu g.yos kun du rab
22a6: tu g.yos te/ mog mog por thar cing 'od med par kun du snang ngo // bdud kyi khyim thams cad kyang kun du 'bar/ rab tu 'bar zhing / kun du rab tu mched cing 'bar te/ me ste gcig tu myur par snang ngo // gang
22a7: dag bdud kyi ris kyi lha'i bu de dag thams cad kyang rdo rje khro bo chen pos sangs phyug ste rang rang gis go rdo rje rnams kyis rnam par 'joms pa mthong nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra
22a8: yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa dang gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la skyabs su dong ngo / / bdud sdig can yang shin tu sdug bsngal ba'i tsho bas nyam thag cing skrag la zhum ste gan/

22b1: pas sngangs nas sangs rgyas la skyabs su song / chos la skyabs su sang / dge 'dun la skyabs su so / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rjel phyag 'tshal te/ zla ba na
22b2: rnga khro ba de dag la 'di skad ces smras so/ / ga ga ma rgyam ni pas shin padag nam byang chub kyi snying po la 'dugag par du sangs rgyas la skyabs su 'gro'o// chos la skyabs su 'gro'o//
22b3: 'dun la skyabs su 'gro'o// sems can thams cad kyi don gyi byir pa lta bu dang / ma lta bu dang spun lta bu dang / gnyen lta bu dang sdug gi gzhan mtshams lta bur 'gyur 'brur byang chub tu sems bskyed do//
22b4: bdag deng phyin chad sems can thams cad kyi ba dang ma dang / spun dang gnyen dang / snag gi gnyen mtshams su 'gyur bar bya'o// lus dang ngag dang / yid kyi las cung zad gang ci byed pa de sems can thams cad
22b5: bla na med pa'i ye shes thob par bya ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ / bdag dbugs phyung nas gzhan yang dbugs dbyung ngo // bdag grol nas gzhan yang dgrol lo// bdag mya ngan las 'das nas gzhan yang
22b6: mya ngan las bzla'o/ / rus pa dang rkang dang / khrag dang sha dang / nyams mthu dang srog gis kyang sems can thams cad la rim gror bya'o// mchod par bya'o// brjed par bya'o// sangs rgyas dang byang chub
22b7: sems dpa' dang / 'phags pa nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang / slob dpon dang bla ma'i gnas thams cad la yang bsen bkur bya'o// sI stang bya'o rim gror bya'o// mchod par bya'o// de nas bdud sdig
22b8: can gyis dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su 'gro ba gzung ste/ byang chub kyi sems rin po che bskyed pa dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de ngo mtshar gyur te/ dga' ba thob nas snga sad kyi rog

23a1: tu 'di skad ces smras so/ / gang gi phyir na bdud khyod kyis// sems can kun la bde ba'i phyir// bla med byang chub sems bskyed pa// bdag cag rjes su yi rang ngo // rin chen sems 'dis
23a2: me ring bar/ / nam 'dren sangs rgyas gyur nas ni// sems can shan du sdug bsngal kun// mya ngan las ni bzla bar gyis// rgyal ba'i mchog 'di ji bzhin du// skye dgu thams cad gdul bar byos// stobs
23a3: po che dang ldan pa yi/ / bdud bzhi po dag gdul bar gyis// de skad ces smras pa dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor chen po de sangs rgyas kyi mthus rang rang gi lag gi snyim pa na me tog gi phur ma thogs par
23a4: shes te/ me tog gi phur ma de dag gis bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa dang / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje dang / khro bo chen
23a5: bo rdo rje'i khro bo de dag dang / / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po dang / phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams nas 'dus pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag la gtor
23a6: bdang / de yang sangs rgyas kyi mthus me tog gi gzhal med khang chen por gyur to// bdud sdig can ni mchog tu bde bas tshim par gyur nas sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa sgom zhing rang gi bsod nams kyi rnam
23a7: par smin pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi mthus dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rjes su sems pas mdun du rin pa che'i gzhal med khang chen po dpag bsam gyi shing du mas mig mangs ris brgyad du bris pa/ rin po ched
23a8: no pa dang / sa dang drung dang / man ga sa dang bya dang / ma gang dang / bai dUr+ya dang and d+he la dang / mthon ga chen po dang // ke na dang / ke ke chuchen po dang / rdo rje dang rdo rje chen po dang / dran las dang dran

23b1: las chen pa dang / 'jam bu 'chu ba 'gasar kya dra bas rnam par smras pa/ gdugs dang rgyal mchan dang / bdan dang rnam par rgyal ba'i ba dan bsdud pas lags par brgyan pa matag sa grang bas brang
23b2: pa/ pog snod dum nas bdug pa dri zhim po'i dad kyi dri zhim par byas pa/ phye ma'i dri zhim pa'i bskabs bskos pas/ lha'i bu mo 'bum phrag du ma sil snyan dang / pheg rdob pa dang glu len cing gar byed pa/
23b3: rdzing bu yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i cha can 'bum phrag du ma'i dbus nas rin po che sna tshogs kyi pad ma dang / ku mu da dang / pad ma dkar po dang / uta pa la dang / dri mchog byung bas mdzes par byas pa
23b4: phyogs dang ldan pa zung nas/ de mchog tu dga' ba dang / rangs pa dang / yid bde ba skyes te gus pa thams cad kyis de blangs nas bdud kyi mthu chen po dang / bdud kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen po dang / bdud
23b5: kyi bu yang rdzu 'phrul chen pos lag pa gnyis ka spyi bo la blangs te/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gas dab pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la dga' ba dang / mchod pa'i phyir phul te/ tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshigs su bcad
23b6: pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do/ / 'jig rten dag la dbang byed dbang gis 'byor gyur pa// stobs bcu'i sras rab mchog ldan khyod la rten nas su/ byang chub phyir ni chags bral dri med byang chub sems/
23b7: sems can bde sgrub gter dang 'dra ba ba dag gis thob// bdag mig gti mug mun pas dri can dri med gyur// srid pa'i 'dod chags rab tu zhi zhing spos dang bral// mya ngan las 'das drang po'i lam ni
23b8: bdag la bstan/ / sems dmyal mi bzad thams cad rab tu zhi bar gyur// sdig bral 'jig rten mgon la skyabs su ma song ba// kye ma dman pa yun ring ji lta bslus shig gu// de ring thub dbang sras

24a1: po rnams la bsod nams dang / / dad dang snying rje ting 'dzin thob nas ngo mtshar gyur// sa mchog gcig pur sangs rgyas myur du grub par shog/ gcig pus 'gro ba ma lus mya ngan bzla bar bya/
24a2: srid pa gzhan na kun du rgyu rtse bdag gi yid// rang phan 'jug dang dge bshes bral bar ma gyur cig/ de nas bdud sdig can gyis tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis gsang ba ba
24a3: bdag po lag na rdo rje la mngon par bstod nas cang mi smra bar gyur to/ / de nas gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rjes khro bo chen po rdo rje khro bo de dag la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu dag sdang ba
24a4: dang / gdon dang bgegs dang / log 'dren de dag thams cad gang gis sems can thams cad las rnam par rtsom pa la rnam par mi 'tshe ba dang / bgegs mi byed pa dang / dkon mchog gsum la
24a5: byabs su 'gro bar 'gyur bar de bzhin gshegs pa'i dam tshig 'dzin du chug shig/ rigs kyi bu dag 'di dag la mi 'jigs pa yang byin cig dang / de sems can thams cad kyi don dang phan pa
24a6: dang bde ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa bla med pa yang thob par 'gyur ro// de skad ces smras pa dang / khro bo chen po rdo rje khro bo de dag gis gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la legs so zhes te tshig la mngon
24a7: par dga' nas yang lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po la sogs pa de dag thams cad dang / sdang ba bgegs dang / log 'dren
24a8: dang ma mo dang / yi dgas dang sha za dang / 'byung po dang gdon dang / brjod byed dang / srul po dang lus srul po dang / ro langs dang mkha' 'gro dang / sgrub pa dang sbrul 'dzin bcas pa la sogs pa de dag thams cad

24b1: chags dang ma ldaldan pa yang bya ya gag na sa pa/ nga // nga ba ma dgas pa shAn/
24b2: ces rnam mo// sdang ba 'thung po dang gdon dang / bgags dang log 'dren la sogs padrug shul can drag bral gyi sems dang ldan pa/ sdig pacan theg pa'i sems dang n+danAs/ thung ba can snang ba'i sa /
24b3: dang ldan pa khyed thams cad nyon cig/ khyed kyis dang phan cad sems can gang dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la zhugs pa dag dang / de la sogs pa gang dag gsang rdzogs b+hA ba bam/ klog pa de dag la
24b4: bgegs 'byung bar mi bya zhing 'tshe bar mi bya ste/ sgrub pa dang rjes su 'thun par stobs sbyin par bya'o// sems can gang dag dam tshig la ma zhugs pa de dag la bsrung bar bya/ zhi ba dang bde legs su gyur pa
24b5: dang / chad pa spang ba dang / dug gzhil pa dang / dug bsad pa dang / rig sngags 'grub pa sbyin par bya'o// sbrang rtsi dang / tshigs ma dang / sgog pa dang / ke'u dang / gtor ma dang / 'byung po dang / mi bsgrangs pa
24b6: rnams kyi sha dang zas zos kyang skyon du mi bzung zhing nyes par mi brtsi'o/ / de nas sdang ba 'byung po dang bgegs dang / log 'dren la sogs pa thams cad ces bya ba nas sgra skad kyi nga ro gcig gis 'di skad
24b7: ces smras so/ / zhes bya ba'i bar du sbyar ro// rigs kyi bu dag bka' lung ci stsal pa de bzhin du sbyar bar bgyi'o// deng slan chad sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dang / chos dang dge 'dun la skyabs su mchi'o//
24b8: sems can thams cad kyi don du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do// de nas gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rjes khro bo chen po rdo rje khro bo de dag dang / sdang ba bgegs dang / log

25a1: 'dren dang 'byung po dang / gdon gyi tshogs de dag thams cad la legs so zhes bya ba byin te/ rig sngags kyi las dang dam tshig dang / phyag brgya thams cad 'dzin du bcug go/ gas rab pa'i
25a2: bdag po lag na rdo rje yang rdo rje'i rnam par thar pa'i sgo chen po'i ting nge 'dzin de las langs so/ / de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu
25a3: gang la gnas nas khyod kyis rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul 'di lta bu 'di bstan pa dang / bdud sdig can yang byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang / gzhan yang sdang ba gdon dang / 'byung po dang bgegs dang / log 'dren
25a4: thams cad kyang dam tshig la bkod cing byang chub kyi sems 'dzin du bcug pa'i ting nge 'dzin 'di'i ming ci zhes bya/ de skad ces smras pa dang / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rjes tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu/
25a5: la 'di skad ces smras so// btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu ting nge 'dzin 'di ni ming dang yi ge dang sgra skad kyis rtogs par bya ba ma yino// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gang ming dam gzugs sam/ dbyibs sam gnas
25a6: sam/ mnyam par bzhag pa 'am/ g.yengs pa yang rung ste/ ting nge 'dzin ces bya ba'i chos de gang yang med do// gang la ming med pa dang / gzugs med pa dang / dbyibs med pa dang / gnas med pa dang /
25a7: mnyam par gzhag pa med pa dang / g.yeng ba med pa 'di btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu ting nge 'dzin 'di ming ci zhig bya zhes de la ji snyam du sems/ yang btsun pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu gsal bar byed pa 'di ni bdag la
25a8: gsal bar byed pa ma yin gzhan la gsal bar byed pa ma yin gan ga la yang gsal bar byed pa ma yin no/ / 'on kyang gsal bar byed par btags pa yod do// de la

25b1: gsal bar byed pa ni gsal bar byed pa'i bdag nyid kyis stong bdag ni bdag gis skyong / gzhan yang gzhan gyi bdag nyid kyis sbyong// gnyi ga yang gnyi ga'i bdag nyid kyis stong ste/ yang dag pa ma yin pa kun
25b2: du brtags pa'i phyir ro/ / 'di ci zhes bya ba'i yi ge gnyis kyi tshig de yang tshig gi bdag nyid kyis stong te yi ge yang yi ge ma yin no// de ltar na rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i don rtogs par byed pa yin no//
25b3: don de brjod pa na yang gang nas kyang mi 'ong gang du yang mi 'gro mod kyi gzhan gyi dbang la rten pa'i phyir yi ger brtags pa yang yod do// yongs su btags pa yin pa'i phyir btags pa yang stong pa'o// rten
25b4: cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i phyir gzhan gyi dbang nyid kod pa'o/ / rgyu dang rkyen las byung ba'i phyir rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba yang stong pa'o// blo bur dur+b+ha dang rkyen gyis bskyed pa'i phyir 'byung
25b5: yang 'byung ba'i bdag nyid kyis stong ngo / / de la rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba ni rang gi mtshan nyid kyis stong ngo // rang gi mtshan nyid kyis stong pa gang yin pa de mtshan nyid med pa'o// mtshan nyid med pag nga yin pa/
25b6: de de bzhin nyid// de bzhin nyid gang yin pa de ma nor ba de bzhin nyid do// ma nor ba de bzhin nyid gang yin pa de gzhan ma yin pa de bzhin nyid do// gzhan ma yin pa de bzhin nyid gang yin pa de ting nge 'dzin to// ting
25b7: nge 'dzin gang yin pa de rtogs pa'o/ / rtogs pa gang yin pa de stong pa nyid// stong pa nyid gang yin pa de lhag mtho/ lhag mthong gang yin pa de zhi gnas so// zhi gnas gang yin pa de rnam par thar pa'o// rnam par thar pa
25b8: gang yin pa de dbu ma'i lam yin no/ / dbu ma'i lam gang yin pa de la mtha' gcig med/ mtha' gnyis med/ gzung ba med 'dzin pa po med/ 'dzin pa med chad pa med rtag pa med/ skye ba med// 'gag

26a1: pa med rtog pa med/ rnam par rtog pa med rang dbang med gzhan gyi dbang med/ 'gro ba med 'ong ba med/ kun nas nyon mongs pa med rnam par byang ba med/ 'du ba med 'bral ba med de/ de ni lhag mthong yin no// lhag
26a2: mthong gang yin pa de la phung po rnams med/ khams rnams med/ dbang po rnams med/ skye mched rnams med/ yul rnams med/ yul du gdags pa med/ las med las kyi 'bras bu med do// gang la
26a3: las med cing las kyi 'bras bu med pa de bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub bo/ / tha na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub gang yin pa de bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so//
26a4: bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gang yin pa de chos so/ chos gang yin pa de mi bye mi mchi'o// mi skye mi 'chi ba gang yin pa de nam mkha' dang mnyam pa nyid du khong du chud par bya'o// btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i
26a5: bus smras pa/ rigs kyi bu khyod kyis ting nge 'dzin bstan pa bshad pa 'di ni shin tu zab te/ 'di la nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'gro ba yang med na/ 'jig rten pa'i mu stegs can dang / phas
26a6: kyi rgol ba thams cad lta smos kyang ci dgos chos kyi rnam grangs 'di ni dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bskyed pa dang / mos pa chung ba thams cad kyis shes par dka' ba ste/ gzhan du na 'di de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan gyi
26a7: yul du gyur pa ni ma gtogs so/ / de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i lhan ni dmigs pa med pa gnas pa med pa'o// de skad ces bka' stsal ba dang / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rjes tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa di'i
26a8: bu la 'di skad ces smras so/ / btsun pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa zhes bya ba de ni de bzhin nyid kyi mtshan nyid do// de bzhin nyid kyi mtshan nyid gang yin pa de ni stong pa nyid do// stong pa nyid gang yin pa de la

26b1: de bzhin gshegs pa med do/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan nyid med do// shA ra dwa ti'i bus smras pa/ rigs kyi bu gal te de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan nyid med pa yin no// de la ji ltar skyes bu chen po/
26b2: mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang ldan zhing de bzhin gshegs pa zhes bstan cing depe byad bzang po brgyad bcus sku legs par brgyan/ ji ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gsum rnam par gzhag par
26b3: blta/ ji ltar de bzhin gshegs pa bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas/ gsang ba pa'i bdag po la kun rdo rjes sbas pa/ btsun pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu
26b4: skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis shes bya ba de ni kun rdzob kyi brda'i tshig go/ brgyun ces bya ba de ni spros pa'i yi ge dang bsku'o// dpe byad bzang po zhes bya ba de ni sgyu ma dang /
26b5: rmi lam gyi ngo bo nyid kyi mtshan nyid do// yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ces bya ba de ni nam mkha'i ngo bo nyid kyi mtshan nyid do// sku gsum rnam par gzhag pa zhes bya ba de ni tshe gas gnyis
26b6: kyis sprul pa'i mtshan nyid do/ / btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu lang 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i gsang ba'i yul te/ de la klu'i gsang ba zhes bya ba de ni bsod nams chen po'i rgyu 'thun pa'i mtshan nyid do// bsod
26b7: nams kyi rgyu 'thun pa gang yin pa de de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdzogs par longs spyod pa'i sku ste/ 'di yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i klu'i phrin las dang su'i gsang ba'o// btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu gsung zhes bya ba de ni
26b8: kun rdzob dang don dam pa gnyis kyi mtshan nyid do/ / kun rdzob dang don dam pa gnyis kyi mtshan nyid gang yin pa de de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa'i sku'o// rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba chad pa med pa dang / rtag

27a1: med par 'jug pa thugs su chud pa/ yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i lam gyis 'jug pa/ bsam gtan goms par bya bar shes par bya ba ste/ dmigs pa med pa/ kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam
27a2: par byang bas stong pa/ lus kyi yul ma yin pa/ ngag gi spyod yul ma yin pa/ yid kyi rang gi ngo bo'i yul ma yin pa gang yin pa de ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi sku nam mkha'i khams su yang dag par 'du ba'o//
27a3: de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gsum rnam par gzhag pa ni de ltar blta bar bya'o// btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i gsang ba gang yin pa de ni chos kyi sku'o// chos kyi sku gang yin
27a4: bde ni chos rnams kyi dbu ma'i lam du blta'o/ / dbu ma'i lam gang yin pa de ni mi skye mi mchi ba ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams byung yang rung mabyung ma'u chos kyi sku 'di ni gnas pa nyid do// btsun pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu bsod
27a5: nams kyi rgyu 'thun pa zhes bya ba de ni pha rol du phyin pa dag gi rnam grangs su gtogs pa'o/ / de la pha rol du phyin zhes bya ba de yang bsod nams kyi rgyu 'thun pa nyid du blta'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ btsun pa sharaH
27a6: ti'i bu sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya ba de ni phyi nang gi dngos po rnam pa gnyis yongs su btang bar bya'o/ / de la phyi zhes bya ba de ni kun rdzob kyi tshig go/ nang zhes bya ba de ni don dam pa'i tshig go// nang zhes
27a7: bya ba de ni don ngas pa'i tshig go/ / de la byi zhes bya ba de ni gang zas 'dod pa rnams la zas dang / gos 'dod pa rnams dang / de bzhin du bran po dang bran mo dang / lus byed pa dang / zho shas mtsho ba dang / thang
27a8: dang rta dang / gya nom pa dang rgya che ba dang / rkang pa dang mig dang / sha dang khrag dang rkang dang tshil dang / rus pa'i bar du sbyin pa ste/ de yang thabs kyi pha rol tu phyin pas yongs su zin pas yongs su bsngos pa rnam par

27b1: smin pa la mi re ba dang / gya nom pa dang / brgya che ba dang / rang gi sti stang du byas te rnam pa thams cad sems can thams cad la sbyin pa 'di ni phyi'i'o// nang gi ni chos sbyin pa'o// de yang rnam pa gnyis te/ rten cing 'brel bar/
27b2: 'byung ba la 'jug par yang dag par gzhol ba dang / sbyin pa'i gtam dang / tshul khrims kyi gtam dang / bzod pa'i gtam dang / brtson 'grus dang / bsam gtan dang shes rab dang / thabs dang stobs dang smon lam/
27b3: dang / ye shes kyi gtam dang / snying rjes yongs su zin pa thabs kyi pha rol du phyin pa yang dag par 'du ba'o// gzhan yang nang gi sbyin pa ni gang 'di mthar 'dzin pa dang skye ba dang / 'gag par yongs su rtog pa dang /
27b4: rnam par rtog pa dang / shes pa de shes bya rnam par spangs pa dga' bas yongs su zin pa stobs kyi pha rol du phyin pa yang dag par 'du ba ste/ 'di ni chos kyi sbyin pa'o// gang 'di nyid la lus dang ngag dang / yid
27b5: rgod pa med pa dang khengs pa med pa dang / lus rnam par g.yeng ba med pa dang ngag rnam par g.yeng ba med pa dang / yid rnam par g.yeng ba med par shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pas yongs su zin pa/ gcig tu nyon mongs
27b6: pa med par gnas pa gtang snyoms kyis yongs su zin pa/ thabs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yang dag par 'du ba 'di ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// gang 'di nyid la rang gi lus dang / srog la mi lta bar bsod nams
27b7: dang / bsod nams ma yin pa dang chos dang / chos ma yin pa dang / bden pa dang bden pa ma yin pa dang / g.yo ba dang mi g.yo ba'i dngos po rnam par spong zhing byams pas yongs su zin pa shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa
27b8: yang dag par 'du ba 'di ni 'dir bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ / gang sbyin pa dang / tshul khrims dang bzod pa dang / ting nge 'dzin thob par bya ba'i phyir sems spro zhing rtsom pa dang / yongs su mi skyo bar rtag tu gnas pa

28a1: med pa de de dmigs pa med pa dang / byams pas yongs su zin pa ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yang dag par 'du ba 'di ni 'dir brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di ni bsod nams
28a2: kyi tshogs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdzogs par longs spyod pa'i sku'i gsang ba grub par byed pa'o// btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu gzhan yang ye shes kyi tshogs ni gang pha rol tu phyin pa bzhi po 'di dag nyid rtogs
28a3: pa ste/ pha rol tu phyin pa rnams 'byed pa dang / 'brel ba dang gsal bar byed pa dang / de la gzhol zhing mi rtag pa dang / bdag med pa dang stong pa dang / gsob dang srog dang / dngos po med pa dang / dngos po
28a4: thams cad dngos po med par yang dag par ston to/ / mdor bsdu na 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang gti mug dang / nyon mongs pa dang / nye ba'i nyon mongs pa sel cing chos kyi dbyings nam mkha' mtha' yas
28a5: skye mched dang mnyam par yang dag ston ste/ dmigs pa dang bral ba 'di ni 'dir bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// de bzhin nyid dang stong pa nyid dang / mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid dang / phyi ma'i
28a6: mtha' stong pa nyid dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi rang gi ngo bo nyid gang yin pa 'di ni 'dir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di ni ye shes kyi tshogs so// bsod nams kyi tshogs
28a7: dang ye shes kyi tshogs dang / tshogs 'di gnyis ni byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos dang shes pa dang / shes bya mtha' dag dang / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub yang dag par rtogs par byed pa ste/
28a8: btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i gsang ba mdor bsdus te bstan pa'o// rgya cher rnam par dbye ba ni gal te de bzhin gshegs pa nyid kyis sku tshe'i tshar bskal par bzhugs te bstan

28b1: cing pa shAd kyang mthar phyin par mi 'gyur ro/ / sku'i gsang ba ji lta ba bzhin du gsung gi gsang ba yang de bzhin no// thugs kyi gsang ba ni de bzhin gshegs pas rnam pa dang / so so'i rnam pa dang kha dog dang rtags dang /
28b2: dbyibs dang / ngag gi rnam par rtog pa'i spyod yul dang / bya ba tha dad pa'i sbyor ba rnams kyis kyang bstan par mi spyod mod kyi/ 'on kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i so so rang gi rig pa na thugs kyi gsang ba yin par shes
28b3: par bya'o/ / btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu de ni de'i phyir rnam grangs 'dis kyang de ltar rig par bya ste/ bdag cag lta bu byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs ma rgyas pa rnams kyis bstan pa lta smos kyang ci dgos/ 'on
28b4: kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi brlabs kyis sems can gyi khams mtha' yas mu med pa'i bsam pa dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa dang / mos pa dang blo gros dang / blo dang rtogs pa dang / mngon par 'dod pa mtha'
28b5: yas mu med pa dang / sems kyi rgyun rnam pa tha dad pa sna tshogs kyi rjes su 'gro ba'i spyod yul dang / skye gnas sna tshogs dang / lhan cig skyes pa'i las sna tshogs dang / mi shes pa dang / ma rig pa'i mun pa dang /
28b6: mi snang ba dang mun nag dang / 'grib lnga dang 'gro drug dang / khams gsum pa thog ma dang / dbus dang / 'jig par gnas pa sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' yongs su mchad par gnas par dus gsum dang /
28b7: phyogs la mgo mongs pa/ skye ba dang rga ba la sogs pa na pa dang / nad dang mya ngan dang smre sngags 'don pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang yid mi bde ba dang / 'khrug pa la sogs pas nyin cig bzhin du bcom pa'i sa/
28b8: can rnams kyi sems can ma khams margal ba babral ba dang / ma grol pa dkrol ba dang / dbugs sa byin par grags byung ba dang / yongs su su ngan las ma 'das pa yongs su mya ngan mas pacwab dag ma

29a1: 'di la gzung ba dang / gnas pa thams cad gyur pa'i lam la dgod pa dang / mya ngan las 'das pa shin tu bde ba/ don dam pa/ zhi ba 'khrug pa med pa/ dge ba nad med pa dang / sangs
29a2: rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi so so rang gi rig pa'i ye shes kyi dbyibs mnyam pa nyid kyis mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa/ rnam pa thams cad kyi mchog dang ldan pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes
29a3: la sbyar ba dang / yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang / yang dag par gzeng stod pa dang / yang dag par rab tu dga' bar bya ba dang / dga' ba dang dang pa dang / mgu pa'i sa la yang dag par gzung ba dang /
29a4: chos rtogs pa'i khyad par brjod pa dang / rgya mtsho chen po ltar 'dul ba'i sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i dus dang / tshod las mi 'da' bar bya ba dang / de dag la rgyu de'i dbang du byas te skye bo'i tshogs
29a5: chen po'i don dang / phan pa dang bde ba dang / lha dang mi rnams kyi don dang / theg pa chen po bla na med pa'i chos kyi tshul gcig nas gcig tu brgyad de gnas par bya ba dang / gcig nas gcig tu ldang byin
29a6: pas thos pa dang / bsam pa dang bsgom pa las byung ba'i shes rab dang / ye shes goms pa rnal 'byor du gyur pa'i rgyud kyi rgyun mi gcad pa dang / skal pa yod la yongs su ma smin pa yongs su smin par
29a7: bya ba'i 'os su gyur pa'i don gyi phyir phyogs tsam gyi sgo gcig mdun du byas te 'jug par byed pa ba cung zad cig bshad par bya'o/ / de skad ces smras pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu mchog tu ngo mtshar
29a8: du gyur cing rmad dubyung bar gyur te dga' ba thob nas gsang ba pa'i bdag po la gan rdo rje la 'di skad ces smras so/ / rigs kyi bu legs so legs so// gang gi phyir kho bo cag lta bu nyi tshe ba'i shes pa dang /

29b1: ba gzhan gyis sgra sbags pa'i rjes su 'gro ba'i nyan thos rnams la chos zab mo'i tshig gi don 'di lta bu gsal bar byas pa ni rigs kyi bu khyod yang legs so// lag na rdo rjes smras pa/ btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bred
29b2: de bzhin te/ ji skad smras pa bzhin no// btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu ting nge 'dzin 'di'i ming ci zhes bya zhes de skad zer ba ni ting nge 'dzin 'di'i ming rdo rje'i rnam par thar pa'i sgo chen po zhes bya'o// de nis bcom
29b3: ldan 'das kyis b+hag gsas pa gser gyil dag bar+b+ba dwe T+Te/ b+hagagayas pa'angam 'ang mnyan la byin du gzhon ga chags pa gas ba pa'i bdag po lagan rdo rje'i mgol gzhag/ tshad du bka' phrul ba'ang
29b4: dge kyang ched du bka' stsal to/ / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje khyod kyis gang mdo sde zab mo 'di lta bu 'di gsang ba ba'i tshig gi don bzhin du sems can thams cad la lung bstan cing bshad de bkrol 'i
29b5: rnam par bye ba legs so legs so/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pas lag na rdo rje la ji ltar legs so zhes bya ba byin pa de bzhin
29b6: phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams su gtogs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis kyang gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje'i mgo la phyag gzhag ste/ ched du bka' stsal pa 'di dag kyang ched du
29b7: bka' stsal cing legs so zhes bya ba byin te/ rigs kyi bu chos kyi rnam grangs 'di 'jig rten gyi khams mang po dag na ming 'dzin pa yang dkon na rab tu gsal bar byed pa lta ci smos/ gsang ba pa'i bdag
29b8: p o lag na rdo rjes chos kyi rnam grangs 'di bshad pa na lha'i bu gang gA'i klung tshad med grangs med dpag tu med pa'i bye ma'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul las shin du 'das pa snyed chos rnams la chos kyi mig rdul mar

30a1: cing dri ma dang bral ba skyes so/ / dge slong dang dge slong ma dang / dge bsnyen dang dge snyen ma dang / lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang
30a2: lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa rab tu mang po dag ni mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob par gyur to// de bas kyang ches mang ba'i sems can rnams ni phyir mi ldog pa nyid du bya ba'i phyir bla na med pa
30a3: yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems skyes so/ / stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di dang / de ma yin pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gzhan dpag tu med cing grangs med la brjod du
30a4: med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag kyang rnam pa drug du g.yos so/ / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la yang chos kyis dka' ba dang / mchod pa'i phyir nam mkha'i dkyil na rnga rnams ma brdungs par kun nas/
30a5: sgrasmra byung ngo // byang chub sems dpa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi gzhal med khang gi khang pa brtsegs pa rnams su kun nas sil snyan dang / pheg rdob pa dang glu dbyangs blangs pas lha'i bu mo rnams gar byed do// spos
30a6: dang byug pa dang / bdug pa dang phye ma dang gos dang / gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / dpag bsam gyi shing ljon pa dang / rin po che dang mu tig gi rgyan phreng dang / me tog pad ma dang / ku mu da
30a7: dang / ut+pa pa la dang / dri mchog dang sna ma'i me tog dang / ba ri sha ka dang ba ri sha ka chen po dang / gtang bzung dang / btang bzung chen po dang / man dA ra ba dang man dA ra ba chen po dang many+dza sha ka dang / many+dzu sha ka/
30a8: chen po dang / kun nas skyes dang / kun nas skyes chen po'i me tog gi char gyi sprin kun nas mngon par bab po// spos chu'i char gyi sprin yang mngon par bab bo// de nas tshangs pa dang / khyab 'jug dang / dbang

30b1: phyag chen po dang brgya byin dang / 'jig rten sbyong ba dang / gnod sbyin dang nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / ma mo'i gdon gyi tshogs dang 'byung po dang / brjed byed dang / ske ma byed
30b2: dang srub pa dang / sbrul 'dzin bcas dang gnon po dang / ma mo dang yi dgas dang / sha ze dang bram ze'i srin po dang / mkha' 'gro ma dang / phyogs dang phyogs mtshams dang / mkhar dang ri dang sa'i lha las
30b3: sogs pa sdang ba gdon bgegs dang / log 'dren thams cad dang / de ma yin pa gzhan yang lha dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa dag thugs rnams phrag pa gcig tu gzar te bus mo g.yas pa'i lhangs
30b4: btsugs nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud de bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gang gis bdag cag gzir cing nye bar gzir bas rigs//
30b5: sngags 'chang thams cad dngos grub stsol pa dang / dam tshig thams cad du 'jug pa la yang dag par gnang bar bgyid par 'gyur ba rang gi snying po 'di bdag cag la bstan du gsol// de nas bcom
30b6: ldan 'das kyis tshangs pa la sogs pa lha'i tshogs de dag la legs so zhes bya ba byin te/ grogs po dag gang gi phyir khyed cag 'di ltar sems can thams cad la phan pa'i phyir zhugs pa ni legs
30b7: so legs so/ / de'i phyir legs par rab tu nyon la yid la zung shig dang / ngas khyed rang gi snying po bstan par bya'o// de dag gis kyang bcom ldan 'das la legs so legs so zhes gsol to// de nas
30b8: bcom ldan 'das kyis lha'i rnga bo che dang / rgya mtsho dang sprin chen po'i sgra lta bu'i gsung tshangs pa chen po'i sgrabs lhag pa sna tshogs pa snyan cing rgya che la zab pa/ thog ma dang bar dang tha mar dge gsems can thams cad

31a1: cad dul drug gas pa/ 'jags / sh+log nyen pa da pa/ brjod pa'i tshig sas pa gsus thathams cad la go byed pa/ de zhan gshegs pa ma ga' skazla tha
31a2: grub pa'i gsang sngags gzhi 'di dag gsungs so/ / de bzhin gshegs pa dag bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// tAd yaT+Ta/ dza ya dza ya/ dza m+b+ha rAta/
31a3: la sa la/ lAT wan+ta/ rjes ny-i rje / / ga(/ a pa dza~M ta// saH du t+ta bra smram b+ha ni rjes nani// 9tAkA rA le/ 1/ ban budad+ha.at+kaSh+Ta Sh+T+r-i/ nad+hA
31a4: tA Te ni/ bAr+Na sha ba ra~M/ shU ya~M ma hA shrI yai barba adad+hA ta ya shrI// pad+ma ma bi ha~M/ pad ma mA la ni/ badz+ra ma gu ni/ badz+ra ma te/ badz+ra pA tA li/ shU li ni/ badz+ra d+ha re/ hi hi hi ti/ badz+ra pA NI/ he he he na
31a5: badz+ra sh+'u la ki tsakra d+ha de/ ha~M hi/ badz+rA rA NaM/ he te badz+ra/ ha te hi hi/ he cen te/ badz+ra ba Ni/ ka la ka la/ bal 59/ ral ra la/ d+ha sa d+ha ma/ sa ra sa ra/ hA hA hA hU~M/ tsi li mi le/ tshi le/ di le/ daM di la/
31a6: si le/ dz+wa le/ ma hA dz+wa le/ dza li ti/ pra dz+wa li ti/ thar thag geH8/ mu gu te/ k+Sha me k+Sha ma me/ grub pa'i tshogs kyis phyag byas ma/ lha thams cad kyi snying kun du 'jug par byed ma/ sems can thams cad
31a7: kyi snying 'bigs ma/ sdang ba rab tu sdang ba thams cad kyi snying 'joms ma/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po// rjes su skyong ma/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi snying po la 'jug sa tshur shog/ dam/
31a8: tshig rjes su skyongs shig/ sems can thams cad kyi snyid rnams khug la dam tshig la khod cig/ thams cad mkhyen pa la phyag 'tshal lo swA hA/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa thams cad la phyag 'tshal la swA hA/ traT/
31a9: Ta/ s+pho Ta ya swA hA/ gyen du lha la swA hA/ rnam par lA la swA hA/ chu srin la swA hA/ me la swA hA/ tshangs pa la swA hA/ khyab 'jug la swA hA/ drag po rnams la swA hA/ brgya byin la swA hA/ 'jig rten skyong ba rnams pa

31b1: swAhA/ thams cad la swA hA/ lha rnams la swAd+d+ha/ nor rnams la swAhA/ ma mo rnams la swAhA/ mtshan rnams la swAhA/ bgegs dang log 'dren thams cad la swA hA/ sa la swA hA/ dbyangs can la swA hA/ lha dang
31b2: klu dang / gnod sbyin dang dri za dang / lha ma yin dang nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang lto 'phye chen po thams cad dang / srin po la sogs pa khams gsum thams cad du gtogs pa'i sems can thams cad la
31b3: swA hA/ tshur shog tshur shog/ dam tshig rjes su skyongs shig/ ku ru ku ru/ sa ra sa ra/ tiSh+Tha tiSh+Tha/ ha na ha na/ da ha da ha/ pa tsa ba tsa/ hU~M yAM b+h+raM/ tsaN Da li/ ma tang gi/ brah+ma ni/ buk+ka si/ de bzhin gshegs pa
31b4: thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bdag la gsang sngags gzhi rnams grub par gyur cig/ swA hA/ de bzhin gshegs pas rang gi snying po dang / lha thams cad kyi snying po 'di gsungs pa na thams cad dang ldan pa'i lha'i
31b5: 'khor de 'jigs dang des skrag par gyur nas/ chu shing gi tshal rlung drag po chen pos bskyod de rtse ba bcad pa bzhin du g.yo zhing 'gul la snying tshig ste/ rdo rje'i phur bus btab pa bzhin du zug cing zhigs la 'dre zhing
31b6: skyabs btsal ba'i phyir 'du shes tsam gyis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das la 'bod pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu lha'i
31b7: 'khor 'di slong shig/ ngas dam tshig 'di yongs su 'dzin du gzhug go/ rig sngags grub pa 'byor par byed pa'i snying po la gzhol ba bsgrags so// de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / gsang ba pa'i bdag
31b8: po lag na rdo rjes gsang ba pa'i snying po 'dis lha'i 'khor de dag thams cad bslang ngo / / dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje drag po la phyag 'tshal lo//

32a1: oM ki li ki li/ shU la ki li ki li yi swAt+ma/ bcom ldan 'das 'di ni bdag gi snying po mchog tu gsang ba lags te/ rig sngags thams cad 'grub par bgyid pa lags so// des ni bdag kyang
32a2: nas gzhan gyi sngam btang bar mchi'o/ / dbang du mdze'o// dngos grub phul bar bgyi'o// lung bzhin bgyi'o// bsrung bar bgyi'o// dpal bskyed par bgyi'o// bgegs dang log 'dren thams cad rnam par
32a3: bshig go/ / sems can thams cad gdul bar bgyi'o// 'byung ba thams cad rnam par bshig par bgyi'o// nad thams cad gsal bar bgyi'o// sngon gyi las
32a4: gyi rnam par smin pa ni ma gtogs so/ / bcom ldan 'das bdug gi snying po mchog tu gsang ba 'di ni 'di nas bskal pa grangs ma mchis pa gsum du dka' ba spyod pa chen po bgyid pa na gnod pa bgyid
32a5: pa bgegs dang log badren thams cad kyis rnam par gtses pa'i che/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rgya mtsho mchog 'dzin me ltar zlos rnam par
32a6: bsgyings shing rnam par rol pa mngon shes dri zhing snang dpal gyis bdag la bsrung ba'i slad du stsal to/ / gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rje rjes snying po mchog tu gsang ba 'di smras ma thag tu 'khor de thams
32a7: cad bsam gtan gyi dga' ba dang bde bas tshim par gyur te/ gsang ba ba'i bdag po lag na rdo rje'i dam tshig gi bstan pa la gnas so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la bka'
32a8: stsal ba/ kan dga' bo khyod kyis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di zung shig/ chongs shig lhogs shig/ 'dzin du chug shig/ kun chub par gyis shig/ gzhan dag la yang rgya cher yang dag par rab tu ston

32b1: cig dang / des sems can mang po la yun ring por phan pa dang / bde ba dang / tha mar de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes bla na med pa/ chags pa med pa/ sgrib pa med pa thob cing rtogs par 'gyur ro// su chos kyi
32b2: rnam grangs 'di 'chang ba dang / klog pa dang / 'dzin du 'jug pa dang / kun chub par byed pa dang / gzhan dag la yang rgya ched yang dag par rab tu ston pa dang / mchod pa dang yi ger 'dri ba dang / yi ger 'brir
32b3: 'jug pa dang / kha ton byed pa dang / nyan pa dang / sems pa de ring por mi thogs par bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro// 'di nas nam byang chub kyi
32b4: snying po la 'dug gi bar du ngan 'gro log par 'gro bar mi 'gyur ro/ / rigs dma' ba rnams su skye bar mi 'gyur/ dbul po'i rigs rnams su skye bar mi 'gyur te/ shes rab med par yang ma yin/ mdul bar ma yin
32b5: che thung bar ma yin zhing tshe rabs tshe rabs su tshe rabs dran par 'gyur ro/ / byang chub kyi sems brjed par mi 'gyur ro// thos pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// rab tu dben pa la mngon par dga' bar 'gyur ro// 'khor ngan pa
32b6: can ma yin par 'gyur ro/ / tshig gzung bar 'os shing nyan par 'gyur ro// rgal pa bzang zhing gzugs bzang bar 'gyur ro// shes rab chen po dang / slobs pa chen po dang dbang dang ldan par 'gyur ro// de bzhin
32b7: gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par bya ba la mkhas par 'gyur ro/ / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs su zin par 'gyur ro// sdig pa'i grogs pa yongs su spong bar 'gyur ro// pha rol tu phyin pa yongs
32b8: su rdzogs par bya ba la mkhas par 'gyur ro/ / sems can thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba la mkhas par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi zhing ci zhing mtha' yas pa la rdzu 'phral dang ldan par 'gyur ro// rnam

33a1: byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug gi bar du de byang chub kyi sems mi brjed par 'gyur ro/ / tshe 'di nyid la bgegs dang log 'dren dang / rig sngags 'chang grub pa dang / 'byung po dag dang gdon gyi tshog
33a2: dang / ma mo dang yi dgas dang / sha za dang lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang dri za dang / lha ma yin dang nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po la sogs pa thams cad kyis mi thul bar 'gyur
33a3: ro/ / de'i las kyi sgrib pa thams cad byang bar 'gyur ro// nad thams cad dang bral bar 'gyur ro// sngon gyi las kyi rnam par smin pa ma rtogs par 'chi ba'i dus byed par mi 'gyur ro// de la rig sngags
33a4: thams cad kyang 'grub par 'gyur ro/ / de la lha thams cad kyang bsrung zhing sbed pa dang yongs su skyob par 'gyur ro// de'i rtsom pa thams cad kyang sla bar 'gyur ro// 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las
33a5: 'das pa dang dkyil 'khor thamacad kyi dam tshig la zhugs par 'gyur ro/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das chos kyi rnam grangs 'di'i ming ci/
33a6: lags/ 'di ji ltar bzung bar bgyi/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' bo de'i phyir khyod kyis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi mchod pa'i sprin du bstan pa zhes
33a7: bya bar zung shig/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo sgrib pa med pa bskor ba zhes bya bar yang zung shig/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi dbyings la mkhas pa zhes bya bar yang zung shig/
33a8: bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad 'joms par byed pa zhes bya bar yang zung shig/ bdud kyi phyogs 'dul ba zhes bya bar yang zung shig/ rten cing 'brel bar 'jug pa rab tu rtogs pa zhes bya bar yang zung

33b1: shig/ dam pa'i chos kyi phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid ces bya bar yang zung shig/ rig sngags dang dkyil 'khor dang / phyag rgya dang dam tshig thams cad la rab tu 'jog pa zhes bya bar yang zung shig/ lag na rdo rje
33b2: rnam par thar pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi cho 'phrul zhes bya bar yang zung shig/ rdo rje'i re rab chen po'i rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzungs shes bya bar zung shig/ de nas tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos bcom
33b3: ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la legs so zhes gsol te mngon par dga' nas cang mi smra bar gyur to/ / de nas byams pa la sogs pa bskal pa bzang po'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po thams/
33b4: cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po la sogs pa phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams nas 'dus pa de dag thams cad dang / lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin
33b5: dang / nam mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa de dag thams cad dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de bcom ldan 'das dang lag na rdo rjes gsungs pa la mngon par bstod
33b6: 'phags pa rdo rje'i ri rab chen po'i rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzungs rdzogs so/ / // rgya gar gyi mkhan po shI len dra bo d+hi dang / dz+nyA na sid d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban d+he le shes sdes bsgyur
33b7: cing zhus te skad gsar chad kyis kyang bcos nas gtan la phab pa/ / / rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya ma hA ba la nA ma ma hA yA na sU tra/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa stobs po che zhes bya ba theg pa chen
33b8: po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das ri btang bzung chen po ni chos bston te/ de nas bcom ldan

34a1: 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rje sangs rgyas thams cad kyis bstod cing bsngags te bkur nas mngon par dga' bar byas pa yang de nyid du 'dug par gyur to/ /
34a2: de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das phyag gis sems can rnams dbugs 'byin cing shar phyogs na me lce kun du 'bar ba'i phreng ba'i pad ma'i gdan la bzhugs so// bcom ldan 'das kyi g.yas logs/
34a3: na stobs po che lag pa bzhi pa/ lag pa gcig na ni rnga yab thogs lag pa gcig gis ni phyag 'tshal/ g.yas pa na ni be con thogs/ g.yon pa na ni zhags pa thogs pa/ sba lam pa gyen du brdzes
34a4: pa/ mig dmar ba'o// de'i 'og na ni bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin 'khor dang bcas pa'o// g.yas na ni rig sngags kyi rgyal po gnod mdzes so// g.yon na ni bdud rtsi thal sbyor ro// de nas snying po
34a5: rnams ni zla ba 'am pa lta bur gzhag go/ snying po ni ki li ki la dang / 'gro lding ba'i gzungs dang / lus dmar po dang / rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa dang / rdo rje rgya chen te/ snying po'i mchog go/ rig sngags
34a6: kyi rgyal po drag po chen po dang nye ba na ni 'dags pa mA mA kI'o/ / 'phags pa bdud rtsi thal sbyor gyi 'og na ni rdo rje'i lcags kyu dang / rdo rje'i lu gu rgyud do// sgo'i nang logs su ni khro bo rdo rje'i tho ba dang / rdo rje
34a7: be tson gnyis mngon du phyogs par gzhag go/ g.yon logs su ni bcom ldan 'das 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug 'khor dang bcas pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyi g.yas logs su ni gos
34a8: dkar mo'o/ / de'i 'og tu ni sgrol ma dang khro gnyer can no// g.yon du ni rig sngags kyi rgyal po rta mgrin dang / de dag la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po brgya phrag stong dang ngo // de

34b1: bzhin du shar phyogs su ni zla ba dang nyi ma dang / yul 'khor srung dang dbang po'o// me'i phyogs na ni me'i drang srong chen po rnams kyis bskor ba'o// lho phyogs su ni gshin rje dang khyab 'jug go/ bden bral
34b2: gyi phyogs su ni srin po'i bdag po ma mo rnams kyis bskor ba'o/ / nub phyogs su ni klu'i bdag po klu la sogs pas bskor ba'o// rlung gi phyogs su ni rlung lha 'khor dang bcas pa'o// byang phyogs su ni lus
34b3: ngan po 'khor dang bcas pa'o/ / dbang bdag gi phyogs su ni dbang bdag tshogs kyis bskor ba'o// lha'i dbang po brgya byin dang khyab 'jug dang / tshangs pa chen po dang / de la sogs pa gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i

36b1: phaT swA hA/ / de nas de'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa'i 'od zer kun du 'bar ba'i snang bas stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams

39b3: lus sbrul gyi ska rags kyis brgyan pa dga' bar byed ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ / snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu khro bo chel pas bgegs bye ba brgya stong phrag du ma 'dar te gzir ba

40b4: rgyal po mtha' yas la sogs pa klu'i rgyal po rnams kyis sprin chen po las char 'bebs so/ / gal te mi 'bebs na srog skam par 'gyur ro// gong du spros pa'i cho ga bzhin du phyogs kyi cha'am/ klung gi ngos

41a1: dud des bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas te phyogs gcig tu 'dug nas stobs po che zhes bgyi ba ci legs shes gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ stobs po che zhes bya ba/

45a4: par 'gyur ro/ / bla mar byed par 'gyur ro// rim gror byed par 'gyur ro// mchod pa byed par 'gyur ro// chos gos dang gsod snyoms dang / mal cha dang na pa'i gsos sman dang / yo byad rnams

45a6: par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngo bar byed do/ / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag la yang bsnyen bkur byed par 'gyur ro// de dag gi chos
45a7: bstan pa la yang sti stang du byas te nyan to/ / len to// 'dzin to// klog go/ byang chub sems dpa' lag na rdo rje ji lta ba dang mtshungs par stobs kyis pha rol gnon par 'gyur ro// stobs po che pha rol gnon
45a8: bakhro bo de'i mthus bdag dang / sems can thams cad swa sti/ swasti/ sid d+hi/ sid d+hi swA hA/ bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ 'phags pa byams pa dang / 'jam dpal dang 'phags pa

45b1: spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la sogs pa bskal pa bzang po'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po la sogs pa phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi
45b2: khams nas 'dras pa de dag thams cad dang / lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / srin po dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang / lho 'phye chen po dang mi dang mi mang yin pa de dag thams
45b3: cad dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dang / lag na rdo rje yid rangs te bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// 'phags pa stobs po che zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo rdzogs s+ho//
45b4: rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya nI lAm+ba ra d+ha badz+ra pA Ni ka la ba nA ma d+hA raN+De/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi cho ga zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo//
45b5: gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can sangs rgyas gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyis rjes su gnang ba/ mche ba gtsigs pa dang 'tsham pa/ mig me mdag gi phung po 'dra ba/ dbugs me lce lngar
45b6: 'bar ba/ 'jigs pa'i nga ro can/ lag pa dang rkang pa klu nor rgyas kyi bus brgyan pa/ klu nag po se ral khar thogs pa/ klu dga' bo dang nye dga' bo 'bar las rna cha byas pa/ sprul 'bar ba rin po che'i gan
45b7: ban thogs pa/ sbrul gdug pa 'bar ba za ba/ gzhin rgyas pa/ sprin ma dang dpral ba bsdus pa/ ya sos ma mchu mnan pa/ gshin rje'i cha byad can/ lce glog ltar 'gyub/ gsus po che thul zab/ lag
45b8: pabarnabs pa'i mas 'gas par byed pa/ kwa'i rgyal pa 'ad ba bzangs rags su bcings baM/ a pa la nas sngags par byed pa/ rgya mtsho'i rabs su dpag tshad brgyad kri yo de pas dang pa'i bum par byin pa/

46a1: dbang po dang nyi ma phrag pa la khu ra ba/ klu thams cad brlag par byed pa/ gad rgyangs chen po rgod pas kun du 'khrug par byed pa/ gshin rje'i gzugs can/ khams gsum pa 'jigs par byed
46a2: pa/ klu rnams 'chi bar byed pa la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyis gsungs pa'i rig sngags 'di brjod par bya'o// tad+ya thA/ b+ho b+ho bAn nA ga a d+hi pa ta
46a3: oM dan nI lA ma bar d+ha ra sha ri ra/ badz+ra pA Ni hr-i da ya/ yaHsa mA ti kA mA ti/ ud sA da naM u0f7fbi shwata/ tad+ya thA/ bud d+ha budad+ha/ bi bud d+ha/ mati za / g+ha gan ta pra ta gas chi nad tshin da nA ga hri da yA ni/ b+hinaH
46a4: b+hin d+ha nA ga da ma ni/ bi si ma d+ha nA ga sha ri raM/ bi s+pho Ta ya nA gA nA ya nA ni/ tad+ya thA hUM phaT/ nA ga bi dA ra nA ya phaT/ nA god sad nA ya phaT/ nI lAM ba sa nA ya phaT/ a pra ti ha ta ba la ba ra kra mA ya phaT/ kri tAn ta
46a5: ya phaT/ kr-i tAn ta rA pA ya phaT/ roShaN ya phaT/ trA sa nA ya phaT/ gu sman tong sa da nA ya phaT/ pre ta bi shAH bi nA sha ka rA phaT/ ak+Sha a bas+pha ra bin sha ka rA sa phaT/ ta sa ha sa/ dA ra
46a6: rA/ mA ra ya mA ra ya/ nA sha ya nA sha ya/ sarba big+h+nA na bi na sha ka rA ya phaT/ sarba sha twAM saM g+ha bi na sha ka rA ya phaT/ nI lA ma ba ra d+ha ra badz+ra pA Ni rA dz+nyA ba ya ti swA hA// de'i cho ga la gnod sbyin gyis zin pa la tshul
46a7: sngags kyis btab te gtor na btang bar 'gyur ro/ / klu bzlog par 'dod na smag shad kyi lcug ma 'am bal po'i se'u'i lcug mas bya'o// yi dgas dang brjed byed rnams la skud pas bya'o// rims nad
46a8: med par bya ba dang / gzhogs byed na pa dang / yig 'chus pa la ni skud pa sngon pos bya'o// nor 'dod na zhag gcig bsrung bar 'dug ste bog por gyis bdugs na rmi lam du dge ba dang mi dge ba'i/

46b1: mas ya ldanapa dang 'dun na pa da// rnas pa pa thal ba nga la kyag// gas pa 'dun sa / //

46b3: kyis nyan pa lan tshen sA lnga'i skud pa la bsrung ba'i mdud pa byas te mgul du btags na srung ba'i mchog tu 'gyur ro// chom rkun bzlog par 'dod nas sa bya'o// dug la ni u0f7fkra shas bya ba bar bya'o//
46b4: bdag bsrung ba la ni yid kyisas ma chus bya'o// gzhan bsrung ba la ni grang ba sngon pos bya'o// las de dag thams cad ma chags brjod pa ni lanags pa'am/ bdun nam/ bcu ba ni'am/ nyi brtsa gcigs

46b7: bsgyur/ / // rgya gar skad du/ badz+ra bi rA ra NA nA ma d+hA ra NI/ bod skad du/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di
46b8: skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje la bzhugs te/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus lag na rdo rjes lus thams cad rdo rjer byin gyis brlabs nas rdo rje'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par

47a1: zhugs so/ / de nas lag na rdo rje sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis rdo rje khro bo las byung ba rdo rje snying pos rab tu smras te/ mi
47a2: chod pa/ mi shogs pa/ bden pa/ srab/ brtan pa/ thams cad du thogs pa med pa/ thams cad du ma tham pa/ sems can thams cad skrag par byed pa/ sems can thams cad 'jil bar byed pa/ rig sngags

47a5: pathams cad rab tu byin pa/ sems can thams cad srung bzhi pa/ rgyas pa/ sems can thams cad rengs par byed pa/ rmugs par byed pa'i gsang sngags kyi mthu chen po 'di sangs rgyas kyi mthus
47a6: lag na rdo rjes rab tu smras so/ / na mo rat+na tra yA ya/ na ma sh+tsaN Da badz+ra pA Na ye/ ma hA yak+Sha se nA pa ta ye/ tad+ya thA/ oM traT traT/ tro Ta ya tro TA ya/ s+phu Ta s+phu Ta/ s+pho Ta ya s+pho Ta ya/ g+haR+sha g+hA R+Sha/ g+hAr+N+Na pa ya
47a7: b+huR+ShA pa ya/ sarba satwA ni/ bo d+ha bo d+ha/ saM mo d+hA ya sa~M bo d+hA ya/ b+h+ra ma b+h+ra ma/ saM b+hu ma ya saM b+h+ra ma ya/ sarba b+hU ta ni/ ku Ta ku Ta/ saM ku Ta ya saM ku Ta ya/ sarba sha trUM naM/ g+ha Ta g+ha Ta/ sa~M g+ha Ta ya/ sa~M g+ha
47a8: sarba bid+yA badz+ra badz+ra/ s+pho Ta ya badz+ra badz+ra/ ka Ta badz+ra badz+ra/ ma Ta badz+ra badz+ra/ mA tha badz+ra badz+ra/ aT ta hA sa badz+ra badz+ra/ ni la badz+ra/ su badz+ra badz+rA ya swA hA/ he bu lu na ru phu lu/ gr-i h+Na kul+lu/ mi li tsu lU/

47b1: ku ru kuny+tsa/ badz+ra ba dza yA ya swA hA/ ka li ki lA la swA hA/ kaTakaH/ mdumaT/ ra Tar Ta/ mo can bri moT nA ya s+yAt+ma/ car ni tsar/ ha ha / sa sa ra/ mA ra ya mA ra ya/ badz+ra bi dA ra NA la swAH/ ts+tshin da ts+tshind/
47b2: b+hin d+ha b+hin d+ha ma hA ki la ki lA ya swA hA/ ban d+ha banad+ha/ kro d+ha d+ha ba dz+ra ka~M bi ki lA ya sA hA/ tsu ru tsu ru tsaN Da li ki li ki lA ya swA hA/ trA sa yatrA sa ya badz+ra ki li ki lA ya swA hA/ ha ra ha ra/ badz+ra d+hA rA ya swA hA/ pra ha ra praha/
47b3: ra/ badz+ra pra b+hany+dzan la swA hA/ ma ti thir badz+ra/ su ti Thi badz+ra/ prat+ti s+thi ra bar+tha/ ma hA baH/ ya pra ti ha ta badz+ra/ a mo g+ha badz+ra/ oM hi badz+ra/ shrI thAbar+tha/ dA rA ya swA hA/ d+ha rad+ha ra/ d+hi ri d+hi ri/ d+hu rud+har+ya/ sirba badz+ra ku
47b4: a ba ra ta ya swA hA/ a mu ka ma ma ra ya pa Ta/ na mas+sa man ta badz+ra nA~M/ sarba ba laM a ba ra ta ya ma hA ba la ka Ta be ta ta le/ a tsa le/ maN Da la ma ye/ a ti badz+ra/ ma hA ba le be ga/ ra Na ra Na a dzi te/ dz+wa la dz+wa la/ ti Ta
47b5: ti Ti/ ting ga le/ da ha da ha/ te dza ba ti/ ti li ti li/ ban d+ha ban d+ha/ ma hA ba le/ badz+rAM kuka dz+wA la ya swA hA/ na mo rat+na tra yA ya/ na ma shuN Da badz+ra pA Na ye/ ma hA yak+Sha se nA pa ta ye/ tad+ya thA/ oM ha ra ha ra badz+ra/ mtha
47b6: mtha badz+ra/ d+hun d+hu na badz+ra/ da ha da ha badz+ra/ btsa ba tsa badz+ra/ d+ha ra d+ha ra badz+ra/ dA ra ya rA ra ya badz+ra/ dA ru Na dA ru Na badz+ra/ ts+tshin da ts+tshin da badz+ra/ b+hin d+ha b+hi nad badz+ra/ hUM phaT/ na ma sh+tsa Na/ badz+ra kro d+hA ya/ hu lu bu lu/ ti/
47b7: tiSh+Tha/ ban d+ha ban d+ha/ ha na tan/ a mri te hU~M phaT// sdig pa thams cad byang byas na/ sdug bsngal thams cad med par byed// rgyud de cog gi rtsa ba ste/ dpal kun gyis ni legs par brkyen// sems can
47b8: dbang po nyams pa dang / / tshe zad pa dang tshe nyams dang / phun sum tshogs min gang chags dang / lha rnams rgyab kyis phyogs pa dang / mdza sdug skye bo sdang ba dang / blamag sa' la sogs gtses pa dang / phan tshun

48a1: 'thun pa ma yin dang / / nor 'gribs pas ni gnod pa dang // mya ngan ngal las gnod pa dang // 'jigs pa dang ni phongs pa dang // gza' dang rgyu ska dbyad snyems dang / mi bzang gdon gyis nyen pang
48a2: mya ngan ngal las byung ba yi/ / rmi lam sdig pa mthong na yang // des ni rab bkrus gtsang ma yin// mdo sde dam pa nyan par bya/ gang dag yid dge sems dang zhing // gtsang ma'i gos kyis rab brgyan te// zab mo
48a3: sangs rgyas spyod yul ba/ / mdo sde 'di ni nyan byed na// mdo sde 'di yi gzi brjid kyis// srog chags dag ni thams cad kyi// mi bzad pa'i nad rnams kyang // de dag thams cad zhi bar blta// tshe dang bsod nams

48b1: gi cho ga rgyas pa chen po gsang ba dang bcas/ gsang chen dang bcas pa bdag gis bshad lags kyis/ bcom ldan 'das rgyal po'i pho brang lcang lo can du mchis la sems can rnams gdul bar 'tshal//

48b3: yin/ / shin tu thub par dka' ba yin/ 'phags pa'i tshul med pa yin te/ lag na rdo rje khyod kyis rig pa mchog gi cho ga rgyas pa chen po bshad pa gang yin pa de dag thams cad ni gsang ba med par
48b4: las mi byed do/ / lag na rdo rje da bas na rdo rje'i rigs 'di dang / rig pa mchog gi cho ga rgyas pa chen po 'di bde blag tu 'grub par bya ba'i phyir khyod kyi ming brgyad po gsang ba gsang sngags kyi 'khor dang bcas

48b8: thams cad kyang de la srung bar mdzad pa dang / las kyi dngos grub kyang stsol bar 'gyur ba bshad par bya'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das lag na rdo rjes bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis la btugs nas/ bcom

49a1: ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das bdag gi ming brgyad po gsang ba gsang sngags kyi 'khor dang bcas pa rnams gang lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal

49b8: ba rnams 'tshe bar mi 'gyur ro/ / byis 'jog pa rnams kyang gnod par mi 'gyur ro// tad ya thA/ u ki ra ma ki ri/ ma rI tsa par+Na sha pa ri/ u li me/ mi li me/ i li me/ mi li me/ i li me/ mi le me/

50a1: e li mi la me/ cag gi sdig ka nyug ka/ d+hud+hA ra/ pra d+har/ a la ma pa le/ pA lam pa la/ khwa khu ma ti kum dum/ kha ri khi ri/ s+yAd+ha sA d+ha/ sarba bag kA le/ ban d+ham pag k+Sha le/ kun
50a2: dga' bo gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje bcu po 'di dag la rtag tu bdag gi phyi bzhin du 'brang bar gyur nas bdag gnyid log pa dang / myos pa dang / rab tu myos pa yang bsrung ba dang / yongasu

50a6: bskyab pa dang / yongs su bzung ba dang / yongs su bskyang ba dang / zhi ba dang / bde legs su 'gyur bar byed par bcom ldan 'das kyi bkas gsol pa thob shig/ gsang sngags gzhi 'di rnams grub
50a7: par gyur cig swAhA/ tad+ya thA/ sa ra sa ra ne swA hA/ de laM lag na rdo rje bcu po de dag gi gsang sngags gzhi rnams ni 'di dag yin te/ tad+ya thA/ u ka te/ ke ta/ sa ka te/ ud du le/ d+ha d+he/ ta te/ ta bang
50a8: te swA hA/ tsatsa/ tsi khe la tshan na/ b+he d+ha na~M/ sarba bir+ya tshad naM/ sarba kri ta ka kha rda/ ba ra kri ta nA sha ne/ de la rig sngags kyi rgyal ba chen po lagan rdzo bcu po de dag gi gsang sngags gzhi dam pa'ang//

50b1: rnams yin no// tad+ya thA/ a le lak+Sha/ pa ke le la k+She/ u ke bke la k+She swAhA/ tad+ya thA/ du tu hu tra/ hu tu t+ta/ bi tu bi tu/ bi tu tu/ gats+tsha sa ba te/ ba ta ha ta ye sAta/ na mo b+ha ga bA te bud d+ha s+ya ma sid d+h+yan tu man tra
50b2: da swA hA/ bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo dang / lha dang mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs
50b3: pa la mngon par bstod do/ / 'phags pa lag na rdo rje bcu'i snying po rdzogs s+ho// // rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / dAn shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo ts+tsha ba ban d+he ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la
50b4: phab po/ / dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje drag po la phyag 'tshal lo// oM mu tsi ni swA hA/ mu khe se swA hA/ mo hA ni swA hA/ dan ti ri swA hA// cho ga ni chu
50b5: khyor ba gang la bzlas pa byas te 'thungs nas sems bzhin du nyal na lag na rdo rjes rmi lam bston par 'gyur ro/ / rmi lam mthong ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ rdzogs s+ho// // dkon mchog gsum pa
50b6: phyag 'tshal lo/ / phyag na rdo rje 'ganod sbyin gyi bdag po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas rdo rje gzhon nu'i rig sngags bshad do// dngos grub thob pa/ dus ma yin par 'chi ba thams cad yongs su skyob
50b7: pa/ gdon thams cad yongs su 'dul ba/ kun du srung ba/ slar log pa 'di ni rdo rje 'dzin pas bshad do/ tad+ya thA/ badz+re badz+re/ sa ra sa ra/ a mo g+ha badz+ra/ badz+ra ka la ka la A tsi ta badz+re ni/ rak+Sha rak+Sha ra/ rnam maH/

51a1: k+Sha/ As tu/ / sa / rdzu d+ha / / da
51a2: nar pa/ rnaM la bas / sa ma ka sA la/ btsin na/ sanan ti sa ka la ras/ kri shan pag me/ bi kri tra ba ta li rak+Sharak+Shaman/ sarbata sarbataM/ b+h+rUM li b+h+ya/ sarba ba lA sa/ b+h+yas sa sa/ sar+b+ba
51a3: tra kaku ru ku ra/ pa rib ba ri grA ma la ni shAn ti swa s+ya yan/ ngan ra ba ri ha raM/ shas tha ra ha ra/ bi sha tu shanan/ sarba a mr-i ta daM ba ra nan/ tad yathA/ badz+ra badz+re/ ma hA badz+re/ badz+ra mA la d+ha ri/
51a4: badz+ra nad ni/ bdag dang / sems can thams cad la srungs shig/ srungs shig/ gdug pa thams cad med par mdzad cig/ had ha ha had/ gdon thams cad la'o// hUM hUM hUM nAM/ phaT phaT phaT/ d+ha

51a6: b+h+yaHb+h+yaH/ ta ma tam/ bdag la su zhig slong de/ d+h+yaH/ sa sa ra/ dar pa dar ma/ gdon thams cad 'gog pa dang / rdo rje gzhon du slar ldog pa'i rig sngags 'di la su zhig 'a yang byed na/
51a7: gnanga' ba bas kyi batshal pa bdun du gsas// pa / zlas rna na nyid dgras gang bdag la gan kyis ga rdzoga' dang / byang bya byed pa dang / byeng du 'dug pa
51a8: dag gi lus la slar 'gro nang slar 'bar bar 'gyur ro/ / gag te/ a tsalaM/ ri bar baM// ma ha~M ra swA ma b+ha ne/ pracangs ka pa d-i/ 'tsha ba'i dbang po la srungs shog/ sras shog/ nags/

51b1: la bgags byung ba/ sdig pa thams cad dgang bar byed pa'i rig sngags kyi byeng bas so// sa ras pa/ swa re Na d+hasU re trAH/ rdo rje'i bu nyams phyogs thams cad bcingad // bcing bar bya'o// d+yaH/ sa tan dzan ni tam b+hani
51b2: thams cad 'jil pa/ sa zhig rig sngags 'di las 'da' bar byed na drug chen bor 'gyur ro// gang zhig rig sngags 'di lus la 'chang ba dang / kha ton byed na/ de lan ma yang drug gis mi tshugs/
51b3: ma rungs pa'i gdon thams cad kyang 'da' bar mi byed/ phra men ma thams cad kyang 'da' bar mi byed/ mthong ba tsam gyis kyang dbang du 'gyur ro// 'thab mo dang / rtsod pa thams cad las rgyal bar
51b4: 'gyur ro/ / rig sngags 'di'i stobs kyis thams cad sbal lo// a mri te sa b+ha ba swA hA/ bdag la srungs shig srungs shig/ dgra thams cad kyi nang du song yang rung / 'tshe ba'i dus su yang rung / mtho
51b5: du song yang rung / btson ra'i nang du song yang rung / 'jigs pa thams cad rab tu 'jil bar byed pa'i rgyal mo las ma 'da' shig/ lha dang 'jig rten dang bcas pa dang / bdud sde dang bcas pa dang / tshangs
51b6: bar bcas pas kyang mi 'da' na 'dre gdon ngan palta ci smos/ phyag na rdo rje gnod sbyin gyi bdag po'i gzungs rdzogs so// // rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya badz+ra a dzi ti an la pra mo ha nI nA ma d+hA ra NI
51b7: bod skad du/ 'phags pa rdo rje mi 'bam pa me ltar rab tu rmongs byed ces bya ba'i gzungs/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa
51b8: dus cig ra/ bcom ldan 'das rin po che'i rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa can gyi ri/ gangs ri sul gyi mchog/ ri rab kyi smad dang rked ltar gser gyi rdo sna tshogs kyis gang zhing ri'ur bres pa 'bar

52a1: ba/ rin po che'i rdo du ma'i 'od sna tshogs 'ja' lta bu byung ba'i rdo leb yangs pa/ me tog dri zhim po bkram zhing phye ma dang / bdug pa dri zhim pa mang pos phug gi nang dang / nags bsgos pa/ gdugs
52a2: dang / a ga ru dang / phye ma dang / dril bu dang / bla res mdzes par byas pa'i ri bo mchog la bzhugs te/ de na bcom ldan 'das lha rnams dang / lha'i bu rnams dang / lha ma yin rnams dang / lham pon gyi bu rnams dang /

52a4: rnams dang / log 'dren rnams dang / sha za rnams dang / snang ba dang mi snang ba'i ma mo'i tshogs khyab par byed pa rgya chen po dag gis dpag tshad lnga brgyar 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du gyur par 'dus te/ de na gnas

52a7: dang/ mi'am ci rnams dang / srin po rnams dang / srin po'i bu rnams dang / dri za rnams dang / rig sngags 'chang grub pa rnams dang / 'byung po rnams dang / log 'dren rnams dang / sha za rnams dang / snang ba
52a8: mi snang ba'i ma mo'i tshogs rnams dang / 'byung po'i tshogs rnams dang / 'byung po'i tshogs rnams rnam par rgyu zhing ku co dang / 'jigs pa dang nyan thag pa'i sgra 'byin to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa/

52b1: dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pas sgra de dag gsan nas 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// kye bzhin bzangs dag ci'i phyir ku co dang / 'jigs pa dang / nyam thag pa dang / 'khrug pa'i
52b2: sgra 'byin/ de dag gis gsol ba/ bcom ldan 'das bdag cag ni dbang du bgyis te/ gnod pa dang drang bas bkug cing drangs te tho brtsams na/ bcom ldan 'das bskyab tu gsol/ de skad ces gsol
52b3: pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis thams cad kyi steng gi dkyil 'khor yangs pa ston pa'i mchog gi blo gros dang / blo dang / las dang las kyi mtha' dang ldan pa/ sa chen po las sa gzhan thob pa rgyal tshab du
52b4: nye ste/ chos kyi rgyal srid la dbang bskur ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i sems dpa' chen po rjes su dgongs par mdzad pa tsam gyis 'ongs te/ rdo rje'i zom ltar dpung mgo yangs pa/ rdo rje ltar mkhregs pa'i
52b5: gcod pan 'od zer 'tsher ba can/ rdo rje'i dpung rgyan dang ldan pa/ lus mkhregs shings pa/ lag na rdo rje dang / zhags pa dang / lag cha brtan po 'bar ba thogs pa/ rdo rje phur bu srabs rab tu 'joms
52b6: bar byed pa/ mthu chen po g.yog bzhi 'bum lnga khri dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'di kun du snang bar byed cing / rdo rje'i rigs kyi gzhon nu dang / rdo rje'i sde dang / rdo rje'i betson dang / rdo rje'i snying po dang /

53a1: rdo rje gnon pa rnams dang / rdo rje rdzil ma ngan byed rnams yang dag par sbal/ rnam par sprul nang 'khar gyi khyams chen por 'dus pa thams cad la kun du snang bar byed/ rnam par snang bar byed/

53a4: rnams dang lha ma yin gyi bu rnams dang / rlung lha rnams dang / rlung lha'i bu rnams dang / nam mkha' lding rnams dang / nam mkha' lding gi bu rnams dang / 'dus pa chen po'i bar dag sgra 'byin cing / 16

53b1: da/ di dang / mangs par spong pa dang / gas ma dang / yod pa dang / rdul thams dang / brtul zhugs dang / dga' byab dang / dran langs su thams ca las byung ba'i las gyu pa nga rje

54a1: gis rdo rje mi 'bam me ltar rab tu rmongs byed ces bya ba'i gzungs gsung ba dang / gzungs 'di'i stobs dang / bden pa'i byin gyis rlabs kyis 'od kyi 'od zer gyi dkyil 'khor chen po las byung ba'i

54b3: cad mchod nas lag na rdo rje la snying po 'di phul te smras pa/ dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje drag po la phyag 'tshal lo// tad+ya thA/ ta thA ga ta sa mA d+hirmA
54b4: ra NI/ ma hA a bar ta yi sh+ya mi/ a Ti le/ ko Ti bA ba kA ku la shi khi/ ka bi la ke shi/ ta Ti tsi Ta tsi Ti ma Ta ni/ karga Da mu Ti bad Ti badz+re/ ma hA bi d+hu la lo la/ bu gu bu lu/ su mu su mu/ sa ra sa ra/ swa Ta swa Ta/

54b7: las 'das pa'i dkyil 'khor thams cad la mchod pa byas par 'gyur ro/ / dam tshig dang phyag brgya la zhugs par 'gyur ro// bsam pa dang rjes su yi rad bas 'gug par byed do// dug dang gsang sngags dang /
