220b4: gom stabs mtha' yas dang / cha byad mdzes dang / lus chen dang / spyang lto dang/ zhi ba dang / dpa' ba dang / gser dang can dang / mchog tu brtson dang / dug can dang / dbyangs snyan dang / klu'i rgyal po bdud rtsi snying po dang / rab tu char 'bebs chen
220b5: po dang / rnam par g.yo dang / 'khrugs sgra dang / rnga sgra dang / bdud rtsi'i rgyan dang / dga' bar byed pa dang / 'brug sgrogs dang / dpa' sde dang / sred med kyi bu dang / rgya mtsho'i klong dang / klu'i rgyal po yon po dang / klu'i rgyal po chen po
220b6: de dag la sogs pa klu bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag brgyad bcu rtsa bzhi dag 'dus te 'khod pa dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so/ / de'i tshe klu'i rgyal po de dag 'khor dang bcas te/ stan las langs nas bla gos phrag pa
220b7: gshe tug sang te/ bras tho gsas pa'i / ngas la grags nas/ bcom ldan 'das gal ba de logs sa thal ma gyur ba byung na sa pa dang / bra nga chen po byed pas seM ga dang / drag pa dang /
220b8: thug pa dang / ma dpa ga' dang / gdugs dang / rgyam yan na dang bad dang / kyi wa rdzi dang / rol mo'i grwa dang / sril kan dang / bag rdob pa dang / thu byangs dang / rin pa ma tog dang / rin pa che'i
220b9: dang / mu tig go phreng ba dang / klu'i me tog dang / mu tig gi dra ba mchog tu mdzes pa rnams pa sna tshogs dpag tu med pa grangs med pa dag/ bcom ldan 'das la phul nas bskor ba byas te phyogs gcig tu 'dug go/

221a1: phyags gcig tu 'duganas blon la ma rnabs btab pa// lus rgyam ma 'jig rten gyi 'ams rgyas tshathams cad kyi dul parabakyi rdul snyed kyis/ sangs rgyas dang byung chub sems dpa'i 'ab da kyi 'ang/
221a2: rgya mtsho thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rab 'byam rgya mtsho thams cad dang sa dang chud med dru mas ca kyi rdul phra rab kyi rdul rnams dang / gzugs su snang ba thams cad kyi rdul phra rab kyi rdul rnams las rdul phra
221a3: rab kyi rdul re re la yang lus kyi sprin rgya mtsho 'grang pa'i rgya mtsho thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa/ grangs med/ dpag tu med/ bsam gyis mi khyag// mtshungs pa med/ gzhal du med/ brjod du med pa las yang
221a4: dag par 'das pa dag dang / lus re re la yang lag ba rgya mtsho'i sprin phyogs kun gyi rgyun du mngon par phyogs pa dpag tu med/ grangs med pa dag byin gyis brlabs nas/ rdul phra rab kyi rdul gyi tshwa re re las kyang mdzod
221a5: pa thams cad kyi sprin rgya mtsho phyogs kun gyi gzhi rgyas par 'gengs pa ma 'dres pa rnams kyis sangs rgyas dang / / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la mchod pa bya'o snyam pa 'di lta ste/ kun tu spyod pa'i lus rgya mtsho sprin
221a6: ma 'dres pa dpag tu med/ grangs med// bsam gyis mkhyeg gzhal du med/ tshad med/ brjod du med pa dag gis nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i rgya mtsho sprin rnams
221a7: kyis ji lta ba de bzhin du rin po cha thams cad kyi tog dang / 'od zer stug po dang / nyem dang / zla ba thams cad lta bu'i lus kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho ga ni rnams dang / rin bo che thams cad kyi phreng ba dang me tog gi rtsa
221a8: mtsho ni rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi snang ba chen po'i snying pabang brtsegs pabargyamatsho ldan rnams dang / phye ma dang / shing sngon thams cad kyi mnod rgyamatsho sbrani rnams dang / spos dang / 'dug pa thams cad kyi gzugs can

221b1: du ston pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sgra thams cad sgrogs pa'i rol me'i sprin rnams dang / spos thams cad kyi shing ljon brgyapa ro sprin rnams kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu 'bas par byin gyis brlabs nas/ de la sogs pa mchod
221b2: pa thams cad kyi sprin rgya mtsho dpag tu med grangs med/ bsam gyis mi khyab/ gzhal du med/ tshad med/ brjod du med pa/ ma 'dres pa rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la sti stang du bya'o// blams
221b3: bya'o/ / ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// yul thams cad du bkod pa rnam par snang bar byas pa'i snying po can gyi nor bu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun du khebs par byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas dang /
221b4: byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la sti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// thams cad kun du snang ba'i nor bu rin po che 'char 'bab pa bkod pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po'i rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che
221b5: thams cad kyi 'od 'gro ba 'bar ba dang ldan pa sangs rgyas la nges par gyur pa'i dbyangs kyi nor bu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / / kun du sbas 'gengs pa sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi dbyangs can nor bu'i rgyal
221b6: po rgyamatsho sprin rnams dang / kur nas sgor rini po che 'od zer gyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul ba sdang bar byed pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor ma 'dres pa rnams su bkod pa thams cad snang ba kun du ston pa'i
221b7: dang bu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho snyi rnams dang / 'od 'thogrob sngon ma sangs rgyas kyi yul thams cad kyi rjes su 'dug pa'i nod bu'i rgyal po rgyamatsho sbyin da sa / sangs rgyas kyi zhing bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams su ni
221b8: gshegs pa'i gzhal med khang snang ba kun tu ston pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi rdul la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi sku snang ba rnam par snang bar byed pa'i nor bu'i

222a1: rgyal po rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyi nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la sti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par
222a2: bya'o/ / rin po che dang / spos dang / me tog sna tshogs thams cad kyi khang pa brtsegs pa ma 'dres pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu rin po che rgyal po kha dog mtha' yas pa thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa khang pa brtsegs
222a3: pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che'i sgron ma dang / spos kyi 'od 'phro ba can gyi khang pa brtsegs pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / mu tig thams cad kyis rnam par spras pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang /
222a4: me tog thams cad kyi za ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che'i phreng ba mtha' yas pas legs par brgyan pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs
222a5: nas/ phyogs bcu kun tu 'od zer snang ba'i snying po can bkod pa thams cad yang dag par 'du ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi rdul gyis rab tu brgyan pa bkod pa du ma kun du
222a6: ston pa khang pa brtsegs pa'i rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / bkod pa thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa kun tu rgyas par 'gengs pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sgo kun du me tog gi rta babs dral bu'i dra ba
222a7: sbyangs pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la sti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o//
222a8: gsar dang / rin po che sna tshogs kyi tshod tshong dang / phreng ba dang / rin po che'i mgul gdub kyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / me tog snang ba lhur sna tshogs kyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin
222a9: rnams dang / an da d+hil dang / 'dzam bu chu bo gser gyi pad ma sna tshogs kyi snying ba tson gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu rin po che'i sgron ma'i pad ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khwa rgya mtsho sprin rnams

222b1: dang nor bu rin po che snang gsal rgyal mtshan gyi pad ma sna tshogs kyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po ches brgyan pa'i pad ma sna tshogs kyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / an
222b2: darnyil mdzes par 'bar ba'i 'od zer ldan gyi pad ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / 'od zer 'bar ba zad mi shes pa'i gzi brjid dang ldan pa'i pad ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho spri
222b3: rnams dang / rin po che 'bar bar thams cad byung ba'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che 'bar ba mchog dam pa thams cad byung ba'i pad ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho rnams
222b4: dang / sangs rgyas kyi gsung sgra'i 'od zer dang ldan pa'i pad ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin ma 'dras pa rnams kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun du khebs par byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas dang / byang
222b5: chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la sti stang du bya'o/ / bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// spos dang / nor bu sna tshogs thams cad kyi shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sbran rnams dang / kun nas sgo lo ma las
222b6: thal mo sbyar ba'i sprin 'byung ba'i spos kyi shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / shing ljon pa thams cad kyi gzugs mtha' yas pa bkod pa kun du ston pa'i shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / me tog thams
222b7: cad kyi sprini rab tu 'phyang ba'i shing ljon pa lta bu rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / bkod pa thams cad 'byung ba'i mdzod mtha' yas pa dang ldan pa'i shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che 'od 'phro ba thams cad kyi kyi
222b8: rnam par snad ba byed pa'i shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lus byed tsan dan thams cad kyi phyi mar kun du ston pa'i shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / byang chub kyi snying po thams cad

223a1: kyi bkod papasam kyis mi khyab pa'i 'docan gyi shing ljon pa'i dzin che'i gos thams cad kyi mdzod nyi ma skang snang bar byas pa dang ldan pa'i gang ldon pa rgya mtsho smin rnams dang / sgra byang sa thams cad rdzogs pa 'i
223a2: du 'ong ba'i dbyangs kun tu gtong ba'i shing ljon pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che kha dog mtha' yas pa'i pad ma'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / kun tu mngon par phyogs pa'i nor bu'i rgyal po sdang bar
223a3: byed pa'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rgyan bkod pa thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che sna tshogs 'od 'phro ba'i sgron ma'i phreng ba'i snying po can gyi
223a4: seng ge'i khri brgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / kun nas skra rin po che'i shing ljon pa 'byung ba'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / spos dang / me tog dang / pad ma thams cad kyi phreng ba rin po che'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i
223a5: rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gdan bkod pa kun tu ston pa'i nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / bkod pa thams cad kyi phreng ba rab tu sbyangs pa'i rta babs
223a6: stegs bus rab tu brgyan pa'i rin po che'i sprin gyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu rin po che'i yal ga dang phye ma'i mdzod yod pa'i sdong po thams cad kyi snying po can gyi seng ge'i khri rgya mtsho sprin rnam
223a7: dang / spos sna tshogs dang / rin po che'i dril bu ga yer ka'i dra ba kun nas rgyan nyi ma snang bar byed pa'i snying po can gyi seng ge'i 'i rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun du khebs par byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas dang /
223a8: byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la sti stang bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// yid bzhin gyi nor bu'i rgyal po thams cad kyi gzhal med khang rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / an dadril gyi ze ba can gyi

223b1: me tog bkod pa thams cad kyi bla re rgya mtsho sbyin rnams dang / spos dang / nor bu thams cad kyi the re rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba'i sgron ma'i gzugs kyi bla re rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul rnam par
223b2: ston par snang ba'i dbyangs kyi nor bu'i rgyal po bla ra rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu sna tshogs kyi gos bkod pa thams cad snang ba kun tu sten pa'i bla re rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / me tog thams cad kyi chu bo 'bar bar snang ba'i
223b3: rin po che'i bla re rgya mtsho spyan rnams dang / dril bu sna tshogs kyi sgras kun tu rgyas par 'gengs pa'i dra ba'i bla re rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / pad ma 'bar ba kha dog mtha' yas pa sna tshogs su snang ba'i nor bu'i snying po can gyi
223b4: pad ma'i dra ba'i gla re rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / gser gyi dra ba can gyi 'od zer snang ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi bla re rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab par snang ba'i 'od mtha' yas pa bkod pa thams cad kyi rgyan
223b5: bla re rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun tu khebs par byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' gang chen mtsho sprin rgya mtsho thams cad la sti stang bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par
223b6: bya'o/ / nor bu rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis nam mkha'i dkyil kun du khebs par byin gyis brlabs la/ rin po che bcu'i 'od snang ba bkod pa'i me tog gi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnam
223b7: dang / mu tis kha dog mtha' yas pa'i mdzod kyi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi snying rje'i sgo'i sgra'i nor bu'i rgyal po'i gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che
223b8: sna tshogs kyi 'od 'phro ba'i phreng ba'i gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che rdul kun tu snang bas rab tu brgyan pa'i dril bu'i dra ba sbyangs pa'i gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu thams cad kyi sdong po yal

224a1: ga'i rgyun gyi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nyi ma rnam par snang bar byed pa'i 'od 'phro ba'i nor bu'i rgyal po dang / spos dang / gdug pa thams cad kyi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / can dan gyi phye ma'i mdzo
224a2: kun tu rgyas par 'gengs pa'i gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul chen po snang bar byed pa'i kun tu bkod pa rgyas par 'gengs pa'i gdugs rgya mtsho sprin ma 'dres pa rnams kyis sangs rgyas dang /
224a3: byang chub sebs dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la sti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// rin po che thams cad snang ba'i dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che 'od 'phro ba thams cad kyi gzug
224a4: kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin ma 'dres pa rnams dang / me tog gi sprin sdang bar byed pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor
224a5: dang ldan pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad snang bar gtogs pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / kun nas sgo sangs rgyas kyi yul sgrogs pa rin po che'i yal ga'i 'od
224a6: dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / bai dUr+ya dang / rin po che'i rigs dang / nor bu rin po che'i rigs dang / nor bu ri'i rgyal po thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sems can
224a7: kyi gzugs mtha' yas pa dag sems kyi skad cig la kun ston pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi smon lam las byung ba yid du 'ong ba'i sgra rab tu 'byin pa dang ldan pa
224a8: 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du sems can 'dul ba'i dbyangs can nor bu'i rgyal po 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams kyis sangs rgyas dang / byang chub

224b1: sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la sti stang du bya'o/ / bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// nor bu thams cad kyi mdzod kyi 'od zer rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gzugs dang / sgra dang
224b2: dri dang ro dang / reg bya'i 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi 'od 'phro rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos sgrogs pa rgyas par 'gengs pa'i 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin
224b3: rnams dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing bkod pa thams cad sdang bar byed pa'i 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / me tog gi khang pa brtsegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che thams cad kyi rdul
224b4: gyi 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / bskal pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa thams cad du sangs rgyas 'byung bas sems can yongs su smin par byed pa sgrogs pa can gyi 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po
224b5: po che mi zad pa thams cad bstan pa dang me tog thams cad kyi za ba'i 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / khri stan bkod pa thams cad kun du ston pa'i 'od zer rgya mtsho sprin ma 'dres pa rnams kyis sangs rgyas dang /
224b6: byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad la sti stang du bya'o// bla mar bya'o// ri mor bya// mchod par bya'o// rin po che'i 'od 'phyo ba'i kha dog mthar yas pa rgya mtsho spyan ma 'dres pa rnams dang / kun tu'ong
224b7: kyi nor bu'i rgyal po'i 'di zang 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi zhing rgya chen po bkod pa sdang bar byed pa'i 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / spos thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin
224b8: rnams dang / bkod pa thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sprul pa'i 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che sna tshogs kyi shing gi ze ba 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin

225a1: rnams dang / gos thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa' mtha' yas pa'i spyod pa dbyangs can nor bu'i rgyal po'i 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho spyan rnams dang / mu tig na/
225a2: spyod ma thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho sprin ma 'dres pa rnams kyis sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' gang chen mtsho'i sprin thams cad la sti stang du bya'o// bra mar bya'o// ri mir bya'o// mchod par bya'o//
225a3: spos dang / me tog sna tshogs thams cad kyi rgya mtsho smin bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams dang / rin po che 'od 'grob thams cad kyi pad mo 'drab rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu rin po che kha dog mtha' yas pa'i rang
225a4: kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rini ci thams cad kyi 'dog dang ldan pa'i mu tig gi mdzod rgya chen po rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / rin po che dang / spos dang / tsan dan thams cad kyi phye ma rgya mtsho ston rnams
225a5: dang / rin po che thams cad kyi gdugs rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / nor bu'i rgyal po yid du 'ong zhing sdug pa mdzes pa'i dbyangs can rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang // nyi ma'i 'od kyi nor bu'i tshogs kyi phreng ba tu mdze sprin
225a6: rnams dang / rin po che'i mdzod mtha' yas pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams dang / thams cad kun du bzang po'i lus ma 'dres pa rgya mtsho sprin rnams sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' gang chen mtsho'i sprin gyi
225a7: rgyamatsho thams cad la sti stang du bya'o/ / bla mar bya'o// mor bya'o// mchod par bya'o// zhes de lta bu'i smon lam btab nas/ klu'i rgyal po de dag gis yang bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor babyas te/ zhabs//
225a8: la phyag 'tshal ba dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang nas rang rang gi stan la 'khod do// de'i tshe stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i bu'i bdag po chen po phyir mi ldog pa'i smon lam gyi stobs can g.yog mtha'

225b1: yas rgya mtsho sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal po zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pa dang / phyag bya ba dang / bsnyen bkur bya ba dang / chos mnyan pa'i phyir 'dzam bu'i glang 'dir 'ongs so//
225b2: de nas klu'i bdag po g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtsho sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal po stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/
225b3: bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud de/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// gal te zhus nas zhu ba lung bstan pa'i slad du bcom ldan 'das kyis bdag la skabs phye na/ bcom ldan
225b4: 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la bdag phyogs 'ga' zhig zhu'o/ / de skad ces gsol pa dang // bcom ldan 'das kyis klu'i bdag po g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtshol
225b5: sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / klu'i bdag po ci dang ci 'dod pa dris shig dang / dris pa de dang de'i lung bstan pas khyod kyi sems rangs par bya'o/
225b6: de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / bcom ldan 'das la klu'i bdag po g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtsho sprin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal pos 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das rnga
225b7: ltar na klu thams cad kyi klu'i sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun chad par 'gyur/ bde ba thams cad dang ldan pa dang / rab tu dga' bar 'gyur/ 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir dus dus su char gyi rgyun 'bebs par 'gyur/
225b8: dang / shing ge la ba dang / sman dang / nags tshal thams cad 'khrud par 'gyur/ 'bru thams cad skye bar 'gyur/ bcud thams cad yang dag par skye bar 'gyur/ gang gis 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams bde ba dang

226a1: ldan par 'gyur/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis klu'i bdag po g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtsho sprini bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal po la 'di skad ces
226a2: bka' stsal to/ / klu'i bdag po khyod sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la don 'di yongs su 'dri bar sems pa legs so legs so// klu'i bdag po de'i phyir
226a3: legs par rab tu nyon la yid la zung shig dang ngas khyod la bshad do/ / klu'i bdag po chos gcig dang ldan na klu thams cad kyi klu'i sdug bsngal rgyun chad par 'gyur ba bde ba dang ldan par 'gyur ro// chos gcig po
226a4: gang zhe na/ 'ad lta ste byams pa'o// klu'i bdag po byams pa de la gnas pa'i lha dang me rnams ni mes mi tshig/ mtshon gyis mi tshugs/ chus mi khyer/ dug gis mi tshugs/ pha rol gyi dmag tshogs kyis zil
226a5: gyis mi non/ bde bar gnyid kyis ldog par 'gyur/ bde bar sang par 'gyur/ rang gi bsod nams kyis yongs su bsrungs par 'gyur/ bsod nams chen pos gzi brjid kyis gzi can du 'gyur/ lha dang bcas
226a6: pa'i 'jig rten gyis mi rdzi bar 'gyur/ mdzes pa dang mthong na dga' bar 'gyur/ 'gro ba thams cad du thugs thogs med par 'gyur/ sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun 'chad pa dang sa rab tu dga' bar 'gyur/
226a7: bde ba thams cad dang ldan pa dang / mi'i chos bla me rtogs nas lus zhig pa'i 'og tu tshangs pa'i 'jig rten du skye bar 'gyur te/ klu'i bdag po lha dang mi byams pa la gnas pa rnams kyi phan yon 'di dag go/
226a8: gru'i bdag po de bas na byams pa'i lus kyi las dang / byams pa'i ngag gi las dang / byams pa'i yid kyi las kyis gnas par bya'o// klu'i bdag po gzhan yang bde ba thams cad sbyin pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs

226b1: brjod par bya ste/ des klu thams cad kyi klu'i sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun gcod par byed/ bde ba thams cad sbyin par byed de/ 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir dus dus su char gyi rgyun 'bebs par byed/ rtswa dang shing gel
226b2: pa dang / sman dang / nags tshal dang / lo tog thams cad skye bar byed do// klu'i bdag po de la bde ba thams cad sbyin pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs gang zhe na/ tad+ya thA/ d+hA ra NI d+hA ra NI/ ud tA ra ni/ sa ma pra tiSh+Thi te/ Shi
226b3: bi dza ya brna/ sa t+ya pra ti da nya sa raha/ dz+nyA na ba ti/ ud de bA da ni bi nA ma ni/ a b+hi she tsa ni/ a b+hi b+hU hA ra/ shu b+ha ba ti/ a dzi ma ku/ e hi kum ba la ni/ ba hA hA rakl-i shA na/ d+hu na bA ba ma/ sho d+ha ya ma rbAn/
226b4: nir ti ka/ d+harma ta shud d+ha/ lo ka bi ti me ra ra tsas/ duHkha sha ma na sarba bud d+ha a ba lo ka na a d+hiSh+Thi ti/ pradz+nyA dz+nyA na b+he swA hA// klu'i bdag po gzungs kyi tshig don thams cad sgrub par byed pa/ chos kyi skul
226b5: 'jug pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa/ bde ba thams cad sbyin pa 'di dag gzung bar bya/ brjod par bya'o// klu'i bdag po gzhan yang sprin gyi rigs las 'byung ba'i byin gyis rlabs
226b6: bkod pa gzi brjid kyi snying po sprul pa snang bar byed pa/ ye shes kyi tog gi chu'i rgyun gyi sprin gyi dkyil 'khor dpal dang ldan pa/ gser gyi 'od zer rnam par spang bar byed pa/ skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas gcig las byung
226b7: ba'i rus dang / rigs kyi de bzhin gshegs popa rnams kyi mtshan gzung bar bya/ yid la bya'o// de dag gis klu thams cad dang / klu'i rigs thams cad dang // klu'i rus thams cad dang / klu'i tsho gyi
226b8: thams cad dang / klu'i 'byung ba thams cad dang / klu'i skye gnas thams cad dang / klu'i rgyal po thams cad dang / klu'i bu mo thams cad dang / klu'i g.yog thams cad kyi klu'i sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun gcod par byed

227a1: pa bde ba'i yo byad thams cad bsgrub par byed do/ / klu'i bdag po de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan de dag gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad snying po
227a2: can gyi sprin chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa klu'i rigs las byung ba'i sprin gyis rnam par mdzes la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gyi chu
227a3: 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dpal ldan sprin gyi gzi brjid la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen 'byung la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom
227a4: ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa klung gi dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par 'joms pa'i sprin la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa nam mkha' dpag med la phyag 'tshal lo//
227a5: bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen po'i glog 'bar ba'i tshogs la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen mthu rtsal dpa' bo la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan
227a6: 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin mdzes la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin sdung chen po la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gyi dkyil 'khor
227a7: chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gyi 'od la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen seng ge la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan
227a8: 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen gdugs la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa blta sdug sprin chen la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin

227b1: chen pos khebs pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin las 'byung ba snang bar byed pa'i dkyil 'khor phyogs bcu mtho 'gebs rnga'i sgra dbyangs shin tu rab sgrogs la
227b2: phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen bsil 'byung mi dga' rab 'joms sgra zab sgrogs la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen dpal la phyag 'tsha
227b3: lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa gang gA'i chu sprin la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rtsal gyi sprin ltar dpa' bo la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
227b4: pa 'brug sgra sgrogs la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen kun tu ston la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin rgya chen la phyag 'tshal lo//
227b5: bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin 'dzag la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin ltar rnam par sgrogs la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa smin
227b6: ltar 'phags la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin lta bu'i na bza' ba nabs pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sbyin gyis lo tog skyed la phyag 'tshal lo//
227b7: bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gyi gnas la gnas pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa char sprin gyi sprin la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
227b8: smin 'du bar mdzad la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin rnam par rgyas la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen mut+pal pa phyag 'tshal lo// com

228a1: ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen spos kyi sku la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen 'phags la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin
228a2: chen dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen 'od mdzad la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen byin la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'dra
228a3: de bzhin gshegs pa nor bu rin po che chen po'i sprin lta bu la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin ltar rnam par 'joms pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
228a4: pasprin gyi chu bo la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin sdud la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dus ma yin pa'i sprin dang lce 'bab pa rnam par 'joms pa la
228a5: phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen po ltar nam mkha' mtho nas bsgrags pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen sna 'byin la phyag 'tshal lo//
228a6: bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin chen char bu skyes la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa snyems pa'i gzi brjid sgrub pa'i sprin la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
228a7: gshegs pa ro bro badrug dang ldan pa'i chu chen po'i sprin la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa chu 'thor sprin chen la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gsheg pa sprin chen rgya
228a8: mtsho 'gengs la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa char mi 'bab pa na sprin gyis kun tu 'gebs pa la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sprin gzugs mtha' yas la

228b1: phyag 'tshal lo/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas sprin chen po thams cad rnam par sgrub pa 'dzam bu'i sprin gyi dpal gyi gzi brjid 'od mdzad pa sprin gyi
228b2: 'od zer can rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ / klu'i bdag po de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'di dag brjod pas klu thams cad kyi sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun 'chad pa dang / bde ba thams cad dang ldan pa dang / 'dzam pa
228b3: gling 'dir dus dus su char pa'i rgyun 'bab pa dang / rtswa dang / shing gel pa dang / sman dang / nags tshal dang / lo tog thams cad skyed par byed do// de nas bcom ldan 'das la stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i klu'i bdag po
228b4: g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtsho sbyin bkod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal pos gsol ba btab pa/ bcom ldan 'das skad ma'i tshes dma'i phrin dzam gyi lding 'dir chur mi'i bab ze'i tsheg
228b5: dag brjod na char gyi rgyun chen po 'bab par bgyid pa dang / mi bzad pa'i dus kyi tshe dang / gnod pa 'byung ba'i dus kyi tshe dang / chos ma lags pas skye bo 'thab pa'i dus kyi tshe dang / yams kyi nad dang / gnod pa
228b6: 'byung ba'i dus kyi tshe dang / nad dang 'chi ba'i dus kyi tshe dang / skar ma ma rungs pa gnas pa'i dus kyi tshe dang / yams kyi nad dang / 'tshe ba dang / gnod pa thams cad rab tu zhi bar bgyid pa dang / de lta bu'i gzungs kyi
228b7: gsang sngags gzhi rnams shad du gsol/ / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis byin gyis brlab par gsol// gang dag klu thams cad la skul ma 'debs par 'gyur ba dang / lha thams cad rab tu dga' bar
228b8: 'gyur ba dang / bdud thams cad rnam par 'joms par 'gyur ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi 'jigs pa thams cad 'jig par 'gyur ba dang / gnod pa thams cad zlog par 'gyur ba dang / zhi ba dang bde

229a1: legs su 'gyur bar bgyid pa dang / rgyu skar ma rungs pas bgyis parab tu zhi bar 'gyur ba dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis chang ba'i bar chad lnga gsungs pa gang lags pa de dag thams cad sel bar 'gyur
229a2: ba dang / 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char ba'i rgyun legs par 'bab par 'gyur ba de lta bu'i gzungs kyi gsang sngags gzhi rnams bcom ldan 'das mchog tu thugs rje dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la phan par
229a3: thugs brtse ba dang ldan pas bshad du gsol/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba'i tshal lo// daskad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis klu'i rgyal po g.yog mtha' yas rgya mtsho smi
229a4: bgod pa'i gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor gdugs lta bu'i rgyal po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ / klu'i bdag po khyod sems can thams cad kyi don dang / phan pa dang / bde ba'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba 'dem
229a5: pa legs so legs so/ / klu'i bdag po de'i phyir legs par rab tu nyon la yid la zung shig dang / snying rje chen po las byung ba 'brug chen po'i sgra can bsgyings pa dpa' bo'i tog ces bya ba'i gzungs sems can
229a6: thams cad kyi don dang / phan pa dang / bde ba'i phyir sangs rgyas thams cad kyis gsungs pa/ byin gyis brlabs pa/ rjes su yi rang ba bshad par bya ste/ de ni char med pa'i tshe char 'bab par byed/ char ches pa gcod/
229a7: 'chi ba'i gnod pa rab tu zhi bar byed/ klu thams cad skul bar byed/ lha thams cad sim par byed/ bdud thams cad rnam par 'joms par byed/ sems can thams cad bde ba thams cad dang ldan par byed do// tad+ya /
229a8: ma hA dz+nyA na/ a ba b+ha sa ni/ shri te dzo lag sma dri Ta bi kra ma/ badz+ra sad ha ta ne/ ba ra ma bi rA dza/ nirma la gu Na ke/ tu sUr+ya pra b+he/ bi ma lA dag yaSh+Ti/ b+ha ra b+ha ra/ sam b+ha ra sam b+ha ra/ du dum bu/ ha na ha na/ ma hA pra b+he bi d+hutra

229b1: mahA mo d+ha aHka re/ pradzA gra shud d+hi/ ba ra pU ra Na me tre/ mai trai bi ra ma na skan d+ha/ mi tre ma bud d+hur/ dz+wa la dz+wa la dz+wa la dz+wa la/ dz+wa lAm bud d+he bo ga ru su med sha ba le/ tsatra bi shA rAd+he/ aSh+Ta dra sha a be ni kA bud d+hAd+d+harma
229b2: shu D+ha ma ti/ pu tu rA shi/ shu k+Sha d+ha ra ma sa ma ni ti/ ga me b+hi re/ ga ma b+hI raM/ bi rA dza skaM/ bi ma lo/ bi she Sha/ prA ba te/ ni rA sra ba d+harma/ sarba lo ka dz+nye s+tha dz+nye s+tha/ pra ra pra ba ra/ a nud ti ra/ a sa da ge/ d+har d+ha ra/ d+hi d+hi raMd+hA
229b3: rba d+huru/ shAn tam te/ shan ta ba be/ tsa ra tsa ra/ tsa ra tsa ra/ tsa ri tsi ri/ tsu ru tsu ru/ ba ra ma bud d+hA nu mi te/ ma hA pradz+nyA b+hA ra mi te swA hA// de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad ye shes rgya mtsho dang ldan
229b4: pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ / sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char dbab pa'i phyir klu thams cad kyi snying po brjod par bya'o// sangs rgyas dang
229b5: byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi bden pas char ba'i bar chad byed pa lnga bsal bar bya'o/ / s+ya ya the dan sa ra sa ra/ si ri si ri/ su ru su ru/ nA gA nAn/ dza ba dza ba/ dzi bi dzi gi dzu bu dzu bu/ klu chen po dag tshur shi/
229b6: sangs rgyas kyi bden pas 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char rab tu phob shig/ tsa ra tsa ra/ tsi ri tsi ri/ tsu ru tsu ru/ klu'i bdag po chen po dag tshur sheg/ kye klu chen po dag sangs rgyas kyi bden pas 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char
229b7: rab tu phob shig/ bar ba ra/ bi ri bi ri/ bu ru bu ru/ sangs rgyas kyi bden pas klu thams cad dgug par bya'o// byams pa'i sems dang / snying rje'i sems dang / dga' ba'i sems dang / btang snyoms kyi sems dang / sangs
229b8: rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs dang / bden pa dang / bsam pa chen pos klu'i bdag po dag tshung shegasangs rgyas rnams dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan rnams

230a1: dran par gyis shig/ b+ha ra b+ha ra/ b+hi ri b+hi ri/ b+hu ru b+hu ru/ chu chen po'i chu dang / sprin gyi chu 'chang ba can lag gis 'gro ba chen po'i g.yog rnams byams pa'i sems kyis tshur shig/ ston pa'i bstan pa dam pa/
230a2: dran par gyis shig/ g+ha Ta g+hu Da/ g+hi Di g+hi Di/ gU D+ha gU r+Na/ drag shul can/ khro bo shugs chen po dang ldan pa/ dug chen po'i lce 'byin pa rnams byams pa'i sems dang ldan pa tshur sheg/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams
230a3: cad kyi bden pas 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char phab shig/ swA hA/ ta Ta ta Ta/ ti Ti ti Ti/ tu Tu tu Tu/ nor bu chen po'i cod pan thigs pa dang ldan pa/ sbrul gdug pa'i gzugs can rnams dkon mchog gsum gyi byin
230a4: gyis rlabs dran par gyis la/ rdo rje 'chang gi bden pas 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char phob shig swA t+ma/ ka la ka la/ ki li ki li/ ku lu ku lu/ chu chen po la gnas pa dang ldan pa sprin chen po brtsegs pa'i bzhon pa la zhon/
230a5: nas mngon par 'gro ba rnams tshur shig/ byams pa'i sems kyis 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir char gyi rgyun thong shig/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bden pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis rlabs kyis lag na rdo rjes
230a6: bsgo ba/ ra la ra la/ ri li ri bi/ ru lu ru lu/ lag gi 'gro thams cad khyed rnams gnyid med par dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i bden pas/ g+ha ma g+ha ma/ g+hi mi g+hi mi/ glu mu g+hu mu swA hA/ klu thams cad dgug
230a7: go/ / khams pa'i sems kyis babyang chu kyi sems sngon du 'gro bas/ na ra na ra/ ni ri ni ri/ nu ru nu ru/ swA hA// yon po sna tshogs su gyur pa'i mgo stong pa/ mgo dang mig dmar ba/ stobs che ba'i lto'i phye chen po rnams

262a1: sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na// bcom ldan 'das 'dam bu'i khrod na gzings pa'i 'dug gnas na

267b8: po/ / de 'drar bdag kyang grub gyur te// srid gsum re rdzogs bgyid gyur cig/ na mo rad tra yA ya/ na mo Ar+yA ba lo ki te shwa rA ya/ bo d+hi satwA ya/ ma hA satwA ya/ ma hA ka ru Ni kA ya/ oM tsakra

268a1: bti/ tsin da ma Ni ma hA ba du me ru ru tin+ta/ dz+wa la A kar Sha ya hUM phaT swA hA/ rtsa ba'i sngags/ rdzogs s+ho// // oM ba du mo tsan dam Ni dz+wa la hUM/ snying po'o// oM b+ha rang pa du ma hUM// nye ba'i snying po'o//
268a2: oM ma Ni brjon d+ha/ gsang ba'i snying po'o// sngags snying bzhin du 'byung / sprin lam dang tshigs su bcad pa dang sngags su bcas pa/ rdzogs s+ho// // rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya b+hadrA tsI r+yapra Ni d+hAn rAng /
268a3: bod skad du// 'phags pa bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyi rgyal ba// 'phags pa 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur ba la phyag 'tshal lo// ji snyed su dag phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten na// dus gsum gshegs pa
268a4: mi yi seng ge kun/ / bdag gis ma lus de dag thams cad la// lus dang ngag yid dang bas phyag bgyi'o// bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam stobs dag gis// rgyal ba thams cad yid kyis mngon sum du// zhing gi
268a5: rdul snyed lus rab btud pa yis/ / rgyal ba kun la rab tu phyag 'tshal lo// rdul gcig steng na rdul snyed sangs rgyas rnams// sangs rgyas sras kyi dbus na bzhugs pa dag/ de ltar chos kyi dbyings rnams
268a6: ma lus pa/ / thams cad rgyal ba dag gis gang bar mos// de dag bsngags pa mi zad rgya mtsho rna mas// dbyangs kyi yan lag rgya mtsho sgra kun gyis// rgyal ba kun gyi yon tan rab brjod cing // bde bar gshegs
268a7: pa thams cad bdag gis bstod/ / me tog dam pa phreng ba dam pa dang // sil snyan rnams dang byug pa gdugs mchog dang // mar me mchog dang bdug pa dam pa yis// rgyal ba de dag la ni mchod par bgyi
268a8: na bza' dam pa rnams dang dri mchog dang / / phye ma'i bur ma ri rab mnyam pa dang // bkod pa'i khyab par 'phags pa'i mchog kun gyis// rgyal ba de dag la ni mchod par bgyi// mchod pa gang rnams bla med rgya

268b1: che ba/ / de dag rgyal ba thams cad la yang mos// bzang po spyod la dang pa'i stobs dag gis// rgyal bkun la phyag 'tshal mchod par bgyi// 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug dbang gis na// lus dang ngag
268b2: dang de bzhin yid kyis kyang / / sdig pa bdag gis bgyis po ci mchis pa// de dag thams cad bdag gis so sor bshags// phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba kun dang sangs rgyas sras// rang rgyal rnams dang
268b3: slob dang mi slob dang / / 'gro ba kun gyi bsod nams gang la yang // de dag kun gyi rjes su bdag yi rang // gang rnams phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten sgron ma dag/ byang chub rim par sangs rgyas ma chags
268b4: brnyes/ / mgon po de dag bdag gis thams cad la// 'khor lo bla na med pa bskor bar bskul// mya ngan 'das ston gang bzhed de dag la// 'gro ba kun la phan zhing bde ba'i phyir// bskal pa zhing gi rdul
268b5: snyed bzhugs par yang / / bdag gis thal mo rab sbyar gsol bar bgyi// phyag 'tshal ba dang mchod cing bshags pa dang / rjes su yi rang bskul zhing gsol ba yis// dge ba cung zad bdag gis ci
268b6: bsags pa/ / thams cad bdag gis byang chub phyir bsngo'o// 'das pa'i sangs rgyas rnams dang phyogs bcu yi// 'jig rten dag na gang bzhugs mchod par gyur// gang yang ma byon de dag rab myur bar//
268b7: bsam rdzogs byang chub rim par sangs rgyas spyon// phyogs bcu ga la'i zhing rnams ji snyed pa// de dag rgya cher yongs su dag par gyur// byang chub shing dbang drung gshegs rgyal ba dang // sangs
268b8: rgyas sras kyis rab tu gang bar shog/ phyogs bcu'i sems can gang rnams ji snyed pa// de dag rtag tu nad med bde bar gyur// 'gro ba kun gyi chos kyi sa don rnams ni// 'thun par gyur cing re ba'ang

269a1: 'grub par shog/ byang chub spyod pa dag ni bdag spyod cing // 'gro ba kun tu skye ba dran par gyur// tshe rab kun tu 'chi 'pho skye ba na// rtag tu bdag ni rab tu 'byung bar shog/ rgyal ba kun gyi rjes su sngom
269a2: gyur te/ / bzang po spyod pa yongs su rdzogs byed cing // tshul khrims spyod pa dri med yongs dag par// rtag tu ma nyams skyon med spyod par shog/ lha yi skad dang klu dang gnod sbyin skad// grul bum dag dang mi yi
269a3: skad rnams dang / / 'gro ba kun gyi sgra rnams ji tsam par// thams cad skad du bdag gis chos bstan to// des shing pha rol phyin la rab brtson te// byang chub sems ni nam yang rjed mi gyur// sdig pa
269a4: gang rnams sgrib par gyur pa dag/ de dag ma lus yongs su byang bar shog/ las dang nyon mongs bdud kyi las rnams las// grol zhing 'jig rten 'gro ba rnams su yang // ji ltar bad ma chus mi chags
269a5: pa bzhin/ / nyi zla nam mkha' thogs pa med ltar spyod// zhing gi khyon dang phyogs rnams ji tsam par// ngan song sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar byed// bde ba dag la 'gro ba kun 'god cing // 'gro ba thams cad
269a6: la ni phan par spyad/ / byang chub spyod pa yongs su rdzogs byed cing // sems can rnams kyi spyod dang 'thun par 'jug/ bzang po spyod pa dag ni rab ston cing // ma 'ongs bskal pa kun tu spyod par gyur// bdag
269a7: gis spyod dang 'thun par gang spyod pa/ / de dag dang ni rtag du 'grogs par shog/ lus dang ngag rnams dang ni sems kyis kyang // spyod pa dag dang smon lam gcig tu spyad// bdag la phan par 'dod pa'i
269a8: grogs po dag/ bzang po spyod pa rab tu ston pa rnams// de dag dang yang rtag tu phrad par shog/ de dag bdag gis nam yang yid mi dbyung // sangs rgyas sras kyis bskor ba'i mgon po rnams//

269b1: mngon sum rtag tu bdag gis rgyal ba blta// ma 'ongs bskal pa kun tu mi skyo bar// de dag la yang mchod pa rgya cher bgyi// rgyal ba rnams kyi dam pa'i chos 'dzin cing // byang chub spyod pa kun tu snang bar byed/
269b2: bzang po'i spyod pa rnam par sbyar ba yang // ma 'ongs bskal pa kun tu spyad par bgyi// srid pa thams cad du ni 'khor ba na// bsod nams ye shes dag ni mi zad rnyed// thabs dang shes rab
269b3: ting 'dzin namathar dang / / yon tan kun gyi mi zad mdzod du gyur// rdul cig sted na rdul snyed zhing rnams te// zhing der bsam gyis mi khyab sangs rgyas rnams// sangs rgyas sras kyi dbus na bkram
269b4: bal/ / byang chub spyad pa spyod cing blta bar bgyi// de ltar ma lus thams cad phyogs su yang // skra tsam khyon la dus gsum tshad snyed kyi// sangs rgyas rgya mtsho zhing rnams rgya mtsho dang // bskal pargya
269b5: mtshor spyod cing rab tu 'jug/ gsung gcig yan lag rgya mtsho sgra skad kyis// rgyal ba kun dbyangs yan lag rnam dag pa// 'gro ba kun gyi bsam pa ji bzhin dbyangs// sangs rgyas gsung la rtag tu
269b6: 'jug par bgyi/ / dus gsum gshegs pa rgyal ba thams cad dag/ 'khor lo'i tshul rnams rab tu bskor ba yi// de dag gi yang gsung dbyangs mi zad la// blo yi stobs kyis bdag kyang rab tu 'jug/
269b7: ma 'ongs bskal pa thams cad 'jug par yang // skad cig gcig gis bdag kyang 'jug par bgyi// gang yang bskal pa dus gsum tshad de dag/ skad cig cha shas kyis ni zhugs par spyad//
269b8: dus gsum gshegs pa mi yi sang ge gang // de dag skad cig gcig la bdag gis blta// rtag tu de dag gi ni spyod yul la// sgyu mar gyur pa'i rnam thar stobs kyis 'jug/ gang yang dus gsum dag gi

270a1: zhing bkod pa/ / de dag rdul gcig steng du mngon par bsgrub// de ltar ma lus phyogs rnams thams cad du// rgal ba dag gi zhing rnams bkod la 'jug/ gang yang ma byon 'jig rter smon
270a2: ma rnams/ / de dag rim par 'tshang rgya 'khor lo bskor// mya ngan 'das pa rab tu zhi mtha' ston// mgon po kun gyi drung du bdag mchi'o// kun tu myur ba'i rdzu 'phrul stobs rnams dang // kun nas sgo bam
270a3: theg pa'i stobs dag dang / / kun du yon tan spyod pa'i stobs rnams dang // kun du khyab pa byams pa dag gi stobs// kun nas dge ba'i bsod nams stobs rnams dang // chags pa med par gyur pa'i ma
270a4: shes stobs/ / shes rab thabs dang ting 'dzin stobs dag gis// byang chub stobs rnams yang dag sgrub par byed// las kyi stobs rnams yongs su dag byed cing // nyon mongs stobs rnams kun tu
270a5: 'joms par byed/ / bdud kyi stobs rnams stobs medarab byed cing // bzang po spyod pa'i stobs ni rdzogs par bgyi// zhing rnams rgya mtsho rnam par dag byed cing // sems can rgya mtsho dag ni
270a6: rnam par 'grol/ / chos rnams rgya mtsho rab tu mthong byed cing // ye shes rgya mtsho rab tu rtogs par byed// spyod pa rgya mtsho rnam par dag byed cing // smon lam rgya mtsho rab tu rdzogs par byed// sangs
270a7: rgyas rgya mtsha rab tu mchod byed cing / / bskal pa rgya mtshor mi skyo spyad par bgyi// gang yang dus gsum gshegs pa rgyal ba yi// byang chub spyod pa'i smon lam bye brag rnams// bzang po spyod pas
270a8: byang chub sangs rgyas nas/ / de kun ma lus bdag gis rdzogs par bgyi// rgyal ba kun gyi sras kyi thu bo pa// gang gi ming ni kun tu bzang zhes bya// mkhas pa de dang mtshungs par spyad pa'i phyir/

270b1: dge ba 'di dag thams cad rab tu bsngo// lus dang ngag dang yid kyang rnam dag cing // spyod pa rnam dag zhing rnams yongs dag dang // bsngo ba bzang po mkhas pa ci 'dra bar// de 'drar bdag kyang de dang mtshung
270b2: par shog/ kun nas dge ba bzang po spyad pa'i phyir// 'jam dpal gyi ni smon lam spyad par bgyi// ma 'ongs bskal pa kun tu mi skyo bar// de yi bya ba ma lus rdzogs par bgyi// spyod pa dag ni tshang
270b3: yong ma gyur cig/ yon tan rnams kyang tshad gzud med par shog/ stod pa tshad med pa la gnas nas kyang // de dag 'phrul pa thams cad 'tshal bar bgyi// nam mkha'i mthar thug gyur pa rdzi
270b4: rnam par/ / sems can ma lus mtha' yang de bzhin te// ji tsam las dang nyon mongs mtha' gyur pa// bdag gi smon lam mtha' yang de tsam mo// gang yang phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams mtha' yas
270b5: ba/ rin char brgyan te rgyal ba rnams la bul// lha dang ma yi bad ba mchog rnams kyang // zhing gardul snyed bskal par bral babs// gang gis bsngo ba'i rgyal po 'ang thos nas// byang chub mchog gi rjes
270b6: su rab mos shing / / lan cig tsam yang dang pa skyed pas ni// bsod nams dam pa'i mchog tu 'di 'gyur ro// gang gis bzang skyod smon lam 'di btab pa// des na ngan song thams cad spangs par 'gyur//
270b7: ngas ni grogs po ngan pa spangs pa yin// snang ba mtha' yas de yang des myur mthong // de dag rnyed pa rab rnyed bde bar 'tsho// mo tshe 'dir yang de dag legs par 'ongs// kun tu bzang po de yang ci 'dang/
270b8: nga dag ring por mi thogs de bzhin 'gyur// 'tshams med lnga po dag gi sdig pa rnams// gang gis mi shes dbang gis byas pa dag/ de yis bzang po spyod pa 'di brjod na// mAr du ma lus yongs su byang ba

271a1: 'gyur/ / ya shas dang na gzugs dang mtshan rnams dang // rags dang kha dog rnams dang ldan par 'gyur// bdud dang mu stegs mang pos de mi thub// 'jig rten gsum po kun na'ang mchod par
271a2: 'gyur/ / byang chub shing dbang drung du de myur 'gro// song nas sems can phan phyir der 'dug ste// byang chub sangs rgyas 'khor lo rab tu bskor// bdud rnams sde dang bcas pa thams cad 'dul// gang yang
271a3: bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam 'di/ / 'chang ba dang ni ston tam klog pa yi// de yi rnam par smin pa sangs rgyas mkhyen// byang chub mchog la som nyi ma byed cig/ 'jam dpal ji ltar mkhyen cing dpa'
271a4: bo dang / / kun du bzang po de yang de bzhin te// de dag gi ni rjes su bdag slob cing // dge ba 'di dag thams cad rab tu ba sngo// dus gsum gshegs pa rgyal ba thams cad kyis// bsngo ba gang la mchog tu
271a5: bsngags pa des/ / bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'di kun kyang // bzang po spyod phyir rab tu bsngo bar bgyi// bdag ni 'chi ba'i dus byed gyur pa na// sgrib pa thams cad dag ni phyir bsal te// mngon sum snang ba
271a6: mtha' yas de mthong nas/ / bde ba can gyi zhing der rab tu 'gro// der seng na ma ni smon lam 'di dag kyang // thams cad ma lus mngon sum 'gyur bar shog/ de dag ma lus bdag gis yongs su bskad//
271a7: 'jig rten ji srid sems can phan par bgyi// rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor bzang zhing dga' ba der// pad ma dam pa shin tu mdzes las skyes// snang ba mtha' yas rgyal las mngon sum du// lung bstan pa
271a8: yang bdag gis der thob shog/ der ni bdag gis lung bstan rab thob nas// sprul pa mang po bye ba phrag brgya yis// blo yi stobs kyis phyogs bcu rnams su yang // sems can rnams la ban pa mang

271b1: po bgyi/ / bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam btab pa yis// dge ba cung zad bdag gis ci bsags pa// des ni 'gro ba'i dge ba'i smon lam rnams// skad cig gcig gis thams cad 'byor par shog/
271b2: bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam bsngos pa yis// bsod nams dam pa mtha' yas gang thob des// 'gro ba sdug bsngal chu bo dbying ba rnams// 'od dpag med pa'i gnas rab thob par shog/ smon lam rgyal
271b3: po 'di mchog gtso des na/ / 'gro ba mtha' yas kun la phan byed cing // kun tu bzang pos brgyan pa'i gzhung grub cing // ngan song rgyung gsum ma lus stongs par shog/ 'phags pa bzang po spyod pa'i//
271b4: smon lam gyi rgyal po/ rdzogs s+ho// / 'phags pa byams pa'i smon lam/ sangs rgyas kun la phyag 'tshal lo// drang srong lha mig ldan pa yi// byang chub sems dpa'
271b5: rnams dang yang / / nyan thos rnams la phyag 'tshal lo// ngan 'gro thams cad zlog bgyid cing // mtho ris lam ni rab ston la// rga shi med par 'dren pagyid pa// byang chub sems la phyag 'tshal lo//
271b6: sems kyi dbang du gyur pas na// bdag gis sdig pacibagyis pa// sangs rgyas spyan mngar mchis nas su// bdag gis de dag bshags par bgyi// bdag las rnam pa gsum gang gis// bsod nams
271b7: tshegs ni bsgreng bde/ / bdag gi kun mkhyen sa bon te// bdag gi byang chub mi zang shog/ phyogs bcu dag gi zhing rnams su// sangs rgyas mchod pa gang byung ba// sangs rgyas mkhyen pa'i yi rang bas// de la bdag
271b8: ni yi rang de/ / sdig pa thams cad bshags par bgyi// bsod nams kun la yi rang ngo // sangs rgyas kun la phyag 'tshal lo// bdag ni ye shes mchog thob shog/ phyogs bcu dag gi phyogs rnams na/

272a1: sa bcu dag la gnas pa yi// byang chub sems dpa' byang chub mchog/ 'chang rgya bgyid par skul ma 'debs// byang chub dam par sangs rgyas shing // sde dang bcas pa'i bdud btul nas//
272a2: srog chags kun la sman slad du// chos kyi 'khor lo bskor gyur cig/ chos rnga chen po'i sgra yis ni// sdug bsngal sems can thar bgyid shog/ bskal pa bye ba bsam yas su// chos ston mdzad cing btsun
272a3: gyur cig/ 'dod pa'i 'dam du byed gyur cing // sred pa'i srad bus dam bcings pa// 'ching ba kun gyis bcings bdag la// rkang gnyis mchog rnams gzigs su gsol// sems kyi dri mar bgyis pa la//
272a4: sangs rgyas rnams ni smod mi mdzad// sems can rnams la byams thugs ldan// srid pa'i mtsho las sgrol bar shog/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gang bzhugs dang // gang dag 'das dang mabyon pa// de dag rje
272a5: su bdag slob cing / / byang chub spyad pa spyod gyur cig/ pha rol phyin drug rdzogs bgyis nas// 'gro drug sems can thar bgyid shog/ mngon shes drug po mngon bgyis nas// bla med byang chub reg gyur cig
272a6: ma skyes pa dang mi 'byung dang / / rang bzhin ma mchis gnas ma mchis// rnam rig ma mchis dngos ma mchis// stong pa'i chos ni rtogs par shog/ sangs rgyas drang srong chen po ltar// sems can ma mchi
272a7: srog ma mchis/ / gang zag ma mchis gsom mchis// bdag ma mchis pa'i chos rtogs shog/ bdag 'dzin bdag gir 'dzin par ni// dngos po kun la mi gnas par// sems can kun la bde slad du// ser
272a8: sna ma mchis sbyin gtod shog/ dngos po dngos po ma mchis pas// bdag gi longs spyod lhun grub shog/ dngos po thams cad rnam 'jig pas// sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin rdzogs shog/ khrims kyi tshul khrim

272b1: skyon med cing / / tshul khrims rnam par dag dang ldan// rlom sems med pa'i tshul khrims kyis// tshul khrims pha rol phyin rdzogs shog/ sa 'am yang na chu 'am me// rlung gi khams ltar mi gnas shing // bzod pa
272b2: 'o ma khro ba ma mchis par/ / bzod pa'i pha rol phyin rdzogs shog/ brtson 'grus brtsams pa'i brtson 'grus kyis// brtan sgro le lo ma mchis shing // stobs dang ldan pa'i lus sems kyis// brtson 'grus pha rol
272b3: byin rdzogs shog/ sgyu ma lta bu'i ting 'dzin dang // dpa' bar 'gro ba'i ting 'dzin dang // rdo rje lta bu'i ting 'dzin gyis// bsam gtan pha rol phyin rdzogs shog/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum dang // dus gsum
272b4: mnyam pa nyid dang yang / / reg gsum mngon sum bgyis pa yis// shes rab pha rol phyin rdzogs shog/ sangs rgyas kun gyis bsngags pa dang // 'od dang gzi brjid 'bar ba dang // byang chub sems dpa'i brtson
272b5: 'grus kyis/ / bdag gi bsam pa rdzogs gyur cig/ de ltar spyad pa spyod byed cing // byams pa grags dang ldan pa yi// pha rol phyin drug rdzogs byas nas// sa bcu po la rab tu gnas// 'phags pa byams pa'i
272b6: smon lam rdzogs so/ / / rgya gar skad du/ a gra tsAr+ya pra Ni d+ha no/ bad ska du/ mchog gi spyod pa'i smon lam/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// ste dgu kun la ldan
272b7: bde skad du/ / phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten sangs rgyas rnams la 'dud// de dag la ni brjed cing mchod par bgyi// 'gro kun byang chub mchog la rig gyur cig/ byams pa dang ni 'jam dpal mnga' bdag rtog/ tshes
272b8: blo gros dpa' bo bdud rtsi gsung / / dpa' bod dag phyag 'tshal ma khyen pa ltar// de bzhin bdag kyang mi dbang rnams la 'dud// thugs rje ldan ne rje rten don mdzad pa'i// rgyal ba mi mkhyen me gzigs pa

273a1: mnga' ba/ / mi dbang thugs brtse byams la gnas pa yi// rgyal ba de kun bdag la dgongs su gsol// sngon gyi srid pa dag tu bdag nyid kyis// sdig pa'i las rnams gang bgyis bdag gis bshags//
273a2: de bzhin lus ngag yid kyis bgyis pa rnams// de dag thams cad bdag gis so sor bshags// shAkya thub dang mi 'khrugs 'od dpag med// de dag gis ni phrin las yongs sbyangs dang // 'chags dang bshags pa
273a3: mkhyen cing rtogs gyur ltar/ / de bzhin bdag gis sdig pa bshags par bgyi// thams cad dga' mdzad skyes bu dam pa gang // byang chub zhugs pa kun la gsol ba dang // ngan song bzhi po myur du zhi gyur cig/
273a4: mi khom 'joms par bgyid cing rgyu bar shog/ sangs rgyas bzang spyod de med mnga' bdag dang // de bzhin lhun po'i dpal dang nyi ma'i sgron// de dag bsod nams yi rang mkhyen pa ltar// de bzhin bdag kyang bsod
273a5: nams rjes yi rang / / phyogs bcu dag na sbyin pa spyod pa gang // de bzhin tshul khrims ting 'dzin spyod rnams dang // shes rab sgom dang bsod nams stobs kun la// byang chub yon tan don du yi rang ngo // rgyal ba kun
273a6: gyi yon tan mtha' yas dang / / chos bstan byang chub 'jog bgyid thams cad la// byang chub yon tan don du yid rang ngo // 'gro kun byang chub mchog la reg gyur cig/ 'jig rten rgyal ba gang bzhugs kun la
273a7: bskul/ / phyogs bcu dag na byang chub brnyes pa gang // de dag tshangs pas ji ltar gsol pa ltar// rgyal rnams bzhugs shing chos mchog ston gyur cig/ rgyal kun bskal pa mang por bzhugs par shog/ 'gro
273a8: kun byang chub mchog la reg gyur cig/ mi rnams thams cad mchog dang bla med pa// 'jig rten sgron ma bde gshegs myur gyur cig/ sangs rgyas rnams la phyag 'tshal mchod gang dang // las dge rnams

273b1: la yi rang gang lags dang / / sdig pa'i las rnams bshags pa gang lags dang // rgyal ba rkang gnyis dbang rnams mthong gang dag/ bdag gis dge ba cung zad ce bgyis pa// lus dang ngag dang sems las byung yang
273b2: rung / / bdag gis bgyis dang bgyid dang bgyid 'gyur gang // thams cad skye dgu sman slad stsal bar bgyi// ji ltar phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas rnams mkhyen nas// srul pa legs par sprul cing legs rgyas pa// de bzhin
273b3: bdagags ste dgu sman slad stsal/ / 'gro kun byang chub mchog la reg gyur cig/ bdag gis 'grol stsal ba gang lags pa'i// bsod nams 'bras bu bla med ci mchis pa// theg pa chen por yongs su bsngo bar bgyi//
273b4: bdag la byang chub 'bras bu grub par shog/ mtshungs pa ma mchis kun nas sgo mo rnams// 'gro ba'i don du bdag la mngon sum shog/ 'jam dpal gyi ni rjes su slob bgyid cing // byang chub spyod pa'i smon lam
273b5: gdab par bgyi/ / mi gcig tsam gyi ched du'ang mnar med pa'i// tshor ba thams cad bdag gis myong 'gyur bar// bskal pa du mar bdag ni spro bar bgyi// 'gro ba thams cad mya ngan med par shog/ sems
273b6: dmyal gshin rje'i 'jig rten sdug bsngal dang / / dud 'gro rnams dang mi yi sdug bsngal dang // 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal phung po mtha' yas dag/ bdag la bab gyur 'gro ba bde bar shog/ rgyal ba rnams kyi zhing ni rnam

279b2: rgyal pos phyag byas pa yi bkra shis gang/ / bkra shis des ni skye dgu rnams la zhi byed shog/ shing rgyal drung gshegs byams pa'i stobs kyis bdud kyi phyogs// mang po btul te sa steng dang ni nam mkha' la// bcom ldan
279b3: bkra shis rnam pa sna tshogs gang byung ba/ / bkra shis des ni skye dgu rnams la zhi byed shog/ sdug bsngal mtha' dag gzhig phyir rdo rje'i gdan bzhugs te// nam gyi tho rangs bdud bzhi po dag rnam btul ba// ston pa bde bar gshegs
279b4: ba'i bkra shis gang yin pa/ / bkra shis des ni ske dgu rnams la zhi byed shog/ grong khyer bA rA Na sIn drang srong mchog bzhugs nas// chos kyi 'khor lo mchog bstan pa yi bkra shis gang // lha yul dang 'dir shin tu rmad du thung sa
279b5: pa bkra shis des ni skye dgu rnams la ni byed sheg/ bkra shis gang zhig par byed dam pa dag byed pa// bsod nams bya byed 'phags pa'i skye bos mngon bstod pa// bcom ldan shA/ kya thub pa'i seng ges gang gsungs pa// kwa
279b6: des ni sde dgu rnams la ni phreng shog/ mu stegs byed pa kun gyi nga rgyal gzhom pa dang // 'gro la bde ba bskyed phyir cho 'phrul dam pa dag/ nyo bar ston pa rgyal ba'i bkra shis gang yin pa// bkra shis des ni skye dgu rnams la'i rje
279b7: gog 'grol ban phyir phrer sanas ni 'dir gshegs te/ / tshangs pa la sogs lha tshogs lagan rnga yib gdugs// sna tshogs thogs pas yongs bskor ba'i kra shis gang / 'akra shis des ni skye dkri rnams la'i byed do// /
279b8: de bzhin gshegs pa zhi ba mchog tu nyer gshegs pa// man dA ra ba'i me tog mang pos mngon mchod pa// lha mchog rnams kyis mngon par bstod pa'i bkra shis gang // bkra shis des ni skye dgu rnams la zhi bye shog/ lha dbang

280a1: klu dang mi yi dbang pos phyag byas pa/ / mkha' lding gnod sbyin dri za'i dbang pos mchod gyur pa// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu ldan pa'i bkra shis gang // bkra shis des ni skye dgu rnams la zhi byed
280a2: shog/ dkon mchog gsum dang mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi bkra shis kyi tshig su bcad pa rdzogs s+ho// / rgya gar gyi mkhan po 'dzin mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo ts+tsha ba ban d+he ye shes sdes bsgyur cang zhus te gtan la
280a3: phab bo/ / rgya gar skad du/ bud d+ha ka ma la sa b+h+ra maM ga la gA thA/ bod skad du/ sangs rgyas rabs bdun gyi bkra shis tshigs su bcad pa/ dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan rnam par gzigs ni rgyal
280a4: rigs gzi brjid can/ / tshe lo brgyad khri'i dus na grong khyer mdzes ldan du// shi ri sha yi shing drung mngon par sangs rgyas pa// deng 'dir bde gshegs bkra shis phun sum tshogs gyur cig/ bde gshegs gtsug tor mnga'
280a5: pa rgyal rigs rdzu 'phrul can/ / tshe lo bdun khri'i dus na su ka'i grong khyer du// shing mchog sun d+ha'i shing drung mngon par sangs rgyas pa// dang 'drir bde gshegs bkra shis phun sum tshogs gyur cig/ rgyal ba thams cad kyi
280a6: ba rgyal rigs blo gros can/ / tshe lo drug khri'i dus na grong khyer mnyam med du// shing mchogs la'i drung du mngon par sangs rgyas po// ding 'dir bde gshegs bkra shis sun sum tshogs gyur cig/ thub pa 'khor ba 'jig na
280a7: bcom ldan bram ze'i rigs/ / tshe lo bzhi khri'i dus na gro dbyer mdzes ldan du// shi ri sha yi shing drung mngon par sangs rgyas pa// ding 'dir bde gshegs bkra shis phun sum tshogs gyur cig/ 'dren pa gser thub bslab
280a8: mchog ldan bram ze'i rigs/ / tshe lo sum khri'i dus na grong khyer bde ldan du/ u dum ba ra'i shing drung mngon par sangs rgyas pa// ding 'dir bde gshegs bkra shis phun sum tshogs gyur cig/ skyob pa 'od srung rgyal

280b1: rigs bla med yon tan can/ / tshe lo nyi khri'i dus na bA rA Na sI ru// n+ya gro d+ha yi shing drung mngon pA sangs rgyas pa// ding 'dir bde gshegs bkra shis mun sum tshogs gyur cig/ 'gro mgon shAkya thub pa rgyal rigs
280b2: brtson 'grus can/ / tshe lo brgya pa'i dus na ser skya'i grong khyer du// a shwa tha yi shing drung mngon par sangs rgyas pa// ding 'dir bde gshegs bkra shis phun sum tshogs gyur cig/ sangs rgyas rabs bdun bkra shis
280b3: phun sum tshogs pa gang / / phyogs dus kun gyi bde gshegs byin brlabs rmad byung ba// chos dbyings rnam dag rten 'brel stobs ldan mi 'gyur ba// ding 'dir bde gshegs bkra shis phun sum tshogs gyur cig/ sangs rgyas
280b4: rabs bdun gyi bkra shis tshigs su bcad pa/ / rdzogs s+ho// @#// rgya gar skad du/ pany+tsa ta thA ga ta maM ga la gA thA/ bod skad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa lnga'i bkra shis tshig su bcad pa/ dkon mchog
280b5: gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ / rnam par snang mdzad ye shes dam pa mtsho chen ldan// zla ba nya 'dra'i sku mnga' srid pa'i mthar phyin pa// dgongs pa mtha' dag rdzogs pa'i bkra shis gang yin pa// bkra shis des ni skye dgu rnams
280b6: la'i byed shog/ mi 'khrugs rgyal po srid dang gti mug rnam sbyor ba// mgon po yon tan thams cad rdzogs pas bkra shis pa// dge mnyam bsam sems ldan pa'i bkra shis gang yin pa// bkra shis des ni skye dgu rnams
280b7: la'i byed shog/ sangs rgyas yon tan kun gyi rgyan gyis brgyan mdzad cing // yang dag bden pa'i 'byor pa sbyin mdzad mi sgrub// rin chen 'byung ldan zhes bya'i bkra shis gang yin pa// bkra shis des ni skyo dgu rnams
280b8: la zhi byed shog/ bsam gtan ting 'dzin me shes dam pa pha rol phyin pa'i gnas// ye shes pad ma'i steng bzhugs dpag med tshe ldan zhing // tshe grangs med par byin gyis rlob pa'i bkra shis gang yin pa// bkra shos des ni

281a1: dgu rnams la'i byed shog/ sems can don gyi las la thugs ni sbyar mdzad cing // 'gro ba kun gyi 'ching bas bcings las grol mdzad pa// thub mchog ngan yod grub pa'i bkra shas gang yin pa// nga
281a2: shis des ni skye dgu rnams la zhi byed shog/ de bzhin gshegs pa lnga'i bkra shis chags su bcad pa/ rdzogs s+ho// / rgyag skad du/ tra~M ku la ma ga la/ bod skad du/ rigs gsum gyi bkra shis/
281a3: dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan gser mdog ri yi rgyal po 'dra// 'jig rten gsum mgon 'jam dpal gzhon nu'i sku// bde gshegs sku yi bkra shis gang yin pa// bkra shis des ni dring
281a4: 'dir bde legs shog/ bcom ldan dung mdog ri yi rgyal po 'dra// 'jig rten gsum mgon spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang // bde gshegs gsung gi bkra shis gang yin pa// bkra shis des ni ding 'dir bde legs shog
281a5: bcom ldan ldang ser ri yi rgyal po 'dra/ / 'jig rten gsum mgon phyag na rdo rje ste// bde gshegs thugs kyi bkra shis gang yin pa// bkra shis des ni ding 'dir bde legs shog/ dpal rigs gsum gyi bkra shis / rngogs//
281a6: shis par brjod pa'i tshig su bcad pa/ dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshalo// lha yi bkra shis don sgrub cing // phyogs rnams bkra shis byed pa des// khyed kyi don rnams grub gyur cig/ thams cad myur du mthun par shog/
281a7: phreng ba mgo la 'dug pa ltar// lag pa g.yas na dpal yod shog/ g.yon na'ang dpal ni gnas gyur cig/ yan lag kun na'ang dpal yod shog/ tshong pa dag ni nor tshol zhing // phyogs bcu dag tu 'gro ba rnams// rnyed
281a8: chen po rnyed gyur cing / / de dag bde ba skyid par shog/ dgos pa la la gang gi phyir// shar phyogasu ni 'gro ba na// gang dag phyogs der gnas pa yi// rgyu skar khyed la skyong gyur cig/ smin drug dang ni sngar ma dang // mgo dang lag dang

281b1: nam so dang / / rgyal dang skrag ces bya ba ste// de dag rnams ni shar phyogs pa// chu skar bdun po de dag ni// 'jig rten skyong ba grags ldan pa// shar phyogs logs na yod ces bstan// de dag khyed la kun du srungs// de dag bdag po rgyal po
281b2: ni/ yul 'khor srung shes grags pa ste// de ni dri za kun gyi bdag/ nyi ma lhan cig srung bar shog/ de la bu ni mang yod la// mkhas shing ming yang mthun pa ste// dgu bcu rtsa gcig zad par yang // dbang po zhes bya stobs po
281b3: che/ de rnams khyer la nad med cing // shes par lhag par skyong gyur cig/ shar phyogs logs kyi phyogs can// lha mo gzhon nu brgyad yod de// rgyal dang rnam par rgyal ma dang // don grub ma dang mi pha ma dang // dga' mchog
281b4: ma dang dga' sde dang / / dga' can ma dang dga' 'phel ma// de dag khyed la nad med cing // shis par lhag par skyong bar shog/ shar phyogs logs kyi phyogs chan// gzhi 'dzin ces bya'i mchod rten yod// rgyal ba skyob pa dgra bcom
281b5: de rnams kyis ni bzhugs shing mkhyen/ / de yang khyed la nad med cing // shis par lhag par skyong gyur cig/ phyogs na khyed cag bde bar shog/ khyed cag sdig par ma gyur cig/ lha rnams kun gyis rab bsrungs nas/
281b6: nor rnams rnyed de ldog par shog/ dgos pa la la gang gi phyir// lho phyogs su ni 'gro ba na// gang dag phyogs der gnas pa yi// rgyu skar khyed la skyong gyur cig/ mchu dang the dang dpo dang ni// mi bzhi nag pa lnga pa yin// sa ri dang ni sag
281b7: steng dag rnams ni lho phyogs pa/ / rgyusar bdun po de dag ni/ 'jig rten sbyang bgrags ldan pa// sgro phyogs logs na yod ces bstan// de dag khyod la kun ta sungs// de dag ba dag po rgyal po ni// 'phags skyes po zhes bya bar brjod/ den
281b8: grul bu pa kun gyi bdag/ gshin rje lhan cig srung bar shog/ de la bu ni mang yod la// mkhas shing ming yang mthun pa ste// dgu bcu rtsa dab cig phrad pa ra yang // dbang po zhes bya stobs po che// de rnams khyed la nad med cing // shis par lhag

282a1: par skyong gyur cig/ lho phyogs ngogs kyi phyogs ma/ lha mo gzhon nu brgyad yod de// dpal ldan ma dang grags ldan pa// grags pa thob dang grags 'dzin dang // legs par langs dang rab snga dang // legs par sa

282b7: phyogs bzhi dag na bdun bdun gnas// lha yi bu mo sum bcu gnyis// phyogs bzhi dgan brgyad brgyad gnas// dge sbyong brgyad dang bram ze brgyad// yul rnams na ni grong rdal brgyad// dbang por bcas pa'i lha brgyad

283a1: dang / dgra bcom padag nyid brtse bas// thams cad duni bkra shis dang / bdud rtsigs pa thob par shog/ tshangs pa ning bzhinan tus dang // zag pa med pa rnam par grol rnams dang / klu dang gnod sbyin rtag tu snying rjes spangs/
283a2: ston pa rgya mtshungs par tshe ni skyong bar shog/ 'phags pa rgya cher rol pa'i mdo'i tshang dpon gagon dang bzang po'i le'u las 'byung ba shes par brjod pa'i tshigs su bcad pa/ rdzogs s+ho//

283a4: byin brlabs kyis/ / bdud dang bgegs rigs gnad pa'i dgra zhi ste// rtag tu dpal gnas nyin mtshan bkra shis shog/ chos nyid bden pa'i chos mchog than med// dam chos bdud rtsi bden pa'i byan brlabs kyis/

283a6: bsngal gdung ba'i dgra zhi ste/ / rtag tu dpal gnas nyin mtshan bkra shis shog/ tshangs dang lha dbang srungs ma'i byin brlabs kyis// phan mdzad lha yi bkra shis gnas gyur te// bde legs bsam pa yid bzhin
283a7: 'grub pa dang / / ma ri nang mang bde zhing ldan par shog/ dkon mchog gsum gyi ba shis kyi tshigs su bcad pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis khyim bdag nges pa la gsungs pa/ rtags so//
283a8: rgyag kyi 'a po 'dzi ni tra dang / 'ur gyi'i ban d+he me shes sdes bsnur cing nus te gtanas pab ba'o// dge'o// rdo khrig pa'i churtings la brten nas/ dpag yas srid pa'i tsholas legs sgrob te/ zung drug yid bzhin nor bu'i dga' ston gyis/ 'gro kun yid kyi rebaskor bar shog/
